et se li apostemes est de soef touchement, non mie de fuxe color, et tu vois c’on le puisse tout coper, si vuide le malaide et lou cope sens paor, et cure le leu de choses sechans et restraignans.	and if the abscess is soft to the touch, not of a reddish color, and you see that it can be completely cut out, then empty the patient of blood without fear, and treat the area with dry and binding substances.
quant li neis est copez et cosus	When the nose is broken and sewn up
Saiches que quant solutions de continuation vient en une de ces cartillagines ovraiges, i profite poc, fuer que en aucuns homes.	Know that when a solution for continuity comes to one of these cartilage works, it is little use, except in some men.
Il covient donques cant ceu avient a aucun, si regarde se li plaie est fresche a tout son sanc;	It is therefore necessary, when this happens to anyone, to examine whether the wound is fresh with all its blood;
et adonques ajoste les II levres a une costure, puis le cure tant qu’il soit sanez;	and then sew the two edges together, and treat it until it is healed;
et se les levres sont ja desevrees d’une part et d’autre, si covient que tu escorches toutes les parties de lor keur tant qu’elles sainent, puis assemble les II levres a une costure, et l’estraint, et poudre sus poudre de sanc de dragon, et encens broiet;	and if the edges are separated on both sides, you must cauterize all parts of their flesh until they bleed, then bring together the two edges with stitches, and press it tightly, and sprinkle powdered dragon's blood, and grind incense;
et met sus les poudres une piece d’emplaustre de fort ou d’autre emplaustre soudant, et le laisse tant qu’il chiece par lui, puis le cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez.	and apply a piece of hot or another adhesive plaster over the powders, and leave it until it sticks by itself, then treat it with ointment until it is healed.
Li maniere de la costure si est que tu assembles la solution:	The method of suturing is such that you bring together the edges:
ou par aguilles, si com nos avons dit en la costure dou ventre;	using needles, as we have said in the suturing of the abdomen;
ou par fil, si com je le t’ai fait savoir.	or using thread, as I have told you.
des apostemes des levres	of abscesses of the lips
A mains homes avient dedens les levres aposteme dur, semblans a grains de veces, et menor et plus grant;	In some people, there occurs in the lips an hard abscess, resembling grains of vesicles, smaller and larger;
adonques couvient que tu tornes les levres, et fendes sus chescun nout, et le prent as pinceures et le cope en chescune partie;	then you must turn the lips inside out, and cut into each knot, and grasp it with forceps and excise in each part;
puis emple lou leu aprés l’incision de vitriole broiet, tant que li sans soit estainchiez;	then apply the area after incising with broiled vitriol, until the blood is coagulated;
et puis lou leive d’aisil, et cure lou leu de choses seches tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then lift the cushion, and treat the area with dry substances until it is healed.
de la char des gencives	of the flesh of the gums
Maintes fois naist sus les gencives char ajostee, que li ancien apelent «albulus»;	Many times, flesh grows on the gums, which the ancients call "albulus";
si covient que tu la sostienes as tenailles, et la cope a sa racine, et laisse corre la bowe ou le sanc;	you must hold it with forceps, cut it at its root, and let the blood or pus flow;
puis met sor le leu vitriole broiet, ou autres poudres restraignans et desiccatives;	then apply powdered vitriol or other astringent and drying powders to the area;
et se celle char revient aprés l’incision, et maintes fois avient, si la cope la seconde fois, et la cauterize:	and if the flesh returns after cutting, which often happens, cut it again and cauterize it:
si ne revient mie aprés le cautere;	it will not return after the cauterization;
et ce sont les formes des estrumens por coper.	and these are the forms of the instruments for cutting.
des sordens	of dirtiness
Aucunes fois sont assemblees au chief des dens, dedens la bouche entre les gencives, escorces qui sont laides et aspres;	Sometimes they are assembled at the top of the teeth, inside the mouth between the gums, rough and unpleasant scales;
et aucune fois sont li dent noir et citrin et vers, tant que li corruption vient a la gencive, et sont li dent puant;	and sometimes the tooth is black and yellow and worm-eaten, until the corruption reaches the gum, and the tooth becomes foul-smelling;
si covient que tu faices seoir lou malaide entre tes mains, et ses chiés soit en ton saint, et reis les dens ou les escorces aperent, tant qu’il n’i demore rien;	it is necessary that you seat the patient between your hands, and place his head in your lap, and remove the teeth or the scales that appear, until nothing remains;
et ensi fai de la noiror et de la verdor, et de la jaunice et des autres taiches, tant qu’elles soient mondees;	and thus do for the blackness and the greenness, and the yellow and other stains, until they are clean;
et s’on oste ceu que i est a la premiere rasion, c’est boin;	and if what is there at the first reason is removed, it is good;
se ceu non, si rencomence a rere le secont jor et lou tier, tant que tu aies tout reis;	if not, then start again from the second day and the third, until you have completely reset it;
et saiches que li dent ont mestier de diverses formes d’estrumens por reire, selonc ceu que li oevre lou demoustre, por ceu que li raseur dont on reit defuer les dens ont autres formes que cil dont on reit entre les dens;	and know that the teeth require various forms of instruments to reset them, according to what the work shows, because the instrument used to remove teeth has a different shape than those used between the teeth;
et cestes formes et autres soient avec toi appareillies.	and these forms and others should be prepared for you.
Il covient quant tu cures lou dent de sa dolor que tu tardes dou traire tant com tu pues, car ce ne doit om mie faire;	It is necessary when you treat the tooth for its pain that you delay pulling it as much as you can, for one must not do this readily;
car c’est une substance mout haute jusc’a donc c’on n’ait point d’excusation dou raier.	For it is a very high substance until one has no excuse for scraping.
Adonques quant li malaides est constrains dou traire, si covient que tu soies certains dou dent doillant.	Then when the patient is forced to pull the tooth, it is necessary that you be certain of the tooth causing pain.
Maintes fois desoit li dolor lou malaide, et cuide qu’elle soit ou dent saint, et fait traire le boin dent;	Many times the pain deceives the patient, and they believe it to be from a tooth, and they pull the good tooth;
et toutevoie ne se depart mie li dolor per ceu, tant que li malvais estrais, car nos l’avons ja veut faire a ces sainors;	and the pain never leaves because of that tooth, until the bad one is extracted, for we have already seen this happen with these patients;
et quant tu es bien certains dou dent doillant, si covient que tu escorches entor lou dent a tout i. spatumile fort por warder la gencive de toutes pars;	and when you are certain of the painful tooth, then it is necessary to scrape around the tooth thoroughly. Use plenty of spatinum to protect the gum on all sides;
puis le mues a tes dois ou as tenailles subtilz au premier poc et poc, tant qu’il soit bien eslochiés, puis i afferme bien les tenailles;	then move it with your hands or with fine tweezers little by little until it is well loosened, then firmly secure the tweezers;
et soit li chiés dou malaide en ton saint entre tes genous, et lou tien bien si qu’il ne se mueve.	And let the head of the patient’s shoulder be between your knees, and hold it firmly so that it does not move.
Aprés estrai lou dent droitement sens brisier, et s’il ne saut fuer, si prent aucun de ces estrumens et le boute dedens de chescune part legierement, et lou remuef si com tu as fait premier.	After extract the tooth straight without breaking it, and if it does not come out easily, take one of these instruments and push into each side gently, and move it as you have done before.
Et se li dens est perciez et mengiez, si covient que tu l’emplisses de drapelz, lai ou li pertus sont;	And if the tooth is pierced and decayed, you must fill it with cloths where the hole is;
et si l’estraint subtilment as tenailles, que il ne brise a l’estraindre;	and if you grasp it gently with forceps so that it does not break when you pull;
et covient mout saigement ovrer entor la gencive por deschaucier lou dent.	and you must carefully work around the gum to loosen the tooth.
Et te done bien en warde que tu ne le brises, et en remaigne une partie, et reveigne au malaide par la malice de la racine plus grans dolors de la premiere.	And be very careful that you do not break it, and leave a part behind, and return to the patient because of the root's mischief greater pain than before.
Et te warde que tu ne faices mie ensi com font li ignorant sainor, qui par lor haste et par lor hardiesce brisent aucune fois le charreit, et n’i amenistrent mie ceu que nos avons conteit;	And be careful that you do not act as the ignorant surgeons do, who in their haste and boldness sometimes break the tissue, and fail to achieve what we have described;
mais font venir aucune fois par l’oquison de ceu grant maladie por les racines que i demorent, ou por lou charreit qu’il brisent, si com nos avons sovent veut;	but they sometimes bring about a great illness due to the roots that remain, or because of the flesh that they tear, as we have often seen;
et quant li dens est trais, si lavez lou leu de vin ou d’aisil et de seil;	and when the tooth is extracted, wash the area with wine or hellebore and salt;
et se decorremens de sanc i vient, que sovent avient, si emple lou leu de vitriole broiet;	and if bleeding occurs, which often happens, then apply ground vitriol to the area;
et se ceu ne vaut, si le cauterize.	and if that does not help, cauterize it.
Les formes des estrumens, a coi om muet les dens premier, soient a longes pointes et a gros mainches, qu’il ne doublent mie quant tu trairas le dent;	The shapes of the instruments used to extract teeth first should have long points and thick handles, so they do not bend when you pull the tooth;
et ce sont les formes:	and these are the forms:
Et soient de gros membres si qu’il ne ploient mie au traire, et soient de fer inde bien fait, et soient dentez por mues tenir.	And they should have thick parts so that they do not bend when extracting, and they should be made of well-crafted iron, and should have teeth to hold the teeth.
de la racine des dens	from the root of the teeth
Quant li racine demoure au traire, si covient que tu mettes sor le leu coton moilliet em burre I jor ou II, tant que li leus soit amolis, pues i boute les tenailles qui sont apelees «algefri», de coi li chiés semblet bec de soigne;	When the root remains in the hair, you should place cotton soaked in butter on it for one or two days until the area softens, then use pliers called "algefri," which makes the head appear like a bird's beak;
et soient dedens faites ausi com une lime et c’est li forme:	and they should be made inside like a file and this is the form:
Et se les racines ne vuellent issir a tout ces tenailles, si covient que tu descuevre la char tot entor la racine, et i met l’estrument qui est apelez «althali», c’est a savoir palainche, de coi ci est li forme:	And if the roots do not wish to come out completely with these clamps, then you must uncover the flesh all around the root, and place the instrument which is called "althali," that is to say a scalpel, here is its form:
Et soit fors et gros si qu’il ne brise mie, et se li racine saut par ceu, c’est boin;	And let it be outside and thick so that it does not break, and if the root jumps out through this, it is good;
se ceu non, si t’aide de toz les estrumens, de coi les formes vienent ci aprés:	if not, then help with all the instruments, of which the forms follow hereafter:
Et si s’aide on de cest estrument qui ait II rains, de coi ci est li forme:	And if one aids with this instrument that has two blades, of which here is its form:
et d’autres ferremens qui sont devant en la rasion des dens, et de cest estrument qui semble unes grans tenailles, dont ci est li forme:	and other iron tools which are mentioned earlier in the rationale of teeth, and of this instrument that resembles large clamps, here is its form:
Et soit cist estrumens fors qu’il ne puisse brisier, et saiches que mout d’estrumens de dens sont;	And let this instrument be such that it cannot break, and know that many instruments of bone are;
et ausi d’autres estrumens, qui ne sont mie contez;	and also other instruments, which are not counted;
et li saiges maistres subtilz trueve par soi meisme son estrument, selonc ceu que ses ovraiges et li maladie li demoustre, car il i a de teilz maladies ou li ancien n’enseignerent point d’estrument por la diversiteit d’au;s et s’om brise point dou charreit ou des autres os, ou il porrit, si i cerche as estrumens qu’il i covient, que je t’ai dit, et t’aide des gestes, de coi ci est li forme:	and the wise masters subtle find by himself his instrument, according to what his work and the illness shows him, for there are such illnesses where the ancients did not teach an instrument due to the diversity of them; and if one breaks a little of the cartilage or other bones, it may rot, so he seeks among the instruments that are needed, which I have told you about, and helps with gestures, of which here is the form:
Et soient gros et bien tenant por tenir l’os, qu’il n’eschaipe, mais le puisse tenir et oster;	And let them be large and well-made to hold the bone, so it does not slip, but can hold and remove it;
et puis restoure lou leu de medicines convenant a ceu, et s’il ait en l’os porriture, et elle est petite, si la reis a tout cest estrument:	and then restore the place with medicines suitable for that, and if there is decay in the bone, and it is small, remove it entirely with this instrument:
Quant li dent apperent ne mie selonc lou cors natureil, et li forme est laide, et meismement en femmes puceles, si covient que tu saiches se li dens est neis aprés lou dent, et n’est mie en droit leu, et on ne lou puet soier ne limer:	When a tooth appears not according to its natural form, and the shape is ugly, especially in virgin women, then you must know if the tooth has grown after another tooth and is not in the right place, and cannot be filed or smoothed:
adonques lou raie;	then remove it;
et s’il est aers avec lou dent, si prent cest estrument dont ci est li forme, et est semblans a I petit bec, et soit de fer inde agut en som:	and if it is embedded with the tooth, then take this instrument whose form is here shown, and it resembles a small beak, and should be made of sharp iron at its tip:
Et lou cope poc et poc em mains jors por la duresce dou dent, et por ceu que tu ne mueves les autres, et s’il est apparans c’on le puisse limer, si lou lime d’une teil lime com ci est li forme:	And cut it bit by bit over several days due to the hardness of the tooth, and so as not to move the other teeth, and if it appears that you can file it, then file it with a tool like this one shown here:
et est ausi com li lime de coi on fait les aguilles;	and it is also like the file used to make needles;
et en lime lou dent poc et poc em mains jors legierement, si qu’il ne se mueve tant qu’il chiece;	and file the tooth bit by bit over several easy days, so that it does not move until it falls out;
puis la plaine en la fin a tout aucun raseur, et se li dens est trop trenchans et il blece la lengue, si covient limer l’aspreteit tant qu’il soit igalz, si qu’il ne blece la lengue ne ne corrompe la parole.	then the surface should be smooth at the end for any grinder, and if the tooth is too sharp and cuts the tongue, it must be filed down until it is even, so that it does not cut the tongue nor impair speech.
quant li dent lochent	When the teeth grind together
Quant li dent devant lochent, ou par percussion ou par cheoir, et li malaides ne puet presser sus ceu qu’il menjue qu’il ne chient, et tu les as curez de medicines restrignans, et ceu ne vaut;	When the teeth in front are loose, either due to impact or falling, and the patient cannot bite down on what they eat without them moving, and you have treated them with constricting medications, but it is ineffective;
si les covient restraindre d’un fil d’or, car li filz d’argent devient vert et porrit, mais li ors ne se mue onques;	then they must be restrained with a gold wire, because silver thread turns green and rots, but gold never moves;
et soit li filz moiens ne trop gros ne trop menus, selonc la quantiteit de l’espaice entre les dens;	and let the thread neither be too thick nor too thin, according to the quantity of space between the teeth;
et se tu vues adrecier les dens, si pren lou fil et lou boute double entre les II dens sains, puis met les chiés entre les dens meus, s’il en i a I ou plusors, tant que tu veignes saigement jusc’au dent sain d’autre part;	and if you wish to align the teeth, take the thread and tie it double between two healthy teeth, then place the head of the needle between the bad teeth, whether there is one or more, carefully until you reach a healthy tooth on the other side;
puis rencomence la coverture jusc’a la partie ou tu encomensas, et estrains ta main subtilment et saigement, tant qu’il ne se mueve point;	then restart the wrapping until you reach the part where you began, and withdraw your hand subtly and carefully, so that it does not move;
et soit ta lieeure a la racine dou dent si qu’il ne puist eschaper.	and tie it at the root of the tooth so that it cannot escape.
Puis cope les chiés dou fil a unes tenailles, et les assemble, et les repont entre le dent sain, et le met ensi qu’il ne blece la lengue;	Then cut the thread with pliers and tie it together, placing it between the healthy tooth, so that it does not irritate the tongue;
et puis le laisse ensi estroit tant com il puet demorer, et s’il deslie, ou li filz ront, si l’estraint d’un autre fil;	and then leave it so tight as it can remain, and if it loosens, the thread slips, then tighten it with another thread;
si demorrait et servira ensi tout son tens, et c’est li forme des dens et li figure de l’adrecement des II dens sains, et des II meus, si com tu vois:	and it will remain and serve in this manner for its entire duration, and this is the form of the teeth and the arrangement of the two healthy teeth, and the two defective ones, as you see:
Et quant li dent chiet, si lou remet on en son leu, de fres en fres, si com nos avons dit;	And when the tooth falls out, replace it in its place, fresh for fresh, as we have said;
et ne s’en entremette mie qui n’est saiges et soffrans, et aucune fois fait on la forme d’un dent d’os de vaiche, et lou met on au leu ou li defaute est, et l’estraint on si com nos avons dit, et demore et sert ensi lonc tens.	and let no one else intervene who is not wise and skilled, and sometimes a tooth shape is made from the bone of a fish, and it is placed in the place where the defect is, and it is tightened as we have said, and it remains and serves for such a long time.
de coper lou liien de la lengue	To cut the ligament of the tongue
Aucune fois est cist liiens qui vient desoz la lengue ou naturez, que on naist ensi;	There is sometimes this condition which comes from below the tongue or naturally, one is born thus;
ou par accident de plaie soudee;	or by an accidental wound that has closed;
et li ovraiges est telz que tu oevre la bouche dou malaide, et ait sa teste en ton sain, et li lieve la lengue;	and the procedure is such that you work on the mouth of the patient, and have their head in your lap, and lift the tongue;
puis cope lou liien nervous dou large, tant que li lengue soit desloie de son tenement, et se il i a duresce ou nout, et c’est de soudement de plaie, si i boute l’uncine et cope dou large celui liement;	then cut the nervous ligament widely, until the tongue is free from its attachment, and if there is hardness or knot, which is due to the closing of a wound, insert the hook and cut that ligament;
et garde que li fendure ne soit mie trop em parfont, por l’artere qui est desoz;	and be careful that the incision is not too deep, for the artery which lies below;
et quant tu as fait, si leve le leu d’aigue rose et d’aisil, ou d’aigue froide, puis met desoz la lengue une tente de lin;	and when you have done this, lift the area with rose water and plantain, or with cold water, then place a pad of linen under the tongue;
et la teigne li malaides chescune nuit, que li leus ne puisse soder.	and let the patient scratch the area each night so that it does not seal over.
Et se decorremens de sanc vient, si met sor le leu vitriole broiet;	And if bleeding occurs, place powdered vitriol on the area;
et se li sans te vaint, si le cauterize au cautere lentiginout, qui est boin a ceu;	and if the skin becomes moist, cauterize it with a lentiginous cautery, which is good for this;
puis le cure d’autre cure tant qu’il soit sanez,	then treat it further until it is healed,
et se tu lou vois de fusse color ou noir ou dur, si que li malaides ne lou sent, si n’i touchier point, car c’est chancre;	and if you see it colored black or hard and the patient does not feel it, do not touch it, for it is a carbuncle;
et s’il est declinans a blenchor, et il i a moistor, si i giete l’oncine, et lou fent d’un spatumile subtil, et lou delivre d’une part et d’autre;	If it is inclined towards inflammation and there is moisture, then pour in the compound, and cut it with a fine scalpel, and release it from both sides.
et se li sans te vaint a ton ovraige, si met sus vitriole broiet tant qu’il soit estainchiez, puis revien a ton ovraige tant que tu traies tout fuer;	And if your strength fails during your work, then apply powdered vitriol until it is dissolved, then return to your work until you have exhausted all energy;
puis leve lou leu d’aisil et de seil, et le cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then lift the place with care and caution, and treat it with other treatments until it is healthy.
des apostemes de la gorge	abscesses of the throat
Aucune fois vient dedens la gorge boces qui sont apelees «godath», et les apele on proprement les II amandres, et quant tu les cures, si com nos avons dit en la division, et elles ne sont sanees, si pren garde:	Sometimes in the throat there are lumps called "godath," and they are properly referred to as the two tonsils, and when you treat them, as we have said in the division, and if they are not healed, be careful:
se c’est apostemes dur de petit sens et de fusse color, si ne lou touchier mie de fer.	If this abscess is hard with little sensation and of dark color, do not touch it with iron.
Et s’il est rouges et li racine est grosse, si ne lou touchier mie de fer, ausi por lou decorrement de sanc;	And if it is red and the root is large, do not touch it with iron, also for fear of bleeding;
mais lou laisse tant qu’il soit meur, et adonques tu lou partiras, ou il rompirait par soi;	but let it be until it becomes black, and then you will open it, as it would burst on its own;
et s’il est de blainche color reont, et li racine est subtilz, si aies apareilliet l’estrument por coper, mais regarde premierement se li apostemes chalz repose et est apaisiez.	and if it is of white color and the root is fine, then prepare the instrument to cut, but first look to see if the abscess lies still and is calm.
Adonques fai seoir lou malaide devant lou soleil, et ses chiés soit en ton sain, et li oevre la bouche et lou preigne li serjans entre ses mains, et presse la lengue desoz a tout l’estrument, de coi ci est li forme;	Then have the patient sit facing the sun, and place your hands under his feet, and work on his mouth and hold the servant's hands between yours, and press the tongue down with all the instrument, as follows this form;
et soit d’argent ou d’arain subtil ausi com uns coutelz:	and whether of silver or tin just like some knives:
Cant tu presses la lengue a tout cest estrument, et tu vois l’aposteme, si pren l’oncine et lou fiche en l’amandre, et la trai fuer au desus plus que tu pues;	When you press the tongue against all this instrument, and you see the abscess, take the lancet and insert it into the kernel, and draw it out forcefully above as much as you can;
et trai aucune chose des toiles avec, puis la cope a l’estrument, de coi ci est li forme, que semble unes forces;	and draw some thing from the cloths with it, then clean it with the instrument, which is shaped like a forceps;
et toutevoie li chief sont corbé, et l’un endroit l’autre, et sont molt agut, et est fait de fer inde ou d’andainne:	and all the heads are curved, and one side to the other, and they are very sharp, and it is made of Indian iron or tin;
Et se tu n’as cest estrument present, si lou cope as tenailles, de coi ci est li forme:	And if you do not have this instrument at hand, cut it with pliers, of which here is the form:
Et soit trenchans d’une part, et d’autre part nom;	And let it be cutting on one side, and on the other side named;
et quant tu as copeit l’une des amandres, si cope l’autre selonc cele meisme maniere, et aprés l’incision gargarize li malaides aigue chaude, et aigue et aisil, et se decorremens de sanc avient, si gargarize li malaides aigue, ou escorces de pomes grenates soient cuites, ou fuelles de mirte, et semblans choses, tant que li sans soit estainchiez;	And when you have cut one of the almonds, cut the other in the same manner, and after the incision, rinse the patient's mouth with hot water, and with warm and soothing water, and if bleeding occurs, rinse the patient's mouth with water, or use boiled pomegranate rinds, or myrtle leaves, and similar things, until the blood is stopped;
puis lou cure tant qu’il soit sanez;	then treat him until he is well;
et aucune fois naissent en la gorge autres apostemes que les II amandres, si les cope donques ensi com les II amandres igament.	and sometimes other abscesses arise in the throat besides the two almonds, so cut them as you would the two almonds equally.
Et je medicinai une femme d’un aposteme que li estoit neis dedens la gorge, c’est a savoir I aposteme de petit sens;	And I treated a woman for an abscess that had arisen in her throat, namely the abscess of the small sense;
et avoit jai bien pres close toute la gorge, si que li femme ne pooit expirer por le conduit qui estoit estoupez, et ne pooit ne mengier ne boivre, et fust morte s’elle demorast ensi I jor ou II.	And I had nearly completely closed the throat so that the woman could not exhale because the passage was blocked, and she could neither eat nor drink, and she would have died if she remained thus for one day or two.
Et li apostemes estoit jai si montez qu’il avoit fuer mis II rains par les II pertuis dou neis.	And the abscess had risen so high that it had forced two inches through each of the two openings of the anus.
Je hastai donques tantost, et fichai en l’un I oncine, puis lou traï fuers, et en traï grant porcion de bowe;	I then hurried and inserted one lancet, then drew it out, and drew out a great portion of phlegm;
puis refis autreteil en l’autre pertus dou neis, et li ovrai la bouche et li pressai la lengue;	then I repeated the procedure on the other nostril, and opened her mouth and pressed her tongue;
aprés fichai l’oncine en ces apostemes, et en copai une partie, et n’en issit fuers que un poc de sanc;	after inserting the lancet into the abscesses, I removed some of it, and only a little blood came out;
et ensi fut destoupez li conduis de la gorge la femme, et comensa maintenant a boivre aigue et puis vin, et ne cessai de taillier de cel aposteme par lonc tens;	and thus the passage in her throat was cleared, and she now began to drink water and then wine, and I continued to incise the abscess for a long time;
et li apostemes recroissoit adés, et remplissoit lou leu que je avoie vuidiet, tant qu’il refut mout gros;	and the abscess regrew quickly, filling the place that I had emptied, until it became very large;
adonques je l’engignai et lou cauterizai dedens la gorge:	then I guided it and cauterized it inside the throat:
ensi demora sens croistre;	thus it remained without growing;
et me partis de ces parties, et ne soi que Deus fist de li aprés moi.	and I left those areas, and do not know what God did with it after me.
de l’uve	of the eye
Quant reume dessent a l’uve, et elle est enflee et elle est longe, si est apelee «perpendiculaire»;	When phlegm descends to the uvula, and it is swollen and elongated, it is called "perpendicular";
et s’elle est desoz grosse et reonde, si est apelee «uve».	and when it is thick and round, it is called "uvula".
Quant elle est curee si com nos avons dit en la division, et li cure ne profite mie, et tu vois que li chaus apostemes est apaisiez, et elle est subtilz, si covient que tu la copes;	When it is treated as we have said in the division, and the treatment does no good, and you see that the gross abscesses are abated, and it is subtle, then it is necessary that you cut it open;
et celle qui est reonde assemblee et n’est mie longe;	and that which is round and assembled and is not long;
et elle est sanguine ou de fusse color ou noire, si covient que tu eschues l’incision de li.	and it is bloody or of dark red color or black, then it is necessary that you avoid making an incision in it.
Car il i a grant peril sus lou malaide.	For there is great danger to the patient.
Il covient donques, quant tu la vois, selonc la maniere que j’ai dit, de sa blenchor et de sa longesce, que tu faices seoir le malaide devant lou soleil, et li presse la lengue a l’estrument dont nos avons fait la remembrance ci devant;	Therefore, when you see it, according to the manner I have said, regarding its blueness and length, you should seat the patient before the sun, and press the tongue with the instrument of which we made mention previously;
puis fiche l’oncine en l’uve, et la trai desoz, et la cope a I des II estrumens que j’ai dit en l’incision des II amandres.	Then insert the lancet into the eye, and draw it out from below, and cut with one of the two instruments that I mentioned for cutting the two almonds.
Et covient que tu ne coper mie fuer que la superfluiteit qui est outre le termine natureil;	And you must not cut beyond the excess that is beyond the natural boundary;
car se tu en copes plus, si grieves a la voix, et a la parolle;	for if you cut more, it will harm the voice and speech;
et aprés l’incision, use de ceu que nos avons dit en l’incision des II amandres, et le cure tant qu’elle soit sanee.	and after the incision, use what we have said about cutting the two almonds, and treat it until it is healed.
Et se li malaides a paor dou coper, si covient que tu i use d’engien a la cauterization de li sens paor.	And if the patient fears the cutting, it is necessary that you use cunning in the cautery to calm his fearful senses.
Et li maniere dou cautere si est aigue ague.	And the method of the cautery is sharp heat.
Et est que li malaides mette son chief en ton sain, et puis li presse la lengue a l’estrument que nos avons dit ou chapistre de cautere, et confis avec aigue vive chaus, si qu’elle ne soit mie trop espesse ne trop clere;	And have the patient place their head on your lap, then press the tongue with the instrument that we mentioned in the chapter on cautery, and rinse it thoroughly with vinegar water, so that it is not too thick or clear;
et en emple le chevement de cest estrument, de coi ci est li forme:	And in using the construction of this instrument, about which here is the form:
Et ait ou chief une cheveure ou om met la medecine, si com li chevemens d’une cuillier, et met l’estrument a tout la medicine sus l’uve;	And at the top it has a container where one puts the medicine, like the bowl of a spoon, and place the instrument with all the medicine over the eye;
et li malaides soit gisans sus son costeit, si que li salive et li muscillaige corre de sa bouche de la medicine dedens, si qu’ele ne dessende a la gorge, et lou blece;	and the patient should lie on their side so that saliva and mucus flow from their mouth into the medicine, so it does not go down to the throat, and bind it;
puis tien ta main a tout la medicine et la presse sus l’uve, la quantiteit de la moitiet d’une houre, tant que tu la vois nercie et li mordications de la medicine soit apaisie;	then hold your hand over all the medicine and press it against the eye for half an hour, until you see it has congealed and the twitching caused by the medicine subsides;
et se tu vues, pren coton et l’envoloupe sus aucun estrument, et moille lou coton en la medicine, et boute l’estrument a tout le couton en la cainne desus, tant que li coton s’aerde sus l’uve;	and if you wish, take cotton and wrap it around any instrument, and moisten the cotton in the medicine, and place the instrument along with all the cotton on the wound, until the cotton adheres to the skin above the wound;
et fai ceu sovent, tant que li cauteres soit parfais, puis la laisse elle seche, et chiet aprés IIII jors ou V.	and do this frequently until the cauterization is complete, then let it dry, and after four days or five.
Et se tu as mestier de rencomencier lou cautere de la medicine, si le rencomence, et aprés le cautere l’essue entor l’uve, de couton embut em burre, et mundifie ceu qui est entor de la medicine;	And if you need to restart the cauterization with the medication, then do so, and after the cauterization wipe around the wound with cotton wrapped in butter, and clean what is around from the medication;
et soit arosez d’aigue froide, et soit curez de gargarismes tant qu’il soit sanez.	and let it be soaked in cold water, and let it be treated with gargles until it is healed.
Ceste cure est plus save de l’incision, ne que li cautere;	This treatment is more effective than incision, or the cautery;
s’elle est curee de fumigation selonc ceste maniere, pren calament et ysope et origanum et rue et camomille et avronne et semblans herbes, et les assemble toutes ou aucunes d’eles en I pot, et i met aisil, et fai bullir;	if it is treated by fumigation according to this method, take calamint and hyssop and oregano and rue and chamomile and wormwood and similar herbs, and put them all or some of them in a pot, add oil, and boil;
et li potz soit bien gluez de fort terre, et enmi le pot ait I estrument cheveit selonc ceste maniere:	and the pot should be well sealed with strong clay, and inside the pot have an instrument shaped as follows:
Et soit d’argent ou d’arain, et soit li uns des chiés boutez en la bouche dou malaide tant que li vapor monte a l’uve par la caine, tant que li uve soit mortifie;	And it should be made of silver or copper, and place one end in the patient's mouth so that the vapor rises to the eye through the tube until the condition is cured;
aprés lou rencomence sovent, tant que li uve seche, et garde que tu ne faices ceu au comencement de l’avenement de l’aposteme chaut, car plusors choses i avienent;	After you start again often, until the swelling subsides, and be careful not to do this at the beginning of the hot onset of the abscess, for many things happen.
et ne faire mie ceu fuer que a la declination d’aposteme chaut.	and do not do this while the heat of the abscess is declining.
Et se cist estrument n’est presens, si pren une caine et met dedens lou chief une craiffe d’uef, si que li bouche au malaide n’ait mie trop chaut;	And if this instrument is not present, take a cane and place a piece of eggshell inside the head so that the mouth of the patient does not become too hot;
car li craiffe d’uef ne lait mie la vapor grever la bouche, et c’est bone cure ensamble salut.	for the eggshell does not allow the vapor to oppress the mouth, and this is a good remedy together with safety.
Maintes fois s’aert a la gorge os ou espinee de poisson, ou aucune chose;	Many times it happens that bone or a fish spine, or some other thing, becomes stuck in the throat;
si covient donc que tu traies ceu que tu pues veoir, et li presse la lengue au soleil a tout l’estrument, si que tu voies mues la chose;	It is therefore necessary that you treat what you can see, and press the tongue to the sun with all the instruments so that you may see the movement of the thing;
et ceu que ne t’apert mie et est reponus en la gorge, covient que tu faices vomir le malaide ainsois que li viande soit cuite en l’estomac;	and what you cannot see and is lodged in the throat, you must make the patient vomit so that the food is cooked in the stomach;
par aventure si istra li chose aerse par le vomissement;	by chance, the foreign object will be expelled through vomiting;
ou li malaides englutisse une piece d’esponge, ou une piece de navel, ou une racine de laitue, ou I morceil de pain sec;	when the patient swallows a piece of sponge, or a piece of silk, or a root of lettuce, or a piece of dry bread;
et lie a l’esponge I fil, et puis la transglutisse;	and tie a thread to the sponge, and then guide it through the throat;
et quant elle venra au leu, si s’aerdra, et puis trairas fuer;	and when it comes to the place, it will harden, and then draw out the fire;
et s’elle ne vient fuer de ceu que nos avons dit, si pren I estrument de plonc selonc ceste forme:	and if it does not come from the place we mentioned, then take the instrument of flint according to this form:
Et soit li estrumens corbés au chief si qu’il puist plus legierement entrer en la gorge, et ait le chief en haut leveit;	And let the instrument be curved at the head so that it may more easily enter the throat, and have the head raised up;
et warde que tu ne touchier l’epiglote, que li tous ne li viegne, ne ne bouter mie l’os dedens;	and be careful not to touch the epiglottis, or suffocation may occur, nor should you push the bone in;
et mues vaut que li malaides i boute l’estrument, por ceu qu’il seit mues ou li chose est aerse;	and it is best for the patient to insert the instrument, so that he may be moved where the obstruction is located;
si la boute aval, ou il la traie fuer a tout l’estrument igalment, tant qu’elle soit fuer.	If the boil bursts, draw it out fully so that all the instrument is equally inside, until it is completely open.
de la sansue de la gorge	of the blood from the throat
Aucune fois est medicinee li sansue, si com j’ai dit en la division, par la cure de medicines;	Sometimes the blood is treated, as I said in the division, by the care of medicines;
et quant ceu ne profite mie, adonques regarde en la gorge dou malaide au soleil, puis que tu li presses la lengue a l’estrument que je t’ai dit.	and when that does not help, then look in the throat of the patient by the light of the sun, and press their tongue with the instrument I told you about.
Et se tu vois la sansue, si la trai a tout I petit uncine, ou as tenailles subtilz que valent a ceu.	And if you see the blood, draw it out with a small hook, or with fine forceps that are suitable for this.
Et se ceu ne vaut, si pren une caine chevee, et la boute en la gorge dou malaide, puis boute ou chevement de la caine I fer chaut, et fai ce sovent.	And if that is not effective, take a hooked cane and insert it into the patient's throat, then place a hot iron on the hook of the cane, and do this frequently.
Et se teigne li malaides d’aigue toute jor.	And if the patient is stained with water all day.
puis pren plein I voirre d’aigue froide, et oevre la bouche, et la giete ens sens englutir, et la mueve a sa main sovent;	Then take a full glass of cold water, work it in the mouth, and pour it down to swallow, and move it with your hand often;
et si tost com li sansue sent l’aigue, si chiet.	and as soon as the blood feels the water, it falls.
Et s’elle ne chiet si com nos avons dit, si subfumige lou malaide d’asefetide, a l’estrument que j’ai dit en la fumigation de l’uve;	And if it does not fall as we have said, then fumigate the patient with asafoetida, using the instrument that I mentioned in the fumigation of the eye;
fai ceu maintes fois, car elle cherra sens targier.	do this many times, for it will fall without delay.
Et li maniere de la fumigation si est que tu preignes I pot ou il ait charbons vis, et soit li pos covert d’un coverseil perciet en mileu, et en celui pertus soit li chiés de l’estrument;	And the method of the fumigation is that you take a pot with live coals inside, and cover it with a perforated lid, and in that hole place the stem of the instrument;
puis i giete ta fumigation, et li malaides mette lou chief de la cainne en sa bouche, et cloie la bouche, si que li fumee n’en isse mie, mais viegne jusc’a la sansue;	then pour in your fumigation, and have the patient place the end of the tube in their mouth, and close the mouth so that no smoke escapes, but reaches only to the blood;
et la sansue cherra maintenant, et s’elle ne chiet, si rencomence la fumigation par maintes fois;	and the blood will now flow out, and if it does not fall, then restart the fumigation multiple times;
et soffre li malaides soif, et menjuce choses salees et als, et ne boive point d’aigue;	and allow the patient to suffer thirst, and let them eat dirty and salty things, and do not let them drink water;
et adonques li iert mestier qu’elle isse fuer par cest governement.	and then it will be necessary for her to discharge fire through this regimen.
Et li forme de l’estrument a coi on trait la sansue, si est, quant on la puet veoir, semblans a tenailles corbés por mues entrer en la gorge;	And the shape of the instrument used to treat the blood, that is, when it can be seen, resembles curved tongs for inserting into the throat;
et ait semblance au bec de soigne, et i ait asperiteit de lime, si que ceu qu’elle prent, elle ne puet lassier;	and it has the appearance of a bird's beak, and there are teeth like a file, so that what it grasps, it cannot let go;
et vez ci la forme:	and see here the form:
li chapistres des apostemes	the chapter of abscesses
Mout de semblances d’aposteme sont, selonc ceu que li remembrance vient ci aprés d’un et d’autre en cest livre, et sont diver en perforation et en taille;	There are many types of abscesses, according to what the memory brings forth one after another in this book, and they differ in perforation and size;
et c’est en II manieres dont l’une est en sa semblance meisme, et de ceu qu’il tient moistor.	and it is in two ways, one of which is in its own likeness, and from those that it holds moisture.
Et li seconde maniere si est por les leus ou il sont au cors.	And the second way is for the places where they are on the body.
car li apostemes dou chief est autres que cil dou fondement, et li apostemes dou leu charnut est autres que cil qui vient en jointures, et chescuns ait son jugement en l’uevre.	for abscesses of the head are different from those of the buttocks, and abscesses of the flesh area are different from those that come in joints, and each has its own judgment in the work.
Et si a apostemes c’on ne doit mie percier, tant que li bowe est meure selonc son acomplissement;	And there are abscesses that one must not pierce until the swelling is dead according to its completion;
et si a de telz qu’il covient percier quant il sont crut, et ne meurent mie selonc lor acomplissement, si com aposteme qui sont delez jointures.	and there are such as must be pierced when they are hard, and do not die according to their completion, such as abscesses near joints.
Car quant apostemes vient delez jointures, et on le laisse tant qu’il est porris entor, par aventure si sont corrumput li liien et li nerf de la jointure, par coi ce est cause de contraction en celui membre.	For when abscesses come near joints, and one lets it remain until it is rotten around, by chance the ligaments and nerves of the joint are corrupted, thus causing contraction in that limb.
Ou li aposteme est delez lou membre principel, et se tu tardes la perforation tant qu’il soit meurez, si nuira au membre principeil;	When the abscess is near a principal limb, and if you delay piercing it until it is dead, it will harm the principal limb;
ou il est delez lou fondement, si le perce on ainsois qu’il soit meurs;	when it is near the fundament, pierce it accordingly so that it may die.
et ne covient mie que tu perces aposteme crut sens digestion acomplie, fuers que celui qui est delez lou fondement, qu’il ne porrisse em parfont, et soit alongiez dedens, et i viegne fistule;	and it is not right to pierce an abscess before the formation of pus is complete, except for one near the fundament, so that it does not fester and spread inside, leading to a fistula.
et ne puisse saner en grant termine.	and cannot be healed in a short time.
Et covient que tu saiches l’oure de la perforation de l’aposteme qui est meur selonc l’acomplissement, et c’est quant li dolor est apaisie, et li departemens de la fievre, et l’amenuisement de la dolor et de la roujor, et dou debatement et de l’aguisement dou chief de l’aposteme, et les autres signes;	And you must know the time for piercing an abscess that is dead according to its completion, which is when the pain has subsided, and the fever has abated, and there is a decrease in pain and redness, and the swelling of the head of the abscess subsides, and other signs.
et covient que tu faices seoir la perforation ou plus dependant leu de l’aposteme, et la ou il apert mues;	And you must make an incision at the lowest point of the abscess, where it is most apparent.
et soit li perforation dou lonc dou cors, et se li apostemes est as mains ou as piez, ou en jointures et au ners et as arteres, et en toz leus igalz ou il n’a point de ploieure.	And let the incision be along the body, and if the abscess is on the hands or feet, at joints and nerves and arteries, in all places equally where there is no tenderness.
En ces que ploient, par selonc celui membre.	In cases of bleeding, according to that limb.
Et quant apostemes est en leu charnut, si vaut mues que tu laisses la perforation tant qu’il soit confermez en digestion acomplie, si com nos avons dit.	And when an abscess is in the flesh, it is better to wait until it is confirmed to be in complete resolution before proceeding with puncture, as we have said.
Car se tu lou perces devant ceu, si iert alongiez li cors dou venim de lui, et est plains de mout d’ordure;	For if you pierce it before these points, the venom of the abscess will spread through the body, and it will be full of much pus.
et par aventure endurcissent les levres et li parfondetez de lui.	And by chance the lips and depth of it become hardened.
Et si a aucun aposteme que sont perciet selonc le large dou cors, selonc ceu que li membres en ait mestier.	And if there is an abscess that needs to be punctured according to the width of the body, according to what the limb requires.
Et covient que tu amenistres em petis apostemes, petis pertus;	And you must treat small abscesses with small incisions.
et en grans apostemes, grans pertus, et maintes fendures selonc la semblance de la grandor de l’aposteme;	and in large abscesses, large openings, and many fissures according to the size of the abscess;
et si a de tels apostemes ou il covient chever lou keur, et coper;	and if there are such abscesses where it is necessary to lay the cautery on them and cover;
quant il est jai devenus ausi com I drapelz, et est amortis, si covient faire ausi com on fait as bubes:	when they have become like the tips of leaves, and are softened, then it is necessary to do as one does with blisters:
et si a de telz que sont fendut en III angles, et si a de telz dont on cope ausi com la fuelle de mirte, si com apostemes des angres;	and if there are some that are split into three corners, and there are others that one covers as with the leaf of myrtle, like abscesses of the armpits;
et si a de telz ou on fait une reonde taille, et autres tailles et semblant copeure.	and if there are some where one makes a round incision, and other incisions and similar coverings.
Cil qui n’ont point de chief, si com aposteme souef superficial, il covient que tu lou perces plainnement;	Those who have an abscess without a head, such as a superficial subcutaneous abscess, you must pierce it completely;
et covient quant li apostemes est gros, et il a coillit grant bowe, et tu lou perces, si ne traire mie toute la bowe en celle houre, mais en trai une partie;	and when the abscess is large and there is much pus collected, and you pierce it, do not draw out all the pus at that hour, but draw out only a part;
puis estoupe l’aposteme jusc’a l’autre jor, puis en trai aucune chose derechief;	then plug the abscess until the next day, then draw out some more afterwards;
fai ceu par maintes fois de greit en greit, tant que li bowe isse toute;	do this gradually over many times, until all the pus has been expelled;
meismement se li malaides est de foible vertut, ou femme portans, ou petis enfes, ou viez hons decrepites.	especially if the patient is weak, or a pregnant woman, or small children, or old men who are infirm.
Car li esperis tressaut aucune fois avec l’issue de la bowe, que par aventure muert li malaides, et tu ne t’en persois.	For the pus sometimes suddenly stops coming out with the pus, which by chance can kill the patient, and you would not be blamed for it.
Eschuez donques cest chapistre par grant cautele, et quant tu as perciet ton aposteme, si essue la plaie, et regarde se li plaie de l’aposteme est petite;	Avoid this chapter with great caution, and when you have punctured the abscess, wash the wound, and examine whether the wound of the abscess is small;
et se c’est une tailleure plainne, si amenistre tentes de lin ou de viez coton;	and if it is a full-sized wound, then apply bandages made of linen or old cotton;
et se c’est uns grans apostemes, et il i a mout de pertus, si covient que tu boutes en chescun une tente si qu’ele viegne l’une contre l’autre;	and if it is a large abscess with many openings, then you must insert a bandage into each one so that they come together;
et se tu as copeit en l’aposteme une partie dou cuir, et tu l’as cheveit entor, si covient que tu l’emplisses de viel couton ou de rasure de dras de lin sens moistor, et le lie jusc’au tier jor;	and if you have cut into the abscess part of the skin and have sewn around it, then you must fill it with old cotton or linen lint that is dry, and bind it until the third day;
puis l’oste, et le cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then remove it, and treat it with ointment until it is healed.
Et se decorremens de sanc avient a ton ovraige, si amenistre aigue froide et aisil, et moille I drapeil, et met sor le leu decorrant par maintes fois.	And if bleeding occurs during your work, administer cold and soothing remedies, and wet a cloth, placing it on the bleeding area multiple times.
Et se li decorremens de sanc persevere, se i amenistre governement et cure, et les poudres que j’ai dit em mains leus en cest livre, et se c’est ou tens d’iver, et li leus ou li apostemes est est mout nervous, si couvient que tu mettes sus tentes et drapelz moilliez en vin et en oile chaut;	And if the flow of blood persists, administer management and treatment, and use the powders that I have mentioned in this book, and if it is winter time, and the place where the abscess is very dry, then you must put up tents and cloths moistened with wine and warm oil;
et se c’est en esteit, et li leus est charnus, si covient que tu mes sus drapelz moilliez en aigue et en oile, ou en vin et en oile froit, jusc’au tier jor, si com nos avons dit;	and if it is in summer, and the place is fleshed out, then you must apply cloths moistened with water and oil, or with wine and cold oil, until the third day, as we have said;
et puis deslie l’aposteme et l’essue et le cure, si com il covient, tant qu’il soit sanez.	and then open the abscess and wipe it clean and treat it as is appropriate until it is healed.
Et ceu covient il conoistre universement en cures des apostemes:	And this must be known universally in the treatment of abscesses:
or vos ai dit coment on doit aler avant as cures des apostemes, et vez ci le chapistre.	And I have told you how one should proceed with the treatment of abscesses, and here is the chapter.
des soros	Of sweats
Ou keur dou chief vienent petis apostemes, et sont manieres de nous que sont en toiles, ausi com li josier d’une geline, et mout en i a de semblances.	For small abscesses in the head come in various forms, like the feathers of a goose, and there are many similarities.
Il en i a de gras et de telz ou il a moistor ausi com poulz;	There are some that are fatty and of such a nature that they contain moisture as well as pus;
et si a de telz qui sont dur et pierous au taillier, et n’i a point de doutance se li artere n’i fait contraire.	and there are some that are hard and stony to the touch, and there is no doubt about them unless an artery opposes.
Et li ovraiges de la taille si est que tu esprueve a tout I estrument qui est apelez «entromissoire», de coi li forme vient ci aprés, quel chose il contient.	And the work on the waist is such that you should try all the instruments called "entromissoire," of which the forms are shown hereafter, what they contain.
Car s’il contient moistor, si lou fent par desus dou lonc.	For if there is moisture, then he splits it from above along the length.
Et quant li moistor est vuidie, si escorche sens rien laissier la peil qui contient celle moistor, car il revient adés quant on i laisse rien;	And when the moisture is drained, carefully scrape away without leaving anything of the skin that contained the moisture, for it returns quickly if anything is left behind;
puis plonge coton en oignement egiptien, s’il est presens;	then dip cotton in Egyptian ointment, if it is available;
se ceu non, en aigue et en seil, et en emple la plaie, et la laisse jusc’a l’autre jor;	if not, in water and in salt, and in poultice the wound, and leave until the next day;
et ceu corront ceu qui est demorez dou nit.	and those who remain from the night shall run these tasks.
Et pues rencomence lou coton, si com devant, le second jor, et lou tier, tant que tu saiches bien qu’il ne demoure point dou nit;	And then restart the cotton, as before, on the second day, and on the third, until you know well that none remain from the night;
puis cure la plaie d’oignement a ceu convenauble, tant qu’il soit sanez.	then treat the wound with appropriate ointment until it is healed.
Et se li apostemes tient I nout gras, si le cope selonc ceste forme, dou lonc;	And if the abscess holds one month, cut it according to this form, lengthwise;
et i giete tes oncines, et l’escorche de toutes pars, et met toute ta cure de traire fuer la cotte ou il gist;	and place your ointments there, and scrape it from all sides, and apply all your care to draining the pus where it lies;
et se li artere te fait contraire, si fai ceu que je t’ai dit aprés.	And if the artery opposes this, do as I told you afterward.
Et ausi fai de l’aposteme s’il est pierous, et dou taillier et dou curer si com je t’ai dit.	And do the same for an abscess if it is stony, and in cutting and curing as I have told you.
Et li taille sus l’aposteme pierous et le moiste, si est plus legiere, car il sont de poc de sanc.	And when you cut into a stony abscess and moisten it, it becomes easier, for they contain little blood.
Et si a aucuns de ces apostemes ou chief ou il n’a point de moistor, et de ces fut I apostemes que je copai ou chief d’une vielle femme;	And if there is an abscess on someone's head where there is no moisture, and it was from such abscesses that I treated one on the head of an old woman;
et trovai l’aposteme ausi com une piere xourde, aspre et blainche, et ne pooit brisier;	and I found the abscess like a hard, rough, and white stone that could not be broken;
et s’on en eust ferut aucun, on li eust ausi bien fait plaie com d’une piere.	and if one had touched it, it would have caused the same injury as a stone.
En autres apostemes venans ou chief, fuer que ces qui vienent as chief des enfans et as racines des oreilles, li overture si soit toz jors au plus dependant leu, por mues issir la bowe;	In other abscesses that occur on the head, such as those that come at the heads of children and at the roots of the ears, the incision should always be made in the lowest place possible, so that pus can exit easily;
et les cure si com il covient.	and treat them as is appropriate.
des scrophules	scrofulas
Maintes fois avienent cist aposteme au col, et desoz les asseles, et ens angres, et aucune fois vienent autre part ou cors, et sont mout, et sont enjanrees l’une avec l’autre.	This type of abscess often occurs in the neck, and sometimes below the armpits, and also in angles, and at times they appear elsewhere on the body, and are very numerous, growing one with another.
Et chescune scrophule est proprement dedens sa cote, si com li nout et li aposteme dou chief, si com nos avons dit;	And each scrofula is properly within its own area, such as the boil and the abscess of the head, as we have said;
et les semblances de ces scrophules sont maintes.	and there are many similarities among these scrofulas.
Il i a de teles que contienent moistor, et si a de malignes qui ne vuellent obeir a santeit.	There are some that contain moisture, and there are others that are malignant and do not wish to obey [the treatment].
en celle donques que tu vois de bone disposition au tochier, et est semblans a la color dou cors, et muet de chescune part et n’est mie aerse as ners dou col ne a l’artere ne au conduit, et n’est mie parfonde;	in the one that you see has good disposition when touched, and it resembles the color of the skin, and is not hard near the neck veins or arteries or conduits, and is not deep;
si covient que tu la copes par desus, et l’escorche de chescune partie, et estent les II levres dou keur as oncines, se tu en as mestier, si com nos avons dit en apostemes dou chief;	you should cut it open from above, and scrape each part, and spread the two edges of the wound with scissors, if you need to, as we have said for head abscesses;
et la trai poc et poc, et soies seur que tu ne coper lou nerf ne la voine, et ne soit mie li spatumile agus ne trenchans, que li mains n’eschaipe, et ne voise trop avant, que tu ne coper mie ceu que tu ne dois.	And move it bit by bit, and be sure that you do not cut the nerve or the vein, and let the spatula not be sharp nor cutting, so as not to harm the hand, and do not go too far forward, so that you do not cut what you should not.
Et se tu copes la voinne ou l’artere, et ceu ne te laisse ovrer, si met en la plaie vitriole broiet, ou aucunes poudres que restainchent sanc, et estraint la plaie;	And if you cut the vein or artery, and it does not allow you to work on it, then put into the wound vitriol ground up, or some powders that constrict blood flow, and press on the wound;
et la laisse tant que li apostemes soit apaisiez, et soit amollie li plaie, et encomence a porrir.	and leave it until the abscess is reduced, and the wound becomes soft and begins to pus.
Et quant li sans est estainchiez, si revien a ton ovraige, tant que tu l’acomplisses;	And when the bleeding is stopped, return to your work until you complete it;
puis quier a ton doit indice s’il i demoure nules petites scrophules, si les cope et les munde.	Then ask your proper instrument if there remain any small scrofulous swellings, and cut them out and clean them.
Et s’il a en la racine de la scrophule voinne grant, si ne covient mie que tu copes celle scrophule en sa racine, mais la lie d’un fil double fort, et la laisse cheoir par li, sens nuisement;	And if there is a large vein at the root of the scrofula, you must not cut that scrofula at its root, but tie it off with strong double thread, and let it fall away without harm;
puis emple la plaie de viel coton plongiet en oignement egiptien, puis la cure.	Then pack the wound with old cotton soaked in Egyptian ointment, and then treat it.
Et se tu copes toute la scrophule, si covient que tu assembles les II levres de la plaie, et les cout maintenant, puis qu’il n’i a point demoreit de superfluiteit por la grandor de la scrophule.	And if you cut out the entire boil, then you must bring together the two edges of the wound and sew them now, since there is no excess tissue due to the size of the boil.
si covient que tu entendes a coper la racine de li, et traire fuer, et la cout si com nos avons dit.	Then you must focus on cutting the root of it, extracting the pus, and sewing as we have said.
Celles scrophules que tienent superfluiteit, perce lai ou il apert meure;	Those scrofulas that hold excess, pierce them where it is most apparent;
et la perce ensi com celle devant dite, en dependant, puis i amenistre tentes avec oignement et semblans choses, si qu’elle corrompe ceu qui est demorez de la corruption;	and pierce them as was said before, then administer strips with ointment and similar things, so that it corrupts what remains of the corruption;
et quant li plaie est bien mundee, si la cure d’oignement enjanrant char, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And when the wound is well cleansed, apply an ointment for healing flesh until it is healed.
de squinance	of contusion
Li ancien dirent et parlerent de la tailleure de la gorge;	The ancients spoke and wrote about the treatment of the throat;
mais je ne vis onques en nostre terre qui la feist, et c’est li escripture de lor parole.	but I have never seen anyone in our land who practiced it, and this is the writing of their words.
A ces qui ont squinance, il covient que li fendure de la gorge qui est apelee «epiglote» soit eschuee;	For those who have a squint, it is necessary that the split in the throat which is called "epiglottis" be excised;
et c’on ne faice aide par ceu, por ceu que toutes les voines et li pormon dou malaide sont a ces qui ont aposteme chaut en la bouche, ou en la gorge ou en II amandres.	and one should not assist with this, because all the veins and the flesh of the patient are affected in those who have a hot abscess in the mouth, or in the throat, or in both tonsils.
Quant li maladie est en la chenal dou pormon, il covient coper l’epiglote por fuir la perdition qui vient de l’estranglement.	When the illness is in the phlegm channel, it is necessary to cut the epiglottis to avoid the danger of choking.
Il covient donques, quant nos volons fendre l’epiglote, que nos le fendons desoz III cercles ou IIII une petite fendure dou travers, entre les II cercles ou par la quantiteit de la fendure dou syfac, ne mie en la cartillaige;	It is therefore necessary, when we wish to divide the epiglottis, that we make a small transverse cut between three or four circles, or rather between two circles, according to the size of the cut on the surface, not in the cartilage;
et cil leus si est covenaubles a la section de l’epiglote qu’il n’i a point de char, et li vasseil sont lonc d’enqui.	and those places are suitable for the division of the epiglottis where there is no flesh, and the vessels are long on both sides.
Et se li maistres est paourous, si covient qu’il estende le cuir de la gorge a tout l’oncine, puis fende lou keur tant qu’il viegne a la cheneil;	And if the master is fearful, he should stretch the skin of the throat for one inch, then cut through until he reaches the cartilage;
et eschue les vasselz de sanc, se tu vois aucune chose, et puis cope lou syfac, si com nos avons dit;	and avoid the blood vessels, if you see any, and then cut the surface as we have said;
et est demostrez par la section dou fleume de la cheneil ki saut fuer par le leu qui est rompus, et par la defaute de la voix;	and it is demonstrated by the division of the blood vessel in the neck which jumps out at the place that is broken, and by the lack of voice;
et laisse la plaie overte une piece.	and leave the wound open for a piece.
Et quant li houre est passee de coi on doute l’estranglement, assemble les II levres de la plaie dou keur, et la cout toute soule sens la cartillaige;	And when the hour has passed from which strangulation is feared, bring together the two lips of the wound of the heart, and sew it all along away from the cartilage;
puis aministre medicines qui font naistre char, tant qu’il soit sanez.	then administer medicines that promote flesh growth until it is healed.
Albucasim dist c’on ne faice ce jusc’a tant que li gorge est toute estoupee, et li malaides est jugiez a mort, et li defaut li alaine.	Albucasim says that one should not do this until the throat is completely blocked, and the patient is judged to be dying, and death approaches.
Adonques cope on l’epiglote por ceu que li malaides ne puet alener, et il respire par la plaie, et ensi est gardez de mort;	Then cut off the epiglottis because the patient cannot swallow, and he breathes through the wound, and thus is saved from death;
et por ce commanderent li anciain a laissier la plaie overte tant que li malice de la maladie soit passee, et elle est passee en III jors ou en IIII Et adonques il comanderent a coudre la plaie et curer, tant qu’elle fut curee;	and for this reason the ancients commanded to leave the wound open until the malice of the disease has passed, and it passes in three days or four; then they commanded to sew up the wound and clean it, until it was cleaned.
et je vos dirai ceu que je vis.	and I will tell you what I saw.
Je vis que une damoisele prist I coutel, et le ficha en sa gorge, et copa partie des chenelz dou pormon;	I saw that a maiden took a knife and stuck it in her throat, and cut part of the windpipe.
et je fui apelez por li curer, et la trovai ausi com morte.	and I was called to treat her, and found her as if dead.
Je descovris la plaie, et trovai le sanc qui en estoit issus, et soi bien qu’elle n’avoit mie copeit voine ne conduit fuer que la gorge, et li vens issoit fuer par la plaie.	I examined the wound and found the blood that had come out, and realized that she had not cut any vein or vital artery but rather the wind was escaping through the wound.
Je me hastai, et cousi la plaie, et la curai tant qu’elle fut sanee;	I hurried, sewed up the wound, and treated it until she was healed;
et n’avint a la damoisele fuer qu’elle fut roge de voix, et revint aprés a sa disposition;	And it happened to the lady that she became red-faced, and afterwards returned to her disposition;
por ceu di je que en la tailleure de l’epiglote n’ait mie paour.	For this reason I say that in the cutting of the epiglottis there should be no fear.
de la grosse gorge	of the large throat
Cist apostemes est apelez «hernie de gorge», et est uns grans apostemes en color d’une jaisse, et est molt en femmes;	This abscess is called a "throat hernia," and it is a large abscess in the shape of a bean, and it occurs mostly in women;
et est selonc II manieres:	and it occurs in two manners:
naturez, et accidens;	naturally, and as accidents;
ou natureil n’a point d’engien.	in the natural case, there is no swelling.
Et li accidens est selonc II manieres, de coi l’une est semblans a gras nous, et li autre maniere est semblans a aposteme qui vient de nous d’artere;	And the accidental case occurs in two manners, one of which is similar to fat for us, and the other manner is similar to an abscess that comes from us due to an artery;
et il i ait paour, et ne covient mie ovrer de feir fuers que en celi qui est petite, et le prueve et cerche a tout l’intromissoire:	And there is fear in it, and one must not operate with fierce force except on the one that is small, and prove and search throughout the entire incision:
se tu le trueves ausi com I nout gras, et ne pent a nulle voine, si le cope, si com on cope les nous, et le trai a tout sa coife, s’il en i a point;	if you find it as thick as fatty tissue, and it cannot be in any vein, cut it like one cuts knots, and draw out all its coat if there is any.
et encerche bien tot, et le cure si com il covient, tant qu’il soit sanez parfaitement.	and search thoroughly right away, and treat it as is appropriate, until it is completely healed.
des nous	from us
Maintes manieres de nous sont, dont je dirai toutes les semblances;	There are many kinds of knots, of which I will describe all the similarities;
et or covient que je die toute la difference qui est entre nout et issue.	and now it is necessary for me to explain all the differences that exist between knots and issues.
Je dis que issue est chalors et fievre tenans, tant que li ebulicions est passee, et est acomplie li porriture;	I say that sweat and fever come then, until the boiling is past, and the pus is complete;
adonques repose li fievre et li chalor.	then the fever and heat subside.
Avec lou nout n’a ne chalor ne fievre ne dolor, et contient I syfac, qui est ses propres sac et est selonc la color dou cors, et encomence ausi com une jaisse, et devient gros;	With the poultice there is no heat nor fever nor pain, and it contains flour, which is its own substance and matches the color of the skin, and it begins like a patch, and becomes large;
et sont selonc II semblances, ou grais, ou moiste, et mout de color sont si com j’ai dit en la division.	and they are of two types, either greasy or moist, and many colors are as I have said in the division.
Il covient, quant tu viens a la cure dou nout, que tu esprueves et l’enquier premierement a tout l’estrument qui est apelez «entromissoire», selonc ce que sa forme venra ou chapistre qui est aprés.	It is necessary, when you come to the treatment of the knot, that you test and inquire first about all the instruments which are called "entromissoire", according to what their form will come in the chapter which is after.
Et li maniere de l’inquisicion des apostemes des nous est que tu preignes ou plus moiste leu que tu trueves en l’aposteme, et torne tes dois poc et poc, tant que tu saiches que li estrumens ait perciet le keur, puis que ce soit selonc la grandor de l’aposteme;	And the method of examining abscesses is that you take the moistest part that you find in the abscess, and turn your two fingers back and forth, until you know that the instrument has pierced the core, as befits the size of the abscess;
puis estrai l’entromissoire, et pren garde en ceu que saut fuer.	Then extract the interosseous element, and take care not to damage it.
Se moistor corrans cort, queil color elle ait, si le fent si com j’ai dit des autres apostemes;	If moisture flows out when cutting, regardless of its color, treat it as I have said for other abscesses;
et se aprés l’entromissoire nen vient moistor, saiches qu’il est gras, si le fent donques en croix, et le prent as pinceures, et l’escorche legierement de chescune part et warde la cotte ou il gist que tu la traies saine avec le nout;	and if after extracting the interosseous element no moisture comes out, know that it is fatty, then cut it in a cross shape, and take it with forceps, and lightly scrape from each side and be careful to treat the coat where it lies so you can pull it out healthy with the knot;
et se tu ne la pues traire saine, si la trai par pieces si qu’il n’i demoure rien.	and if you cannot pull it out whole, then remove it piece by piece so nothing remains.
Car s’il i demoure rien, si revient li nous par maintes fois;	For if anything remains, the pain will return many times;
et s’il en demore un poc, et li sans te grieve, si emple la plaie d’aucunes poudres corrosives agues, et estraint la plaie, et met sus choses apaisans aposteme chaut, et le cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez;	and if it remains a little while, and the blood does not flow, then apply the wound with some corrosive powder, and hold the wound steady, and place hot poultices for abscesses, and treat it with other remedies until it is healed;
et se li nous est grans, si cout les II levres de la plaie, et le cure de ceu qui enjanre char.	and if the wound is large, then sew together the two edges of the wound, and treat it with what promotes flesh growth.
et se li voine batans t’est contraire ou autre si te haste et emple le leu de vitriole broiet, et lou laisse liiet II jors ou III, tant que li plaie porrisse, et repose li ebulicion dou sanc;	and if the wound resists or another issue arises, then hurry and apply a place treated with powdered vitriol, and leave it for two days or three, until the wound begins to pus, and then treat it with blood boiling.
puis revien au coper ceu que i est demoreit dou nout.	then return to copper the remaining part of the wound.
Vez ci les formes des estrumens entromissoires, et sont de III manieres:	See here the forms of the instruments used for insertion, and they are of three kinds:
grans et moien et petit;	large, medium, and small;
et s’en i a III quarrez qui sont apelez «albaret», et I qui est apelez «breb», et s’en i a de III manieres:	and there are three squares which are called "albaret," and one which is called "breb," and they are of three kinds:
grant, moien, et petit, por encerchier les apostemes de fistule;	large, medium, and small, for encircling the abscesses of fistulas;
et sont ausi com les aguilles dont on cout les sorceles, et sont d’arain citrin, ou de fer, ou d’argent, et mues valent cil qui sont jaune, et sont plus esprovez de plonc noir por encerchier les corbeures de fistule;	and they are also like the needles used to sew sorcerers' tools, and are made of yellow brass, or iron, or silver, and those that are yellow are said to be more effective for encircling fistula bends;
et sont de III manieres:	and there are of three manners:
grans, moiens, et petis, selonc la quantiteit de la largesce des pertus.	large, medium, and small, according to the quantity of the width of the holes.
Les formes des oncines sont de mout de semblances, si com tu vois ci:	The forms of tumors are of many appearances, as you see here:
grans, moiens, et petis;	large, medium, and small;
et si a oncines qui ont II corbeures de III manieres ausi;	and there are tumors that have two curves in three manners as well;
et si a oncines qui ont III corbeures, et sont ausi de III manieres;	and there are tumors that have three curves, and they are also of three manners;
et si a oncines qui ont II corbeures, et oncines d’une corbeure soulement, et sont de III manieres;	and there are tumors that have two curves, and tumors with only one curve, and they are also of three manners;
et tuit cist sont necessaire en lor leu.	And all these are necessary in their place.
Li chief de ces a coi on fent sont trenchant, et de telz i a qui ne taillent mie fuer que d’une part, dont on escorche les nous, por ceu c’on ne cope la voine ne le nerf;	The head of these for which one performs the operation is sharp, and there are some that cut only from one side, so as not to scrape the flesh, for this reason one does not cut the vein or the nerve.
et de ces intromissoires sont les alemeles reponues en mainches, si que li malaide ne s’en persoivent a l’overture des apostemes;	and of these interosseous ones, the alemeles are placed in sleeves so that the patient does not feel them at the opening of abscesses;
et sont de III manieres:	and there are three kinds:
grant, petit, et moien, si com tu vois;	large, small, and medium, as you see;
et n’en use on mie fuer que en leu charnut, si com jambes, et bras, et mameles, et as angres, et en semblans leus;	and one uses them only in fleshy parts such as legs, arms, breasts, and similar places;
et aucune fois fait on I autre estrument petit, semblant a escorces de fistices, selonc ceste forme, a coi on estainche sanc:	And sometimes one makes another instrument small, resembling the rind of figs, in this form, with which one stops blood:
et le met on aucune fois au leu qui saine a copement des voines, et as arteres, et aucune fois reont selonc ceste grant forme:	and it is placed sometimes at the place where the veins are cut, and at the arteries, and sometimes follow this large form:
Aucune fois enflent les mameles d’aucuns homes quant cil encomencent estre corrumput, tant qu’eles semblent mameles de feme;	Sometimes the testicles of some men swell when they begin to be corrupted, so much that they seem like women's breasts;
et demorent laides et enflees, et qui les vuet curer, si le covient soier selonc ceste forme des ceste ligne .b. jusques a .g.:	and remain deformed and swollen, and if one wishes to treat them, it is necessary to incise according to this form from line b to g:
puis escorche la graisse, et emple la plaie de medicine enjanrant char, puis assemble les II levres de la plaie a costure, et la cure tant qu’ele soit sanee;	then scrape off the fat, and apply medicine that heals flesh to the wound, then bring together the two edges of the wound with stitches, and treat it until it is healed;
et se li mamele cline aval, et est amolie por sa grandor si com il avient as femmes, si la fent en II costelz desus, par II semblans fendures;	and if the testicle descends and is enlarged due to its size as happens with women, then cut it into two parts above, through two similar incisions;
de coi l’une soit tenans a l’autre a la fin de l’une et de l’autre, si que li plus grans ligne conteigne la menor selonc ceste forme, des ceste ligne .b. jusc’a la ligne .g.;	so that one is held to the other at the end of each, so that the larger line contains the smaller according to this form, from this line 2 until the line g;
puis escorche le cuir qui est entre les II levres, et oste la graisse, et i amenistre ceu que nos avons dit de costure et de poudres, et ceu qui est necessaire en la cure, tant qu’il soit sanez;	then peel the skin that is between the two lips, and remove the fat, and apply what we have said about suturing and powders, and whatever is necessary for treatment until it is healed;
et s’il n’est sanez, ou li incision n’est mie toute faite, por ceu que li malaides ne vuet reposer, ou por le decorrement de sanc, si covient que tu emplisses la plaie de coton moilliet en oignement corrosif;	and if it is not healed, or the incision has not been fully made, because the patient does not want to rest, or due to excessive bleeding, you must fill the wound with cotton soaked in a caustic ointment;
et le laisse tant qu’il menjuce le remenant et la graisse, puis le cure tant qu’il soit saneis.	and leave it until it has absorbed the remaining fluid and fat, then treat it until it is healed.
des apostemes des asselles	abscesses of the buttocks
Cist apostemes que vienent desoz les asseles sont manieres de scrophules dures ou il ait cotes, et s’en i a que contienent moistor.	These abscesses that come under the buttocks are like hard scrofulous lumps containing sides, and there are some that contain moisture.
Cil donques qui contienent moistor covient qu’il soient copez selonc ceste forme, des la ligne .b. jusc’a la ligne .g.:	Those that contain moisture should be cut according to this form, from line .b. to the line .g.:
Et quant toute li bowe qui est en l’aposteme est vuidie, si emple la plaie de viel coton, et la laisse jusc’a l’autre jor, puis oste tout le coton, et cure d’oignement avenant a ceu tant qu’il soit sanez.	And when all the pus in the abscess is emptied out, fill the wound with old cotton, and leave it until the next day, then remove all the cotton, and treat it with ointment as needed until it heals.
Et se li apostemes est de semblances de scrophules, si le fent si com nos avons dit en fendures des scrophules, et se li plaie rent bowe, si amenistre cautere si com nos avons dit devant.
