And if the abscess resembles a scrofula, then cut it as we have said for incisions of scrofulas, and if the wound discharges pus, then treat it with cautery as we have said before.
de la routure de l’artere	Of the rupture of the artery
Quant li artere est route, et li cuir est soudez qui est sus, si en vient maintes fois apostemes, et tout aussi avient il a la voine enflee et aposteme;	When the artery is ruptured, and the skin above it is sealed, abscesses often occur; and similarly, when the vein swells and becomes an abscess,
et si le conoist on ensi quant c’est por l’artere, si est li apostemes lons em parfont;	and when it is recognized as such for the artery, the abscesses are long and deep;
et quant tu le sens a tes dois, si sens I estraignement;	and when you feel it with your fingers, you sense the tightness;
et quant c’est por la voine, si est reons defuer aparans;	and when it is for the vein, it appears swollen and protruding;
et c’est folie de coper cest aposteme, et meismement quant il est desoz les asseles et as angres et ou col et em mout d’autres leus, et est mout grans.	and it is foolish to incise this abscess, especially when it is near the armpits and angles of the neck and on the collarbone in many other places, and it is very large.
Il covient donques eschuir la cure de fer, et celui qui est a chief covient eschuir ausi, et en celui qui est d’enfleure d’artere fent par desus le cuir dou lonc;	One must therefore avoid the treatment with iron, and for one who is at the head it should also be avoided, and in one who is swollen from an artery cut above the skin;
puis oevre la taille as oncines, et depart bellement l’artere des toiles, tant qu’ele soit descoverte;	then treat the area with bandages, and carefully separate the artery from the tissues, until it is exposed;
puis boute desoz li une aguille, et la fai percier jusc’a l’autre costeit, et estraint l’artere d’un fil double en II leus, selonc ceu que je t’ai ensigniet en l’estraction des II arteres qui sont en temples;	then insert a needle into it from the opposite side, and pierce it to the other side, and tie the artery with a doubled thread in two places, as I have taught you in the extraction of the two arteries that are in the temples;
puis point le leu qui est entre les II liens d’un intromissoire tant que li sans en isse qui i est, et soit deliiez li aposteme;	then puncture the area between the two ligatures with an instrument so that the blood flows out which is inside, and release the abscess;
puis amenistre la cure que enjanre bowe, tant que li liien chient;	Then administer the treatment that induces urine flow, until the patient urinates;
puis cure ceu d’oignement avenant a ceu, tant qu’il soit sanez;	Then treat them with appropriate ointment until they are healed;
et se li apostemes est por la taille de la voinne, si covient que tu teignes a ta main ceu que tu pues de l’aposteme a tout le cuir, puis boute l’aguille desoz le leu que tu tiens a ta main, et la fai percier, et i ait I fil double, si que tu le trais de l’autre costeit;	and if the abscess is near the vein, then you should paint with your hand as much of the abscess area as possible, then pierce the needle beneath where your hand is, and make a puncture, and there should be double thread so that you can draw it out from the other side;
puis lie l’aposteme, si com je t’ai dit, ou liien de l’une de II pars as II chiés dou fil;	then ligature the abscess, as I told you, with one part of the thread around each of the two threads;
et se tu doutes que li filz n’isse fuer, si i reboute une autre aguille a tout I fil desoz tout l’aposteme a l’incision de la premiere aguille, et estraint les filz en IIII leus;	and if you fear that the thread might break, then pierce another needle along the entire length of the first incision beneath the abscess, and tie the threads in four places;
puis cope l’aposteme tant que li superfluitez en isse, puis cope la superfluiteit dou keur et laisse ceu qui est liiez;	Then cut the abscess until the excess matter flows out, then cut the excess of the heart and leave those that are bound;
puis met sus I drapeil moilliet en vin et en oile, puis li amenistre cures de tentes et d’oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then apply a moist cloth soaked in wine and oil, then treat with bandages and ointments until he is healed.
des apostemes des ners	abscesses of the nerves
Ausi com aposteme vienent en l’artere et en la voine, vienent aposteme as ners quant il sont ferut, ou par trop grant travail, et semblans choses.	Just as abscesses can occur in the artery and vein, abscesses also affect the nerves when they are injured, or from excessive labor, and similar circumstances.
Et ceu avient plus sovent as adjutoires et as dois et en toz leus ou il ait jointures, et c’est I grief apostemes, et sa color semble la color dou cors, et est em plusors dispositions sens dolor;	And this happens more often in the shoulders and elbows and in all places where there are joints, and these are severe abscesses, and their color resembles the color of the skin, and they cause great pain in many conditions.
et quant on l’estraint forment, si sent li malaides dolor, et n’est mie em parfont dou cors, mais desoz lou keur;	and when it is pressed firmly, the patient feels pain, and it is not in the flesh but near the heart;
et muet bien de toutes pars, et ne va ne avant ne arrier, ne desoz ne desus, et celui qui est en jointures ne covient mie coper par fer:	and it moves well in all directions, and does not go forward or backward, nor up nor down, and those that are in joints should not be cut with a knife:
par aventure i vanroit contraction;	by chance there might be contraction;
et cil qui est ou chief ou ou front, fent le cuir au spatumile.	and for those who have it on the head or forehead, cut the skin with a scalpel.
Se li apostemes est petis, si le tien a unes tenailles, et le cope en sa racine;	If the abscess is small, grasp it with forceps and cut it at its root;
et s’il est grans, si le sospent a l’oncine, et l’escorche, puis l’oste et assemble la plaie a la costure, et lou cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	and if it is large, suspend it with an incision, then peel it, remove it, and sew up the wound, healing it until it is healed.
des grosses boces pendans	large hanging mouths
Aucune fois avient en ventres et ne mie autre part thelul, et est une maladie qui est apelee «funge» par la semblance d’aus, et est li racine subtilz, et li chiez gros;	At times, this occurs in the abdomen and not elsewhere, and it is a disease called "fungus" by its likeness, and its root is subtle, and the growth is large;
et en i a de petis et de mout grans;	and there are both small and very large ones;
et je vis I home qui en avoit II ou ventre qui estoient plus semblans a funges que ai autre chose, et n’i avoit point de difference, et estoient blanc, et avoient menue racine, et estoient jai fendut, et en corroit adés moistor.	and I saw a man who had two of them in his abdomen which resembled mushrooms more than anything else, and there was no difference between them, they were white, and they had fine roots, and moisture corroded them quickly.
Je les copai et trovai en l’un XVIII onces pesant, et en l’autre VI З., et li ovraiges en l’incision si est que tu regardes se li malaides est moistes, et li color de l’artelul est blainche et moiste et de subtil racine;	I removed them and found one to weigh eighteen ounces and the other six, and in the procedure during the incision you must observe if the patient is moist, and the color of the muscle is white and moist with a fine root;
si le cope au spatumile large, et soient en ta presence li cautere au feu.	cut it wide with a scalpel, and have the fire cautery ready at hand.
Car au taillier vient maintes fois trop grans decorremens de sanc, et se li sans te vaint, si te haste donques dou cauterizer;	For when cutting, there are often excessive blood flows, and if the blood overwhelms you, then quickly apply a cautery.
et se tu vois le malaide espoanteit et paourous de l’incision dou fer, si prent I fil de plonc bien fait, et en lie l’artelul si com nos avons dit, et le laisse II jors;	and if you see the patient frightened and fearful of the iron incision, then take a well-made linen thread and tie it around the artery as we have said, and leave it for two days;
et puis le restraint, et ne cesser d’estraindre lou fil de plonc tant qu’il cope l’artelul, et chiece par lui sens travail;	and then tighten it, and do not stop tightening the linen thread until it cuts through the artery, and each time with careful work;
et se les racines sont grosses, si a paour au coper meismement por le ventre, mais tu em pues bien coper la moitiet, puis le cauterize qu’il ne reviegne;	and if the roots are thick, be cautious when cutting to avoid harming the belly, but you can safely cut half of it, then apply a cautery so that it does not regrow;
puis cure la plaie, et garde que tu ne coper le thelul qui est de fuxe color et de povre sens et de lait regart.	Then treat the wound, and be careful not to cut the tendon which is of dark color and poor feeling and milk-white in appearance.
Car c’est uns apostemes enchancrez, et je venrai a la cure de chancre ci aprés.	For this is an embedded abscess, and I will come to the treatment of ulcers shortly thereafter.
quant li boude ist fuer	when the swelling subsides
Se li apparance de la boude vient par cautere de plaie ou de fendure de syfac, et est sus le ventre et en ist aucuns des bouez, si com il avient en autres routures, ou de sanc qui cort de voines ou d’arteres selonc ceu qui est devant, ou de ventositeit;	If the appearance of the swelling comes from a cautery wound or a tear on the surface, and it is on the abdomen and some of the bowels are exposed, as happens in other ruptures, or due to blood that seeps from veins or arteries according to what is before mentioned, or due to gas;
et se c’est par la routure dou syfac et par l’issue dou bouel, si est li color de l’aposteme semblans a la color dou cors, et est legiere chose sens dolor, et apert de diverse issue.	and if it is due to the rupture of the surface and the exit of the bowel, then the color of the abscess resembles the color of the skin, and it is a minor matter without pain, and evident from various exits.
Et se c’est por l’issue de l’intestine, adonques est il plus divers, et quant on le presse a ses dois si se repont, et puis revient, et par aventure si est sarrez, et agrandist mout a l’entree dou bain et por fort travail.	And if this is due to the opening of the intestine, then it is more varied, and when it is pressed at its sides it swells up, and then subsides, and perhaps it is hard, and greatly enlarges at the entrance of the bath and for heavy work.
Et se c’est por moistor, c’est legiere chose, et apert bien quant tu le presses a ta main, ne ne constraint mie;	And if it is due to moisture, it is a minor matter, and clearly visible when you press it with your hand, without any constraint;
et se c’est por sanc, si apert par ces signes li apostemes gros et dur, et est fichiez selonc une quantiteit;	And if it is due to blood, then by these signs, large and hard abscesses are recognized, and they form according to a certain quantity;
et se c’est por ventositeit, si est souef au tochier, et li ovraiges si est que tu regarde se li apparance est por le sanc de l’artere, ou de la voine, ou ventositeit.	And if it is due to windiness, then it is shallow upon touching, and the treatment is to observe whether the appearance is due to arterial blood, or from a vein, or windiness.
Si covient que tu laisses la cure.	It is necessary that you leave the treatment.
Car il en a doutance et paor, si com je t’ai dit ou chapistre des apostemes, por l’artere et por la voine.	For there is doubt and fear about it, as I told you in the chapter on abscesses, regarding the artery and the vein.
Et se li apparance est por l’intestine ou lou boueil, si covient que tu comandes au malaide qu’il teigne son alaine, et soit estendus tout drois, puis seigne d’enche tout entor la boude;	And if the appearance is due to the intestine or the bile, then you must instruct the patient to hold their breath, and lie completely straight, then bleed around the navel.
puis le comande a gesir sovin entre tes mains, puis va entor le leu que tu as signiet a tout le spatumile, puis estent la moitiet de l’aposteme au desus a tout le grant uncine;	Then instruct him to lie still between your hands, then go around the place you marked for the entire span of his wrist, then extend half of the abscess above to the full length of his thumb;
puis le lie entor d’un fil fort, ou d’une corde de fort soie fermement, et soit li nous dou liien assolz;	Then bind the area tightly with a strong thread or a rope of thick silk, and let the bandage be firmly applied.
puis oevre la moitiet de l’aposteme estendut sus le liien, et i boute ton doit indice, et quier l’intestine;	Then work on half of the abscess extended over the bandage, and place your index finger inside, seeking the intestine.
se tu le trueves pris dou liien, si le deslie, et boute l’intestine au defuer dou ventre;	if you find it caught in the bandage, then untie it and push the intestine out of the belly.
et se tu trueves le boueil, si le prent a l’oncine, et en cope la superfluiteit;	and if you find the bowel, grasp it with your hook and cut off the excess.
et se li artere te fait contraire, ou li voine, si vai belement entor, puis revien a ton ovraige et pren II aguilles, et i boute II fors filz, et boute les II aguilles entor ceu que tu as fait en crois que tu feis percier;	and if the artery or vein opposes you, proceed gently around it, then return to your work and take two needles, and insert two threads outside of what you have done in a cross shape to pierce.
puis estrain l’aposteme en IIII leus sus les aguilles, et se tu vues, oste les aguilles, et laisse lou leu tant qu’il porrisse, et chiece li char morte par soi;	Then incise the abscess in four places over the needles, and if you wish, remove the needles, and leave the wound until it becomes pus-filled, and the dead tissue will slough off on its own.
ou tu la cope quant elle iert subtiliie et porrie, puis le cure de ceu qu’il covient, et cheve l’aposteme si com nos avons dit;	When you incise it when it is subtle and pus-filled, then treat it as needed, and drain the abscess as we have said.
et estrai le sanc ou la moistor que tu trueves, puis cure le leu de ceu qu’il couvient, et soude le leu.	And extract the blood or moisture that you find, then treat the wound as needed, and close the wound.
dou chancre	of the ulcer
Nos avons dit en la division les semblances de chancre, et coment on i doit ovrer par medicines, et coment on doit eschuer la cure de fer;	We have discussed in the section the similarities of gangrene, and how it should be treated with medicine, and how one should avoid treating it with iron.
et disons le chancre enjanreit en la marris, et grant cautele a en la cure, et dirent li ancien que quant chancres est en leu ou on le puet raier si com chancre qui est em mameles, et en la cuixe, et en semblans leus, et le doit tout oster quant il est en l’encomencement;	And we say the ulcer spreads in the flesh, and great caution is needed in its cure, and the ancients said that when ulcers are in places where they can be scraped out as ulcers which are in the breasts, and on the thigh, and in similar places, and it should all be removed when it is at the beginning;
et quant il est grans et anciens, si ne covient mie que tu l’aproches, car je n’en poi onques nul saner;	and when it is large and old, then you should not approach it, for I have never seen anyone heal such a condition;
ne nulz n’en sana onques devant moi.	nor has anyone ever been healed before me.
Et li ovraiges, quant il est en leu ou on le puet oster, si com nos avons dit, est que tu purge aucune fois le malaide de cole noire;	And the treatment, when it is in a place where it can be removed, as we have said, is that you should occasionally purging the patient of black bile;
puis le fai sainier s’il ait manifeste repletion, puis afaite le malaide I boin leu por faire l’ovraige;	Then make it bleed if there is obvious congestion, then position the patient properly for the procedure;
puis giete tes oncines ou chancre, et le cheve de toutes pars, et l’oste de toutes pars sens rien laissier;	Then pour your ounces into the ulcer, and clean it from all parts, and remove everything without leaving anything behind;
et laisse corre le sanc tout fuer, et espreint bien le leu a ta main ou a aucune chose, et se li decorremens de sanc te fait contraire de l’incision de l’artere ou de la voine, si le cauterize tant que li sans soit estainchiez;	and let the blood flow freely until it stops, and press firmly on the area with your hand or something else, and if the continued bleeding prevents you from cutting into an artery or vein, then apply a cautery until the bleeding is stopped;
puis le cure d’autre cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	then continue to treat it until it is healed.
de ydropisie	of hydropsy
Nos avons jai dit en la division les semblances d’idropisie, et en queil maniere li assemblee de l’aigue est faite, et les signes de chescune semblance, et la cure qui est faite par medicines, et cele qui est curee par fer:	We have already discussed in the division the similarities of edema, and how the accumulation of fluid is formed, and the signs of each type, and the treatment that is done with medicine, and that which is treated with iron:
si est eclites soulement;	It is only contusions;
et ne doit on touchier de fer en ces II semblances:	and one should not treat with iron in these two cases:
c’est a savoir, tympanites et yposarche, car c’est mortelz chose;	that is to say, tympanitis and hypochondriac pain, for it is a fatal thing;
donques quant tu medicines ceste semblance de ydropisie qui est apelee «eclites» de medicines, et li cure ne profite, si regarde se li malaides est foibles, ou s’il ait autre maladie que ydropisie, si com toust et solution de ventre et semblans choses;	then when you treat this condition of hydrops which is called "ecclites" with medicines and the cure does not help, look to see if the patient is weak, or if he has another illness besides hydrops, such as coughing and intestinal discharge and similar things;
si n’i touchier de fer, car il i a doutance;	do not treat with iron, for there is doubt;
et se tu vois le malaide de fort vertut, et il n’a autre maladie que ydropisie soulement, et il n’est mie trop jones ne trop vielz, si dois ensi ovrer:	and if you see the patient is of strong constitution, and he has no other illness but hydrops only, and he is neither too young nor too old, then you should act thus:
lieve le malaide droit sus tes mains, et li ministres presse le ventre em boutant l’aigue a la plus basse partie dou pis, puis pren le spatumile espinous selonc ceste forme:	Lay the patient straight upon your hands, and the assistant presses the abdomen while inserting water into the lowest part of the bladder, then take the splatinum spiral in this form:
Et soit trenchans de II pars.	And let there be cuts from two sides.
a pointe, et toutevoie ne soit mie si entrans qu’il puist venir jusc’a l’intestine quant on le fiche ens, et ne le puist blecier;	point it, and ensure that it does not enter so deeply as to reach the intestine when inserted, nor can it be bent;
puis regarde se li ydropisie est enjanree devers les intestines:	then observe if the dropsy is located towards the intestines:
si covient que tu fendes ensus de la boude III dois droit desoz sus lou poignil;	if it is necessary, you should cut three fingers above the navel directly towards the groin;
et se li ydropisie est por la maladie dou foie, si soit ta fendure au senestre de la boude III dois;	and if the dropsy is due to liver disease, your incision should be three fingers to the left of the navel;
et se c’est por la miuce, si soit a destre, et ne covient mie que li malaides gise sus la fendure que les superfluitez ne corrent a celui foible leu;	and if it is for the middle, let it be to the right, and it must not be that the patient lies on the fissure so that the excesses do not run to that weak place;
puis perce tout le cuir a l’estrument, et le boute, et lieve ta main a tout le spatumile entre le cuir et le syfac ausi com en escorchant a la quantiteit d’une ungle ou enqui entor;	then pierce the entire skin with the instrument, and lift it up, and raise your hand to all the subcutaneous tissue between the skin and the muscle as when flaying, to the quantity of a fingernail or slightly around;
puis perce lou syfac tant que li spatumile viegne au leu vuit, et c’est li leus de l’aigue, puis le trai fuer, et i boute cest estrument de coi ci est li forme:	then pierce the muscle until the subcutaneous tissue reaches the empty place, and that is where the fluid is, then draw it out forcefully, and insert this instrument which has the following form:
Et est semblans a une caine d’argent subtil, et est d’arain ou d’archaut legier, et a en la partie desoz I petit pertus;	And it is similar to a thin silver chain, and it is made of light brass or reed, and at the end has a small hole.
et ou costeit d’une part, III pertus;	and when it is on one side, three perforations;
et II d’autre part, et I d’autre;	and two from the other side, and one from another;
et est li chiés tailliez si com une penne, et c’est li forme de l’incision dont li escrivains taille la penne:	and the head is cut like a feather, and this is the shape of the incision that writers make on a quill:
au chief desus est li alemele, si que quant li estrumens vient a l’aigue, si dessent maintenant sus l’estrument;	at the top is the blade, so that when the instrument reaches the tip, it now descends along the instrument;
vuide la donques la moitiet ou la tierce part, car se tu en vuides plus qu’il ne covient en celle houre, par aventure si muert li malaides por la resolution de son esperit de l’arme, ou il chiet paumez, ou il aproche a la mort;	empty then half or one-third of it, for if you empty more than is necessary at that time, by chance the patient may die from the shock of the weapon's effect on their spirit, or they fall weak, or approach death;
mais en vuide selonc la quantiteit de sa vertut, et selonc ceu que les dispositions de la vertut dou malaide signifient, et ses poulz;	but according to the emptiness according to the quantity of its strength, and according to what the disposition of the strength of the patient signifies, and his pulses;
puis trai l’estrument et retien l’aigue, et elle est retenue maintenant por le keur qui estoupe le pertus qui est sus le syfac, de coi j’ai parleit, que tu perces selonc ceste maniere;	then draw the instrument and retain the fluid, and it is now retained for the heart that stops up the passage above the liver, of which I have spoken, that you pierce according to this manner;
puis rencomence l’estrument l’autre jor, se tu vois le malaide soffrant ceu, et trai de l’aigue une petite quantiteit;	then restart the instrument on the other day if you see that the patient is suffering from this, and draw off a small amount of fluid;
fai ce aucun jor, et te garde de foloier tant qu’il ni demore mais c’un poc d’aigue.	do this on certain days, and be careful not to overdo it so that there remains only a little bit of fluid.
Et se tu doutes sus le malaide, et tu i lais mout d’aigue, si le cure de la sepulture ou sablon chaut, et par mout sueir ou bain et au soleil, et se teigne de boivre;	And if you doubt about the patient, and you leave much fluid, then treat with the grave or hot sand, and by much sweating or bathing and in the sun, and let them drink.
et le cure de medicines desiccatives tant qu’il soit sanez, et cauterize sus l’estomac et sus lou foie et sus l’esplen aprés l’estraction de l’aigue, si com j’ai dit devant.	and treat with drying medicines until he is healthy, and cauterize on the stomach and on the liver and on the spleen after the extraction of fluid, as I said before.
de l’estopement de la verge	about the numbness of the penis
Aucune fois naissent enfant qui n’ont point de pertus en la verge, ou li pertus est petis, ou il n’est mie en son leu.	Sometimes children are born without an opening in the penis, or the opening is small, or it is not in its proper place.
Si le covient tantost qu’il n’aist percier a tout I spatumile molt subtil selonc ceste forme:	It is necessary to pierce it immediately throughout the spatumile very finely according to this form:
puis met ou pertus I clo subtil de plonc, et le lie et le tien ensi III jors ou IIII et quant il vuet faire urine, si soit ostez li clos, et faice urine, et puis li remet;	then place a fine cloth plug in the opening, and tie it securely for three days or four, and when he wants to urinate, remove the plug, let him urinate, and then replace it.
et par aventure nen i couvient point, car li urine qui vient fuer ne lou laisse close.	and perhaps it is not necessary, for the urine that comes forth does not leave it closed.
Cil de cui li pertus est petis, si est medicinez dou clo de plonc, si com nos avons dit, si s’eslargera.	He whose orifice is small should be treated with a cloth plug of flax, as we have said, and it will enlarge.
Cil qui n’ont mie le pertus en lor leu sont bleciet, car aucun naissent qui ont le pertus au chief de la verge, por coi il ne puient pissier avant s’il ne lievent lor verge en haut;	Those who do not have the passage in its place are afflicted, for some are born with the passage at the head of the penis, so they cannot urinate unless they raise their penis upwards;
et ne pueent enjanrer por ceu que li matiere ne puet venir jusc’a la marris, et c’est une male maladie.	and they cannot urinate because the matter cannot reach the bladder, and this is a serious illness.
Et li maniere de l’ovraige si est que li malaides gise sovin sus son dos, puies estent le chief de la verge et le cope ausi com la taille d’une penne, si ke li pertus chiece em mileu, si com il covient;	And the method of the procedure is that the patient lies supine on his back, then stretches the head of the penis and cuts it as thick as a quill, so that the passage sits squarely in the middle, as it should;
et te garde de decorrement de sanc qui i vient maintes fois, et s’il avient, si l’estainche de ceu qui estainche sanc, et cure la plaie tant qu’il soit sanez.	and be careful of blood loss which often occurs, and if it happens, stop the bleeding as one would for stopping blood, and treat the wound until it is healed.
des pustules de la verge	pustules of the penis
Maintes fois vienent cist albathe en la verge, et est une apparance de char laide;	Often this ailment comes to the shaft, and it is an ugly appearance of flesh;
et en i a malignes et non malignes;	and there are both malignant and non-malignant ones;
si covient que tu les preignes a I oncine subtil, et les cope et munde toutes, puis met sus coton moilliet en oignement egiptien;	it is necessary that you remove them with a fine needle, and clean and treat all of them, then apply cotton soaked in Egyptian ointment;
puis le cure d’oignement diafinicon tant qu’il soit sanez.	then cure it with Diafinicon ointment until it is healed.
Et se li albathe est maligne, de pute color et depuant, si covient que tu i amenistres cautere.	And if the ulcer is malignant, of foul color and spreading, then you must apply a cautery to it.
Quant tu l’as copeit, et se li albathe est en som la verge, et en ait partie dedens la peil et partie defuer, si covient que tu oste l’albathe qui est dedens premier;	When you have cleaned it, and if the ailment is in the shaft of the penis, and part of it is inside the skin and part outside, then you must remove the part that is inside first;
et quant il est soudez, si le cure defuer.	and when it is sealed, then treat it to open.
Car quant tu le cures ensamble, si n’est mie asseurez li chiez de la verge qu’il ne soit perciez, et vient noiror et corruption en son la verge et ou coion;	For when you treat it together, the head of the penis is not assured that it will not be pierced, and blackness and corruption come to the penis and the testicles;
si covient chever tout ceu qui est noir et corrumput, puis lie sus l’emplaustre de miel et de farine qui soit fait d’escorce de poumes grenates et de veces, puis le cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	it is necessary to remove all that is black and corrupted, then apply a plaster made of pomegranate peel and vinegar, then treat it with other treatments until it is healthy.
Et se decorremens de sanc vient, si amenistre le cautere lunaire selonc ceste forme:	And if bleeding occurs, then treat with the lunar cautery according to this form:
Li cauteres si aide as II dispositions ensamble:	The cauterization helps with both conditions at once:
c’est asavoir, au decorrement de sanc, et a la corruption;	that is to say, in the flow of blood, and in corruption;
et se li chiés de la verge est corrumpus et retrais, si covient que tu boutes ou conduit de la verge une cainne de plonc, et pisse li malaides parmi;	And if the head of the penis is corrupted and withdrawn, it is necessary to insert a tube of lead into its channel, and the patient urinates through it;
et quant li pelz iert aerse au chief de la verge qui avient a ces qui n’ont mie esteit circoncis, ou il avient por plaie ou por aposteme, si covient donques que tu l’escorches a I estrument cheveit, tant que li liiens soit desliiez, et soit delivrez li chiez de la verge de toutes pars;	And when the skin is irritated at the head of the penis, which happens to those who have not been circumcised, whether it be due to a wound or an abscess, then you must burn it with a sharp instrument until the ligaments are loosened, and completely free the head of the penis from all sides;
et se c’est grief chose de deviser ceu, si covient que tu l’escorches a I spatumile aucun poc dou chief de la verge et de la peil;	And if it is difficult to describe this condition, then you must burn it with the spatula slightly at the head of the penis and around the skin;
puis dessevre belement entre II, et i met I subtil drapeil de lin moilliet an aigue froide, qu’il n’aerse derechief.	Then gently separate them, and place a fine damp strip of linen soaked in cold water between them, so that it does not irritate again.
de la circoncision	Of circumcision
Circoncision n’est mie desliemens de continuation si com les autres plaies;	Circumcision is not a disconnection of continuity as other wounds are.
toutevoie quant nos faison ceste oevre de nostre volenteit, et proprement as enfans, si est mestier que nos faisiens la millor oevre, et la plus legiere a salut.	Nevertheless, when we perform this work of our own will, and properly on children, it is necessary that we do the best work, and the lightest for their well-being.
Je dis que li ancien ne dirent mie la circoncision de lor enfans, car il n’en usent mie en lor loi, et n’en avons mais que ceu que nos avons aquis par experiment.	I say that the ancients did not speak of circumcision for their children, because they did not practice it in their law, and we only have what we have acquired through experience.
Car j’ai veut la plus grant partie des maistres et des sainors qui faisoient circumcision entor I dal, et as forces, et a tout une novacule;	For I have seen the majority of masters and seniors who performed circumcision around the time of St. Paul, and in many places, with a single incision;
si fuioit li keurs car il i a II toiles, et par aventure si cope on celi desus et demore celle desoz.	It is risky because there are two layers, and by chance one might cut through the upper layer while leaving the lower intact.
Or la recovient coper, et est li dolor double, et a la mundification qui est dou dal n’est mie asseuree li pointe dou membre;	Now there is the need to cut again, and the pain is doubled, and in the cleansing which follows St. Paul's method, the tip of the member is not securely protected;
et a la mundification de l’ungle par aventure eschaipe li fer, et corront l’uevre, et maintes fois naissent ensi qu’il n’ont mestier de mundification et je l’ai veut.	And in the cleaning of the nail, by chance the iron slips, and they run the work, and many times they are born such that they do not need cleaning and I have seen it.
De la mondification qui est faite as forces a tout le liien de fil ai je troveit la bonteit de l’experiment, car les forces taillent justement ausi bien desus com desoz.	Of the cleaning that is done with force to the entire length of the filament, I have found the goodness through experiment, for the force cuts precisely both above and below.
Car quant tu presses ta main, si tailles igalment en I tout soul tens;	For when you press your hand, cut evenly in one single motion;
mais que li filz soit bien estrois entor lou cuir;	but the thread should be tight against the skin;
et soit li maniere dou premier ovraige si est que tu faices penser l’enfant, s’il entent, que tu ne li fais fuer que liier le fil entor la verge tant soulement, et pues le fai esjoir en toutes les manieres que tu pues;	and the method of the first procedure is such that you make the child understand, if he understands, that you are not going to tie the thread around the penis solely for tying, but rather you can do it in all ways that you can;
puis le fai ester entre tes mains tout droit, et repont les forces entre tes mains ou desoz tes piez que li enfes ne les voie, ne aucun des estrumens;	then hold it straight between your hands, and apply the force between your hands or behind your feet where the child cannot see, nor any of the instruments;
puis boute ta main a la verge et souffle ou keur, et la trai en haut tant que li chiés de la verge soit ens;	Then place your hand on the shaft and blow at the joint, and pull it up until the head of the shaft is in place;
puis la mundifie bien de l’ordure qui i est assemblee, puis lie le leu signiet d’un fil double, puis la lie desoz I poc a I autre liien;	Then clean it well of the debris that has accumulated there, then tie the area with a doubled thread, then secure it from the pit to another knot;
et la tien as II dois par la seconde lieeure au pouchet et au doit indice, et cope entre les II liiens, puis lieve le keur desus hastanment et trai le chief de la verge;	and hold it with two hands at the second knot and at the thumb index, and cut between the two knots, then lift the joint quickly and pull the head of the shaft;
puis laisse corre le sanc poc et poc, car c’est li muedres;	then allow the blood to drip slowly drop by drop, for this is what happens in such cases;
et met poudre sus et sus la poudre I drapeil glueit d’un moieuf d’uef cuit destempreit d’aigue rose, confit avec oile roset boin et fres, et lou laisse sus jusc’a l’autre jor, et le cure d’autre cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	and apply powder and on top of the powder place a small cloth moistened with the yolk of a cooked egg mixed with rose water, seasoned with good and fresh oil, and leave it there until the next day, and treat it further as needed until it is healed.
Li forme des forces a la mundification si est ceste:	The form of the forces for the purification is thus:
li dui chiés soient tenves et soient trenchans, et soient li chiés ausi grant com li mainche igalment:	the two shoulders should be sharp and cutting, and the shoulders as large as the blade evenly:
li error de la mundification si est quant li keurs dedens fuit a l’incision;	the mistake in the purification is when the pus inside goes to the incision;
donques il covient que tu l’estendes a ton ungle, ainsois que li leus faice aposteme;	then it is necessary that you extend it to your fingernail, as if the flesh were forming an abscess;
et le cope igalment, et se tu ne lou pues tenir a ton ungle, si le tien as tenailles, et puis le cope.	and cut it evenly, and if you cannot hold it to your fingernail, then hold it with pliers, and then cut it.
Et s’il trespassent III jors, et ceu qui est desoz la verge est enflez, si le laisse tant que li apostemes chaus soit apaisiez, et l’escorche legierement;	And if they exceed three days, and that which is below the groin is swollen, let it be until the abscess is sufficiently reduced, and then gently scrape it;
si le cope si com tu pues mues, et te garde de la partie de la verge, ce ne li nuira niant.	Move the area as much as you can, and avoid the part of the shaft, so it will not harm him.
Cure donques le leu de choses soudans plaie de poudre, que nos avons dit ou traitier des poudres, et s’on cope dou keur outre mesure, et il va au desus, si ne nuira point;	Treat the area of sharp wounds with powder, as we have described in the chapter on powders, and if you move the heart too much, and it goes beyond what is necessary, it will do no harm;
cure le donques, si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez.	treat it as we have said until it is healed.
dou retenement de l’urine	from the retention of urine
Li retenue de l’urine si est d’opilation de piere, ou de sanc congeleit, ou de bowe, ou de char nee, ou de semblans choses, que nos avons dit en la division;	The retention of urine is due to the presence of stones, or clotted blood, or tumors, or dead tissue, or similar things, as we have said in the division.
et se li urine n’est desliie , et tu vois estre la retenue por la piere qui est jai ou col de la vessie, si covient que li malaides soit corbés sus ses genoulz;	and if the urine is not released, and you see that the retention is due to a stone that is stuck in the neck of the bladder, then it is necessary for the patient to be bent over their knees;
et li soient mis li piez sor le dos, et estende son ventre de la partie desus lou dos, et restraigne li malaides s’alainne tant com il puet;	and place the feet on the back, extend his abdomen above the part of the back, and restrain the patient's flanks as much as possible;
et adonques est constrains li colz de la vessie a l’expression de la piere au desus, por coi li urine est desliie e;	and then press the bladder to expel the stone upwards, thus freeing the urine;
et s’elle ne vient, si com nos avons dit, et li malaides sent grant dolor, si covient que tu i aministres extraction a tout l’estrument qui est apelez «siringue», de coi ci est li forme:	and if it does not come, as we have said, and the patient feels great pain, then you must administer extraction with all the instruments called "syringe," of which here is the form:
et soit d’argent subtilz legiere chevee, si com li penne d’un oiseil;	and let it be made of thin silver, like the feather of a bird;
et soit li caine d’une palme de lonc et demie, et soit subtilz au chief.	and let the tube be one and a half palms long, and thin at the tip.
Et li maniere de l’issue de l’urine si est que tu pren I fil double, et lie au chief I poc de laine ou de couton, et boute le chief dou fil dedens la siringue;	And the method of urination output is that you take a doubled thread, tie one end to the head of a piece of wool or cotton, and put the other end of the thread inside the syringe;
et cope la superfluiteit de la lainne et le boute jusc’au chief de la siringue, puis oint la siringue d’oile ou de burre et d’aubin d’uef, et fai seoir le malaide sus I siege, et li arose la vessie et la verge d’oile moiste et d’oile d’olive et d’aigue tede;	and cut the excess wool and push it up to the head of the syringe, then grease the syringe with oil or butter and egg yolk, and have the patient sit on a chair, and anoint the bladder and penis with moist oil, olive oil, and vinegar;
puis met legierement la siringue en la verge, tant qu’elle viegne a la racine de la verge, puis double la verge desus devers la boude;	then gently insert the syringe into the penis until it reaches the base of the penis, then press the penis upwards towards the body;
puis boute la siringue avant jusc’a la vessie, et la sente li malaides venir jusc’a la chose vuide, et ceu n’est mie fait selonc cest ordre fuer que por ceu que li conduis ou elle vait est tors;	then push the syringe forward until it reaches the bladder, and feel when the patient senses that it has reached the empty space, and this is not done according to this order unless what guides its path is twisted;
puis estent le fil a tout la laine poc et poc, et li urine en suit la laine, puis l’estrai fuer, et fai corre l’urine;	Then stretch out the thread over all the wool bit by bit, and the urine follows the wool, then extract it forcefully, and let the urine flow.
et rencomence la siringue tant que li vessie soit vuidie, et soit aligiez li malaides.	and continue using the syringe until the bladder is empty, and ensure the patient is comfortable.
des maladies de la vessie	diseases of the bladder
Quant escorcheures ou sanc vient en la vessie, ou porriture i est assemblee, et tu i vues distiller aigues et medicines, si fai a tout l’estrument qui est apellé «clepsedre», et c’est li forme:	When blood or pus comes to the bladder and putrefaction gathers there, and you wish to introduce liquids and medicines, use all the instruments that are called "clepsydre," and this is their form:
Elle est close, et si a III pertus:	It is closed, and has three openings:
II d’une part, et I d’autre, si com tu vois;	Two on one side, and one on the other, as you can see;
et li leus chevez par coi li medicine cort soit telz qu’il estoupe bien la verge sens adition, si c’on em puisse traire la moistor, et bouter quant mestier est;	and the leather strap through which the medication cord passes should be such that it stops up the tube well without addition, so that one can draw out moisture and insert when necessary;
et quant tu vues giter tes medicines en la vessie, met le chief dou keusteur en la moistor, et trai au traiant qui est ens;	and when you want to administer your medications into the bladder, place the head of the catheter in the moisture, and pull out with the syringe that is inside;
si trairas la moistor au kesteur, et puis reboute fort le traiant ens;	So you will draw the moisture to the chest area, and then firmly set it by pulling it in;
si entrera li moistors ens, et venra a la vessie maintenant, si que li malaides la sentira;	The moisture will enter inside and reach the bladder now, so that the patient can feel it;
et c’est li forme dou clistere subtil dont on clisterize la vessie:	and this is the form of the subtle enema with which one enemas the bladder:
si est ci:	this is as follows:
Et est d’argent ou d’archaut, et est li chiés plus haut;	It is of silver or rush, and the head is higher;
et desoz a I sein ou li liiens chiet;	and direct it to the side where the ligament falls;
puis pren une vessie de mouton et i met la moistor dont tu vues clisterizer la vessie, puis la lie entre les II seins forment d’un boin fil double, et chaufe I poc celle moistor sus le feu;	then take a bladder of sheep and put the moisture you wish to use for enema inside it, then tie it between the two breasts tightly with a good strong thread, and heat the container of this moisture over the fire;
puis boute le chief dou clistere en la verge, puis estrain ta main sus la vessie a tout la moistor avenanment, tant que li malaides sente que celle moistor est jai venue a la vessie;	Then insert the head of the enema into the penis, then press your hand above the bladder gradually to bring all the moisture up, until the patient feels that the moisture has reached the bladder;
et se tu n’as la vessie, si pren une piece de parchemin, et en fai I cercle, et le perce rondement entor;	and if you do not have access to the bladder, take a piece of parchment, make a circle out of it, and pierce it roundly around;
puis boute I fil fort en ces pertus, puis assemble le cercle si com on assemble I dal, et met dedens ceu que tu vues d’oile et de moistor et d’aigue, et le lie en l’estrument;	then insert a strong thread into these holes, then attach the circle as one would a sieve, and place inside it what you wish of oil and moisture and water, and secure it to the instrument;
et fai si com tu as fait de la vessie, de presser a ta main tant que li moistor veigne a la vessie.	and do as you did with the bladder, pressing with your hand until the moisture reaches the bladder.
de la piere	of the stone
Nos avons jai dit en la division les manieres de piere, et l’estraction ensamble medicines;	We have already discussed in the section the ways of stones and their extraction along with medicines;
et ai dit la difference entre la piere enjanree as rains, et toz les signes, et en queil piere on doit ovrer de taille;	and I have explained the difference between stones formed in the kidneys, and all the signs, and which stones one should treat with cutting;
et en la vessie, et en la verge;	and in the bladder, and in the penis;
et je le vos dirai apertement et briément.	and I will tell you clearly and briefly.
Je dis que li piere qui est enjanree en la vessie si avient plus sovent as enfans, et c’est signe que li aigue saut de la vessie semblans a aigue en sa subtiliteit;	I say that the stone which is formed in the bladder occurs more often in children, and this is a sign that the urine jumps from the bladder similar to how it does in its subtlety;
et i apert harene, et graite li malaides sa verge, et li pent maintes fois, et puis enroidist;	and there is an obvious urge, and the patient itches his penis, and does so many times, and then becomes stiff;
et a mout de ces saut li fondemens;	and in many cases the foundations;
et est legiere li sanation des enfans jusqu’il ont IIII ans, et est mout grief en viellars, et est as jones moiene, a ces qui sont entre jonesce et viellece;	and the healing of children is easy until they are four years old, and it is very difficult in the elderly, and for young adults it is moderate, for those who are between youth and old age;
et est li cure plus legiere de ces qui ont la piere grans, que de ces qui l’ont petite.	and the treatment is easier for those who have large stones than for those who have small ones.
Et quant nos venons a la cure, si couvient premier mundifier le malaide per clistere, por traire tout le fiens qui est as intestines.	And when we come to the treatment, it is necessary first to cleanse the patient with an enema, to draw out all the feces that are in the intestines.
Car il encombre aucune fois a querir la piere.	For it sometimes hinders in finding the stone.
Puis prenez le malaide par les piez, et lou deboutez et movez au desoz, si que li piere dessende au parfont de la vessie, et saille aucune fois dou leu haut;	Then take the patient by the feet, and lift him up and move him backward, so that the stone descends to the bottom of the bladder, and sometimes it comes from a higher place;
puis le fai seoir entre tes mains appareilliet, et ses mains soient desoz ses cuisses, si que li vessie soit toute declinans aval;	then make him sit between your hands which are prepared behind his thighs, so that the bladder is completely tilted downward;
puis la quier et la touche dedens;	then feel and touch inside;
se tu sens la piere en l’espaice, si te haste maintenant de taillier sus la piere.	if you feel the stone in the space, then hurry now to cut into the stone.
Et s’elle ne chiet au touchier dou tout, si moille ton doi indice d’oile de la main senestre, se li malaides est enfes, ou ton doi moien, se li malaides est jovencelz acomplis;	And if it does not fall out on touching with the entire finger, then moisten your index finger with oil from your left hand, if the patient is a woman, or your middle finger, if the patient is an adult male;
et le boute en son fondement, et quier la piere, et quant tu la sens a ton doi, si l’amoine au col de la vessie;	and insert it into its base, and feel for the stone, and when you sense it with your finger, gently push it towards the bladder neck;
puis presse sus a ton doi, et la boute au defuer lai ou tu vues taillier.	then press with your finger, and push it out where you intend to make the incision.
Et comande au ministre qu’il presse la vessie a sa main, et li comande qu’il estende a sa main destre les coions en haut, et a sa main senestre oste le cuir qui est desoz les coions en la partie ou on fait la taille;	And instruct the minister to press the bladder with his hand, and tell him to extend his right hand towards the genitals upwards, and with his left hand remove the skin that is underneath the genitals in the part where one makes the cut;
puis i boute le spatumile copant, de coi ce est li forme:	then place the scalpel, which is its form:
Et fent entre ceu qui est entre les coions et le fondement, ne mie em mileu mais au costeit de la naige senestre;	And make an incision between the genitals and the anus, not in the middle but towards the left side of the navel;
et soit drois sus la piere, et tes dois soit adés ou fondement, et soit li taille dou traver si qu’ele soit large par defuer, et dedens estroite, selonc la quantiteit de la piere, ne mie trop grans;	and let it be straight over the stone, and your two hands should immediately be at the anus, and the cut should traverse so that it is wide at the beginning, and inside narrow, according to the size of the stone, not too large;
par aventure la presse si li dois qui est ou fondement, qu’elle saut fuer sens travail;	by chance the pressure is so strong at its base that it springs forth without effort;
et saiches qu’il i a teil piere ou il a angles, et marges:	and you should know there are such stones with corners and edges:
si est griés a issir;	it is difficult to remove;
et si a teil qui est souez, semblans a une glant, et reonde, dont li issue est legiere.	and there are some that are smooth, like a rosehip, and round, from which the removal is easy.
A celi donques ou il a angles et marge, fai la taille plus grant;	For those that have corners and edges, make the incision larger;
et s’elle ne saut, si covient que tu estraignes sus as tenailles qui sont ausi com une lime au chief, por mues estraindre la piere si qu’elle n’eschaipe;	and if it does not spring forth, then you must clamp it with forceps that are like a file at the tip, to firmly grip the stone so it does not slip;
ou tu boute desoz li I estrument subtil corbé au chief;	When you place behind the eye a subtle curved instrument;
et se tu ne la pues engignier ensi, si eslarge I poc lou pertus, et se li sans decort, si l’estrainche de vitriole;	and if you cannot do it thus, then enlarge the socket and if blood leaks out, then constrict with vitriol;
et s’il i a plus d’une piere, si boute premier la plus grant au col de la vessie, puis cope sus, puis le trai fuer, et les petites aprés s’il en i a plusors.	and if there is more than one stone, then place the larger one into the bladder neck first, then cut above it, and extract it forcefully, and the smaller ones afterward if there are any.
Et s’elle est mout grans, si la covient soier, et faire plus grant plaie.	And if it is very large, then you must observe it carefully and make a larger incision.
Car II choses avienent au malaide:	For two things happen to the patient:
ou il muert, ou li urine vient adés par lai que li leus ne puet souder;	either he dies, or the urine comes out immediately so that the wound cannot close;
mais toutevoie t’efforce dou traire, ou dou debrisier as tenailles, tant que tu la traies par pieces;	but still strive to extract it, or disintegrate with pliers, until you remove it in pieces;
et quant tu as acomplit ton oevre, si emple la plaie d’encens et d’aloe et de sanc de dragon, et l’estraint, et met par sus I drapeil moilliet en oile et en vin, ou en oile et en aigue rose et aigue froide, por apaisier l’aposteme chaut;	and when you have completed your work, then apply the wound with incense and aloes and dragon's blood, and compress it, and place over it a moist cloth in oil and wine, or in oil and rose water and cold water, to soothe the hot abscess;
puis resovine le malaide sus son col, et ne desliier lou lien jusc’au tier jor.	then lift the patient onto their neck, and do not loosen the bandage until the third day.
Et quant tu le desliies, si arose mout bien lou leu d’oile et d’aigue, puis le cure d’oignement dyafinicon et d’oignement basilicon, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And when you dislocate it, wash the area very well with oil and water, then treat it with diafinicon ointment and basilicon ointment until it is healed.
Et se apostemes chaus vient en la plaie et corrosions, et congelemens de sanc en la vessie, et soit par ceu retenue li urine, qui est conue en teil maniere que sans saut avec l’urine:	And if hot abscesses and corrosion come to the wound, and clots of blood in the bladder, and because of this the urine is retained, which is recognized in such a manner that without straining with the urine:
boutes donques ton doi en la plaie, et estrai celui sanc, car s’il i remaint, si corront la vessie, et la porrit;	then put your finger in the wound, and extract that blood, for if it remains there, it will corrupt the bladder, and cause harm.
puis leve la plaie d’aigue et d’aisil et de seil, et li aide en toutes les manieres que tu seis, tant qu’il soit sanez;	Then lift the wound of water and urine and pus, and help it in all ways that you know, until it is healed;
et covient que toutes les oures que tu le cures, que tu li lie les II cuisses, et assemble les medicines sus le leu.	And it is necessary that every time you treat it, you bind the two thighs together, and apply the medicines to the site.
Et se li piere est petite, et ele est ou conduit de la verge, et fichie ens, et li urine ne puet issir;	And if the stone is small and it is in the channel of the penis, stuck inside, and the urine cannot exit;
si le cure de ceu que je dis ainsois, que tu lou tailles maintes fois, est on escusez de la taille per ceste cure.	then treat it as I say thus, that you cut it many times, and the cutting is forgiven by this treatment.
Je ai ja ce proveit ensi.	I have already tested this in this way.
Pren I foret de fer selonc ceste forme et soit a III angles fichiees en I tison:	Take an iron fork according to this form and let it have three prongs fixed in one handle:
puis pren I fil et lou lie entor la verge desoz la piere, si qu’ele ne puist venir arrier en la vessie;	Then take some thread and tie it around the penis below the stone, so that it cannot move back into the bladder;
puis boute le foret en la verge legierement, tant qu’il viegne a la piere;	Then gently insert the probe into the shaft until it reaches the stone;
et torne le foret a ta main en la piere poc et poc, tant que tu puisses percier la piere d’autre part;	and turn the probe in your hand within the stone bit by bit until you can pierce the stone from another direction;
si venra tantost li urine, puis presse ta main sus ceu qui est demorez de la piere qui est dedens la verge.	the urine will come soon, then press your hand on what remains of the stone that is inside the shaft.
Si est tantost brisie, et saut fuer avec l’urine, et est garis li malaides;	If it is broken immediately, and the stone passes with the urine, then the patient is cured;
et se tu ne pues ce faire por aucune chose qui le deffent, si lie I fil desoz la piere et I autre desus, puis fent la verge endroit la piere entre les II liiens, puis l’estrai fuer, et deslie lou liien, et mundifie lou sanc congeleit qui est en la plaie;	and if you cannot do this for any reason that prevents it, tie a thread below the stone and another above it, then cut the shaft directly over the stone between the two ties, then extract the stone, undo the ties, and clean the clotted blood from the wound;
et le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	and treat until he is well.
de la piere des femmes	of women's stones
Poc avient que piere soit enjanree en femmes, et s’il avient aucune fois, si est li cure grief, et est deffendut por III choses:	It rarely happens that a stone is formed in women, and when it does occur, the treatment is difficult, and it is prohibited for three reasons:
l’une est que per aventure li femme est vierge;	one reason is that perhaps the woman is a virgin;
et li seconde est c’on ne puet trover femme bien saichant qui se descuevre as mires, meismement quant elle est caste.	and the second reason is that one cannot find a woman who is willing to reveal herself to doctors, especially when she is chaste.
Et li tierce maniere si est que par aventure on ne puet trover femme bien saichant en cest art de mains;	And the third reason is that perhaps one cannot find a woman who is skilled in this medical practice;
et li quarte maniere si est que li piere de la femme si est plus em parfont que li piere de l’ome, por coi il i couvient faire plus parfonde taille, et grant paour i a. Et se necessitez semont a ceu, si covient que tu preignes une mieresse bien sachant, et a poines la trueve on, et se tu n’en trueves, point si quier I caste mire subtil;	and the fourth reason is that the stone in a woman is harder in composition than the stone in a man, so it requires deeper incisions, and there is great risk. And if necessity demands this, then you must seek out an experienced midwife, and finding one is difficult, and if you cannot find one, do not desire even a chaste doctor.
et li presente une baile bien saige en la vie des femmes, ou une femme qui saiche une partie de l’art, et li comande qu’ele faice ceu que tu li comandes de l’inquisicion de la piere;	and present a wise woman in the lives of women, or a woman who knows part of the art, and command that she do what you command regarding the inquiry into the stone;
et regarde mout bien se li femme est vierge:	and carefully observe whether the woman is a virgin:
adonques li covient bouter son doit ou fondement et querir la piere;	then she must insert her finger into the fundament and search for the stone;
et s’ele la trueve, si la constraigne desoz son doit, et li recomande qu’elle boute son doit ou con la malaide, et quiere et presse sa main senestre sus la vessie forment.	and if she finds it, she should press it down with her finger, and advise her to insert her finger into the patient's vagina, and search and firmly press her left hand on the bladder.
S’elle la trueve, si covient qu’elle la mueve de greit en greit des l’entree de la vessie jusque desoz, tant qu’elle viegne a la racine de la cuisse;	If she finds it, she should gently move it from the entrance of the bladder down to below, until it reaches the root of the thigh;
puis cope sus la piere en la racine de la cuisse encontre le mileu dou con, lai ou il est mues apparilliet, et sent la piere en celle partie;	Then cut around the stone at the root of the thigh opposite the middle of the groin, where it moves, and feel for the stone in that area;
et ne mueve son doi desus la piere ou desoz, et soit li taille au premier petite;	and do not move his hand above the stone or below it, and let the waist be slightly bent at first;
puis boute lou rait en la taille, se tu sens la piere si acroi la plaie tant que li piere puisse issir fuer, et saiches que maintes manieres de pieres sont:	then insert the probe into the waist, if you feel the stone then enlarge the incision so that the stone can come out easily, and know that there are many types of stones:
c’est a savoir, petites et grans et aspres et souez, longes et reondes, et qui ont rains.	that is to say, small and large stones, rough and smooth, long and round, and those with edges.
si saiches les semblances por savoir l’issue.	know the signs to understand the outcome.
Et se li sans te vaint, si met au leu vitriole broiet, et li tien une houre tant que li sans soit estainchiez;	And if the flesh prevents you, then place ground vitriol at the site, and hold it there for an hour until the flesh is softened;
puis revien a ton ovraige, tant que li piere soit fuer, et aies des estrumens que je t’ai dit en l’estraction de la piere as homes por toi aidier en ton oevre;	Then return to your work until the stone is out, and have the instruments that I told you about for extracting stones from men to help in your work.
et se li sans te vaint, et c’est de l’artere qui est copee, si met la poudre sus le leu et l’estrain de tentes et de bendelz, et ne rencomencier plus ceu, et laisse la piere et ne la traire mie, que par aventure morroit li malaide;	And if the blood flows from there, and it is from the artery that has been cut, apply the powder to the area and bind with cloths and linen strips, and do not attempt this again, and leave the stone unextracted, for the patient might die.
puis cure la plaie.	Then treat the wound.
Et quant li chalor dou sanc est apaisie, et li leus porrist, si revien a ton ovraige, tant que li piere soit fuer.	And when the heat of the blood is calmed, and the swelling subsides, then return to your work, until the stone is expelled.
de hernie carnouse	of flesh hernia
Ramice aquouse n’est autre chose que assemblee de moistor ou blanc syfac, qui est desoz lou keur des coions, que contient l’uef;	Aquous humor is nothing other than a collection of moisture or white substance, which comes from the testicles, contained within the egg.
et est apelez «syfac», et aucune fois est proprement en la toile de l’uef, si c’on cuide que ce soit I autre oef;	and it is called "syfac", and sometimes it is properly on the membrane of the eye, so one thinks that it is another eye;
et c’est li cuir dou coion entre lou blanc syfac que nos avons dit;	and this is the skin of the cornea between the white syfac that we have mentioned;
et ceu n’avient se poc non.	and this happens only if there is pus present.
Et li generation de cest ramice si est de foibleteit que vient as coions, et est espandue celle matiere.	And the generation of this aqueous retention is due to weakness that affects the bladder, and this material spreads out.
Et aucune fois si vient de percussion sus les coions, et ceste moistor si a maintes colors:	And sometimes it comes from striking the eyes, and this moisture can have many colors:
ou c’est color declinans a jaunice, ou c’est sans rouge, ou noir, ou aquous blans, et ce avient plus;	where it is a color declining to yellow, or without redness, or black, or clear white, and this happens more frequently;
et ce sont li signe de conoistre ceste assemblee, car s’elle est ou blanc syfac que nos avons dit, si est li apostemes reons, I poc lonc si com li figure d’un oef, et n’apert mie li coions, car il a moistor tout entor.	and these are the signs to recognize this condition, for if it is in the white membrane that we have mentioned, then there are small abscesses, with pus long as the figure of an eye, and does not affect the eyes themselves, because there is moisture all around.
Et s’il a moistor en la propre toile, si est li apostemes reons avec une partie de l’uef, et por ceu pense on que c’est uns autres oef;	And if there is moisture in the proper tissue, the abscesses are accompanied by part of an egg, and because of this, it is thought to be another kind of egg;
et se li moistor est entre le cuir des coions et le blanc syfac, si le sent om bien;	and if the moisture is between the skin of the scrotum and the white membrane, one can feel it well;
donques quant tu vues savoir la color de la moistor, si esprueve a tout l’intromissoire quarreit, de coi li forme est ci devant.	then when you wish to know the color of the moisture, test it throughout the entire area, as its form has been described above.
Selonc ceu donques qui vient aprés l’intromissoire, juge de ceu qui est dedens.	According to what follows the introduction, judge what is within.
Et quant nos la curons par fer, si covient que li malaides soit sainiez selonc som pooir et la repletion de son cors;	And when we treat it with iron, the patient should be bled according to his strength and the condition of his body;
puis le sovine sus son dos, sus une chose un poc haute, et met desoz lui mout de drapelz;	then place him on his back on something slightly raised, and put many cloths under him;
puis sié sus sa senestre, et comande au ministre qu’il sié a destre, et estende la verge a l’un des II costelz dou keur des coions;	Then sit on his left side, and instruct the assistant to sit on the right, and extend the rod to one of the two ribs below the heart.
puis pren le spatumile leit, et cope le cuir des coions parmi leu dou lonc jusque delez lou poignil, et soit ta fendure toute droite en devisant le cuir des coions jusc’a syfac blanc, et l’escorche subtilment selonc tom pooir;	Then take the scalpel and cut through the skin from the middle to where it is long, right up to the base of the thigh, and make your incision perfectly straight while carefully cutting the skin until you reach the white fat layer.
puis perce lou syfac plain d’aigue a I large pertus, et estrai toute l’aigue, et puis met tes oncines, et estent lou syfac amont;	Then pierce the white fat layer full of fluid with a wide incision, and drain all the fluid out, and then apply your forceps, and stretch the white fat layer upwards.
et ne touchier le keur des coions, mais que le syfac soulement;	and do not touch the heart of the groin, but only the white fat layer.
cope tout ou par pieces meismement le costeit de lui subtil, que se tu ne le copes bien saigement, si revenra li aigue;	Cut through entirely or piece by piece carefully, so that if you do not cut it thoroughly wisely, the fluid will return.
et se l’uef saut fuer a ton oevre, si le ramoinne en son leu quant tu avras acomplit l’uevre dou syfac;	and if the eye jumps during your work, then reset it in its place once you have completed the work of the operation.
puis assemble les II leivres dou keur des coions a une costure, puis le cure si com les autres plaies, tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then sew the two halves of the buttocks together with one seam, then treat it like other wounds until it is healed.
Et se tu trueves l’uef corromput d’autre maladie, si covient que tu lies les vasselz que sont suspensoire, en doutant le decorrement de sanc;	And if you find the eye corrupted by another illness, then it is necessary to tie the vessels that are suspensory, fearing the loss of blood.
puis cope le coion a tout le suspensoire, et estrai l’uef, et le cure si com nos avons dit.	Then cut the area around the eye along the suspensory part, and remove the eye, and treat it as we have said.
Et se aigue est assemblee en II parties ensamble, saiches que ce sont II ramices;	And if heat is gathered in two parts together, know that these are two branches;
si cope l’autre partie si com tu as fait la premiere igalment, puis essue lou sanc, et met en la plaie lainne moillie en oile roset;	if you cut the other part as you did the first equally, then wipe the blood, and place in the wound linen soaked in rose oil;
et met defuer autre laine moillie en vin et en oile, et met sus les II coions, et met desus drapelz doublés, et le lie sus a tout le liien qui est selonc ceste forme:	and place another piece of linen soaked in wine and oil, and put on the two sides, and cover with doubled cloths, and tie it up according to this form:
Puis pren II drapelz, et les emple de laine charpie selonc ceste semblance et soient assemblez par cousture en la gorle des braies, et li uns des chiés preigne sus le fondement jusc’au dos, et li autres a la partie dou poignil;	Then take two cloths, and wrap them with linen strips according to this appearance and join them by stitches at the waist of the trousers, one extending from the buttocks to the back, and the other to the side part;
et li autre dui chief sus les II angres, et soit toute assemblee li restreinture en la boucle dou braier;	and the other two heads on the two sides, and let the entire ligature be secured in the ring of the bandage;
et aucune fois est medicinee ceste ramice de cautere en leu de taille de fer, et est que tu preignes I cautere cultellaire subtil, et cope le cuir des coions, et soit eschaufez si com nos avons dit, si que li syfac blanc que contient l’aigue est descovers;	and sometimes this part is treated with a cautery instead of an iron cut, and you should take a fine knife-shaped cautery, cut the skin on both sides, and heat it as we have said, so that the white surface containing the fluid is exposed;
si pren lou cautere selonc ceste forme, et perce celui syfac as oncines, et l’escorche a cest subtil cautere chaut:	take the cautery in this shape, and pierce that surface with tongs, and scrape it with this fine hot cautery:
Et lou cope en toutes les manieres que tu pues, tant que tu esraiches tout;	And cut in all the ways you can, until you scrape it clean;
et garde que li feus ne touche l’uef;	and be careful that the fire does not touch the egg;
et saiches que ceste oevre est plus salve;	and know that this work is more safe;
et mues gardans de decorrement de sanc, et muedres que li ovraiges de taille;	and move while preventing blood loss, and proceed with the work of surgery;
et se nulle chose te fait contraire, ou aposteme chaus ou decorremens de sanc ou autre chose, si cure ce qui te fait contraire, selonc ceu qui est devant dit.	and if anything opposes you, whether an abscess, blood loss, or something else, then treat what opposes you according to what has been said before.
Et se li malaides est paourous, et ne vuet atendre cest ovraige por son horribleteit, si amenistre perforation, si com je te di, et est que quant tu es bien certains par les significations que nos avons dit que ramice aquouse est lai, si fai seoir le malaide sus I siege leveit;	And if the patient is fearful and does not wish to endure this work because of its horror, then perform perforation as I tell you, and it is that when you are certain by the signs we have said that watery pus is there, make the patient sit on a raised seat;
pues perce l’aposteme an la partie desoz a tout le spatumile large, et met la perforation dou lonc dou cors;	then pierce the abscess on the underside across the entire span of the body, and place the incision along the length of the body;
et soit larges li pertus, si que toute li aigue corre fuer;	and let the openings be wide so all the fluid runs out;
puis met coton sus le leu, et le lie, et laisse por corre le remenant de l’aigue, puis le cure tant que li plaie soit sanee;	then place cotton on the area, secure it, and leave it so that the remaining fluid can drain, then treat it until the wound is healed;
et se li blainche toile ne laisse issir l’aigue en la bouche de la plaie, si covient que tu i boutes une penne ou l’estrument dont on trait l’aigue des ydropiques, de coi li forme est ci devant;	and if the white cloth does not allow the fluid to drain from the wound opening, then you must insert a feather or the instrument used for treating the fluids of hydropics, as described above;
et eslarge I poc la plaie, et saiches que li aigue revient, et est assemblee aprés VI mois ou enqui entor, et quant elle est assemblee si com devant, et ensi passera li malaides ses jors.	and enlarge the pit of the wound, and check that the fluid returns, and it will heal after six months or thereabouts, and when it is healed as before, then the patient will live out their days.
de l’aposteme des coions	of the abscess of the testicles
Saiches que en la section de ceste ramice a paor em plusors dispositions, por coi il me semble que mues vaut c’on la laisse;	Know that in the section of this branch there is fear in many conditions, so it seems to me that one should leave it as it is;
et je vos dirai l’ovraige et les semblances de l’aposteme.	and I will tell you the work and similarities of the abscess.
Je dis donques que maint aposteme vienent ou cors, et meismement as coions;	I say then that many abscesses occur in the body, especially in the groin;
et c’est par mout de cas.	and this is due to many causes.
C’est a savoir par superfluiteit aigre et ague, qui est espandue as coions, ou de percussion;	This is known to be due to sharp and bitter excess, which spreads to the groin, or from impact;
et est li color de l’aposteme selonc la color dou cors;	and the color of the abscess is according to the color of the skin;
et ne trueve point de dolor, et est aposteme grief;	and finds no pain, and there is a severe abscess;
et par aventure est uns apostemes griés paourous et pierous, et de fuxe color, et aucune fois vient de nout d’artere, ou d’enfleure de voine.	and sometimes a severe abscess is fearful and stony, and of dusky color, and at times it comes from the blockage of an artery or swelling of a vein.
Quant c’est par nout d’artere, si est conus par la disposition d’aposteme chaut, quant tu la presses a tes dois;	When it is due to the blockage of an artery, it is known by the hot condition of the abscess when you press it with your fingers;
et ne covient mie que tu i touches.	and it is not appropriate for you to touch it.
Cil qui est fais d’enfleure de voine est conus par sa disposition a l’expression dou touchement des dois, et puet om bien faire la taille sus ceste semblance, et sus les autres chars;	One who is affected by the swelling of a vein is known by its condition and the expression upon feeling it with fingers, and one can properly treat this condition as well as others.
et est que tu cope lou keur des coions, puis estent l’uef en haut, et le trai fuer dou blanc syfac, et delivre lou suspensoire de toutes pars de l’uef.	And it is that you cut the cord of the testicles, then place the egg above, and draw out from the white membrane, and release the suspensory ligament from all parts of the egg.
Se li uef est ja sodez avec ces chars nees, si covient donques que tu traies l’uef, et lou cope;	If the egg is already hardened with these new membranes, then you must draw out the egg and cut it.
et s’il est aers au syfac, ou en ceu qui est dedens les vasselz, si covient que tu delivre toute celle tenve, et la cope reondement.	And if it is air in the membrane, or within what is inside the vessels, then you must release all of that space, and cut it completely.
Et se li naissance de la char est ou leu derrier, si covient que tu la copes toute, et estrai l’uef, si com nous avons dit.	And if the birth of the flesh is at the back, then it must be cut entirely, and remove the eye, as we have said.
Et quant tes ovraiges est acomplis, si emple la plaie de laine moillie en oile roset et en vin, puis le cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	And when your work is complete, apply the wound with moist wool in rose oil and wine, then treat it with other treatments until it is healed.
de l’aposteme des coions	of the abscess of the testicles
Cis est uns apostemes envoloupez d’un envoloupement semblant a I borjon, avec le mollifiement des coions, et se muet li malaides griement quant il vait;	This is an abscess wrapped in a covering similar to leather, with the softening of the testicles, and the patient moves very painfully when he walks;
et li cure de ceste maladie si est bien pres ausi paourouse com ceste ci devant, et toutevoie nos vos dirons l’ovraige de li, selonc ceu que li ancien firent.	And the treatment for this illness is also very dangerous as the previous one, and nevertheless we will tell you about it, according to what the ancients did.
Il covient que tu faices seoir lou malaide sus I siege aleveit, puis li boute le suspensoire des coions aval a tes dois, a tout le vasseil qui sont prochien a la verge, et les teigne li maistres, et les estende forment;	It is necessary that you seat the patient on a raised chair, then attach the suspensory from below to both hands, to all the vessels that are near the penis, and hold them tightly, and stretch them firmly;
puis cope au spatumile trenchant large dou traver endroit les vasselz, tant qu’il soient descovert, et puis escorche de chescune part, si com nos avons dit en l’estraction des arteres qui sont en temples;	then cut through the flat spatula with a wide and sharp blade across the vessels until they are exposed, and then peel them back on each side, as we have said in the extraction of arteries that are in the temples;
puis i fiche une aguille ou il ait I fil double, et le lie au premier leu ou li vis est venue, et le lie derechief a l’autre chief;	then insert a needle with doubled thread, and tie it at the first place where the vein is, and tie it again to the other end;
puis les cope em mileu droitement, selonc la longesce dou cors, et en trai les moistors corrumpues;	Then cut them straight down the middle, along the length of the body, and draw out the corrupted moisture;
puis cure la plaie si com les autres ou on enjanre bowe, si que aucun vassel chiecent que norrissent l’un des coions;	Then treat the wound as you would others where boules [blood clots or swellings] are raised, so that no vessel bleeds which nourishes one of the sides;
car par ceu n’i vient point de mal, et se a toz les vasselz vient vis, si covient traire les coions a tout les vasselz;	for by this no harm comes, and if it happens to all the vessels, then it is necessary to draw out the sides from all the vessels;
si que li oes ne perde son norrissement por l’incision des vasselz, et sechent et ne se puient aidier.	so that the eye does not lose its nourishment due to the cutting of the vessels, and dries up and cannot be helped.
de la routure dou syfac	of the fracture of the cheekbone
Li avenemens de ceste ramice si est par la section que vient ou syfac, ou l’estension sus le ventre en la partie des angres, por coi li intestine dessendent de celle routure a l’un des coions;	The occurrence of this condition is due to the section that comes from the syphac [a surgical procedure], or the extension on the abdomen in the part of the flanks, because the intestines descend from that rupture to one of the sides;
et ceste routure est ou dou syfac, ou de l’estension de li, et vienent ces II manieres de mout de causes:	and this rupture is either on the surface or from the extension of it, and these two manners come from many causes:
ou de percussion, ou de saut, ou de braire, ou de levement de grief faix, et par semblans choses;	or from impact, or from jumping, or from lifting heavy loads, and from similar things;
et li signes quant c’est de l’estension dou syfac, si est qu’il avient poc et poc, en lonc tens, et ne vient mie soudainnement;	and the signs when it is from the extension of the surface are that they occur gradually over time, and do not happen suddenly;
et est li apostemes igalz jusque vers le parfont, por ceu que li syfac apresse l’intestine.	and the abscesses are equal up to the depth, because the surface presses on the intestine.
Et li signes est quant c’est de la section dou syfac, qu’elle fait venir a l’encomencement dolor soudaine, et est li apostemes divers apparans, desoz le cuir pres, et c’est por l’issue de l’intestine et le cors au defuer dou syfac.	And the signs when it is a section of the cheekbone are that they cause sudden pain at the beginning, and the abscesses appear differently, near the skin, because of the exit of the intestines and the body's reaction to the absence of the cheekbone.
Et aucune fois dessent li cirbes avec l’intestine, et est retenus enqui, et fait grant dolor soffrir au malaide, meismement quant il est pressez.	And sometimes the intestines descend with the hernia, and are retained inside, causing great pain for the patient, especially when they are constricted.
Et en ces cures de fer a paor, por coi il s’en covient eschuir.	And in these iron treatments there is fear, because of which it is necessary to avoid them.
