Et li maniere de l’ovraige si est que tu comande ou malaide qu’il ramoine l’intestine a sa main au dedens en la plaie, s’il i puet rentreir;	And the method of treatment is that you instruct the patient to probe the intestine with his hand inside the wound, if it can be reached;
puis soit sovinez sus son col. entre tes mains, et lieve les cuixes;	Then bind him around his neck with your hands, and lift his thighs;
puis estent le keur au desus, et cope tout le cuir des coions dou lonc;	Then stretch the heart above, and cut all the skin of the genitals long;
puis boute dedens les leivres de la taille uncines selonc ceu que tu en as mestier por ovrir la plaie, et soit telz que li oes em puist issir;	Then insert hooks into the sides of the waist according to what you need to open the wound, and make them such that the eyes can come out;
puis escorche lou syfac que est desoz lou cuir des coions, tant que li blans syfac dur soit descovers de toutes pars;	Then peel off the skin that is below the genital skin until the white tough skin is uncovered from all sides;
puis boute ton doi indice en ceu qui enseut lou coion, en ceu qui est entre lou blanc syfac qui est desoz lou cuir de l’uef, et entre lou secont syfac, et depart ceu qui est derrier l’uef, et entre lou secont syfac;	Then insert your middle finger into the area below the genitals, between the white skin that is beneath the genital skin and the second layer of skin, and separate what is behind the penis, and between the second layer of skin;
et pues muef a la main destre dedens lou keur des coions, et estent lou blanc syfac en haut a ta main senestre, et lieve l’uef a tout lou syfac devers la taille;	and then move to the right hand inside the groin area, and stretch the white skin upwards with your left hand, and lift the egg across the entire surface towards the waist;
et comande au ministre qu’il estende l’uef en haut, et deslie ceu qui est aers derrier le liement;	and instruct the attendant to raise the egg upwards, and undo those who are tied behind the binding;
et quier a tes dois s’il a point de l’intestine envoloupeit ou blanc syfac dur, et se tu en trueves aucune chose, si le boute au ventre desoz;	and ask your two assistants if there is any intestine wrapped around the white skin, and if you find anything, push it back into the abdomen;
puis pren une aguille ou il ait I gros fil fait de X filz, et la boute en la derriere partie dou syfac, qui est aprés lou cuir des coions;	then take a needle with a thick thread made of several strands, and insert it into the rear part of the skin, which is behind the groin skin;
aprés la taille, puis cope les chiés qui apperent des filz, tant qu’il i ait IIII filz;	after the waist, then cut the threads that appear as strands until there are four strands;
puis les assemble l’un sus l’autre en maniere de croix, et en lie lou syfac, dont nos avons dit qui est desoz lou cuir des coions, d’un fort liien de II pars;	Then they arrange them one on top of the other in the manner of a cross, and bind the surface, which we have mentioned is beneath the skin of the genitals, with a strong ligature from two sides;
puis envoloupe les chiés des filz, et les lie forment de II pars, si que nuls des vasselz que les norrissent ne puissent entrer en ous, que aposteme chaus n’i viegne;	Then wrap the head with thread and bind it firmly from two sides so that none of the substances nourishing them can enter inside, preventing an abscess from forming;
et met derechief le liien selonc le premier liien lonc II dois de celui, et aprés ces II liiens laisse dou syfac qui est desoz lou keur des coions le grant d’un doi;	and place the ligature again according to the first ligature for two digits long, and after these two ligatures leave the surface that is beneath the skin of the genitals exposed for one digit;
et aprés tout l’autre selonc la rondesce que li euf porte;	and then wrap the rest according to the circumference that the egg carries;
puis cope en la partie qui est desoz le cuir des coions, tant qui li sans corre, et li bowe, si com nos avons dit ci devant;	Then cut in the part which is away from the skin of the thighs, until the blood flows, and the bowel, as we have said before;
puis amenistre laine moillie en oile, et met em plaies, et i amenistre le liien que nos avons dit.	Then apply moistened wool in oil to the wounds, and wrap it as we have said.
Et aucune fois est cauterizez li blans syfac que nos avons dit, aprés l’incision, par doutance de decorrement de sanc.	And sometimes the white membrane we have mentioned is cauterized after the incision, out of fear of blood leakage.
Car ce avient maintes fois, et laisse le liien tant qu’il chiece per lui;	For this often happens, and leave the bandage on until it falls off on its own;
et s’il tarde au cheoir, si soit arosez d’aigue chaude, et met sus ceu que nos avons dit, tant qu’il chiece;	and if it delays in falling off, soak it in warm water and put on what we have said until it falls off;
puis cure la plaie d’autre cure, tant qu’il soit sanez parfaitement.	then treat the wound with another method until it is completely healed.
de hernie carnouse	of flesh hernia
En ceste ramice ne vis je onques nul qui osast faire la cure par fer.	In this case, I have never seen anyone dare to treat it with iron.
Et li ancien dirent qu’ele est faite si com li ramice qui est ensamble la vis, en teil maniere que tu lie les vasselz, aprés la taille sus ous legierement au desoz;	And the ancients said that it is made like a vine shoot attached to the skin, in such a way that you bind the vessels above the waist lightly towards the back;
puis cope em mi, et cure l’aposteme de ceu qui oevre, tant que li vasselz chient;	Then cut it open, and treat the abscess of the one who is working, until the pus flows;
et le cure si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez.	and treat it as we have said, until it is healed.
Aucune fois vient routure ens angres, si com nos avons dit, et apert li leus;	Sometimes a rupture occurs in the groin, as we have said, and it is apparent;
et ne dessent nulz des intestines as coions, et s’il en i dessent, c’est poc, et repaire toutes houres;	and no part of the intestines descends into the scrotum, and if it does descend, it is serious, and repair must be done at all hours;
et toutevoie s’il demoure trop en cest point, si croit li plaie ou syphac, tant que li intestine dessent;	and if it remains too long in this state, the wound or sphincter will worsen, until the intestines descend;
et ceu avient par l’estension dou syfac qui est as angres, si com nos avons dit, car il est estendus, puis est mollifiez et enflez li leus et apert;	and this happens due to the extension of the sphincter in the groin, as we have said, because it is stretched, then becomes lax and swollen and apparent;
et li cure si est par cautere, si com nos avons devant dit;	and the treatment is by cautery, as we have said before;
et aucune fois est curee par fer en ceste maniere:	and sometimes it is treated with iron in this manner:
et est que li malaides gise sovin sus son dos entre tes mains, puis cope le leu de la routure enfleit dou large selonc la quantiteit de III dois;	and the patient lies supine on their back between your hands, then raise the area of the fracture swollen in width according to a measure of three fingers;
et puis estrai le syfac qui est desoz le cuir que l’ensuet, puis pren lou rait et lou met sor le leu apparant dou syfac;	and then extract the sinew which is beneath the skin as follows, then take the thread and place it on the apparent part of the sinew;
et lou presse au parfont dou ventre, puis cout les II leus apparans dou syfac sus lou chief dou rait, et cout l’un et l’autre;	and press it firmly to the abdomen, then stitch the two apparent parts of the sinew above the head of the thread, and stitch one and the other;
puis estrai le chief dou rait, et ne coper point dou syfac ne n’estendre l’uef n’autre chose, si com je t’ai fait savoir en la cure de la ramice des intestines;	Then extract the head of the shaft, and do not cut into the surface or extend the egg or anything else, as I have told you in the treatment of the root of the intestines;
puis le cure par la cure des plaies.	Then treat it with the treatment for wounds.
Et quant tu copes les filz, si le mundefie et cure la plaie, tant qu’elle soit sanee.	And when you cut the threads, then anesthetize and treat the wound until it is healed.
Li syfac est constrains, et n’a point d’apparance en la routure, et li cauteres est muedres en cest leu, et plus prochiens a salut.	The swelling is constrained, and there is no appearance in the rupture, and the cauterization is soft in this place, and closer to healing.
de l’amollissement dou cuir des coions	of the softening of the skin of the genitals
Maintes fois est amollis li cuirs des coions en aucuns homes, por ceu que les chars que sont dedens sont mollifiees, et est lait a veoir;	Many times the skin of the testicles becomes soft in some men, because the tissues inside are softened, and it appears milky.
et est mestier, quant on le vuet curer, c’on faice gesir lou malaide sus son dos, et li cope le cuir qui est mollifiez sus le cuir natureil;	and it is necessary, when one wishes to treat it, that the patient lie down on his back, and cut the soft skin over the natural skin;
puis assemble les II levres a une costure, et se tu vues, cout premier la superfluiteit dou cuir mollifiiez a III costures ou IIII fermement;	then sew the two lips together at one seam, and if you wish, suture the excess soft skin at three seams or four firmly;
puis cope entre les costures, et lou cure si com les autres plaies, tant qu’il soit sanez, et chient li fil.	Then cut between the stitches, and treat it as other wounds, until it is healed, and remove the thread.
dou chastrement	of the discipline
Saiches que chastremens est escomeniez en nostre loi, et por ceu il me plairoit que je n’en parlasse mie en cest livre;	Know that castration is condemned in our law, and for that reason I would prefer not to speak of it in this book;
et n’est necessaires fuer que por II manieres:	and it is necessary only for two reasons:
dont l’une est que li mires en saiche respondre quant on li demandera, et en saiche la cure;	one of which is that the priest knows how to respond when asked, and knows the treatment;
et li autre, por ceu que nos avons sovent mestier de chastrement d’aucunes bestes por nos aidier, si com de bouc et de mouton et de chait et d’autres bestes.	and the other, because we often need castration of certain animals to help us, such as goats and sheep and cats and other animals.
Je dis donques que chastremens est fais selonc II manieres:	I say then that castration is performed in two ways:
ou par atraction, ou par fendure.	By attraction, or by incision.
En celle que nos faisons par attraction, faisons nos seoir la beste en aigue chaude, tant que li coion soient mollifiez et pendant;	In the one we do by attraction, make the animal sit in hot water until the joint is softened and hanging.
puis les preing a ta main, tant qu’il soient remis et que tu ne les sentes plus.	then take them in your hand until they are reset and you no longer feel any discomfort.
Du chastrement de taille:	On castrating the calf:
covient que tu teignes la beste, et li presse le cuir des coions a ta main senestre, puis lie le suspensoire, et cope sus chescun oef a I cop, quant tu les avras bien escorchiez;	you should restrain the animal, and press the skin around the testicles with your left hand, then tie the suspensory ligament, and cut around each one in one stroke after you have sufficiently flayed them;
et i laisse aucun poc dou syfac et lou subtil syfac qui est sor les vasselz;	and leave some of the fatty tissue and the fine tissue that is on the vessels;
et ceste maniere de chastrement est muedre que cele qui est faite par attraction, por ceu que a l’atraction demoure par aventure aucune chose des coions, par coi li beste desire luxure;	and this method of castration is more brutal than that which is done by attraction, because with the attraction some part of the testicles may remain, causing the animal to desire lust;
puis cure la plaie tant qu’ele soit sanee.	then treat the wound until it is healed.
des hermofrodites	Regarding hermaphrodites
Hermofrodie est selonc II manieres as homes:	Hermaphroditism occurs in two ways among men:
l’une si est que entre les II coions apert ausi com li figure de la nature d’une femme, ou il ait poil, et aucunes fois en cort li urine.	one in which between the two testicles there is an opening as in the form of a woman's anatomy, where there may be hair, and sometimes it encircles the passage for urine.
Et li autre maniere si est en femmes, et ait sus lou poignil ausi com une verge et II coions.	And the other method is for women, and place on the navel as with a rod and two eggs.
Et li cure de l’ome et de la fame si est que tu copes les chars ajostees toutes, et les cure si com autres plaies;	And the treatment for both the male and female is that you should cut away all adjacent tissues, and treat them as other wounds;
en la seconde maniere, des homes dont li urine saut par lou cuir des coions, si n’a point de cure.	In the second manner, for those whose urine sprays along the skin of the genitals, there is no cure.
de la tentigene	of the examination
Tentigene est une chars ajostee sus la partie natureil, tant qu’elle est trop laide a veoir;	Tentigene is a condition attached to the natural part, so much so that it is too ugly to look at;
et aucunes femmes l’ont ausi grant com une main, et c’est li cure.	and some women have it as large as a hand, and that is the cure.
Il covient que tu teignes la superfluiteit de la tentigene a ta main ou as oncines, et la cope legierement;	It is necessary that you paint the excess of the tentigene on your hand with scissors, and then cover it lightly;
et n’aler mie trop em parfont, que decorremens de sanc n’i viegne, puis le cure d’autre cure tant qu’il soit sanez;	and do not go too deep, so that no blood comes out, then treat it with another treatment until it is healed;
et a une autre char que naist a la bouche de la marris, et l’emple, et par aventure saut fuer, et est selonc la semblance d’une kowe, et por ceu l’apelerent li ancien «maladie kowee».	and for another condition that appears at the entrance of the mouth and spreads, and sometimes becomes severe, it resembles a cow's condition, and therefore the ancients called it "cow sickness.
Si covient que tu la copes, si com nos avons dit la tentigene, et la cure tant qu’elle soit sanee.	It is necessary that you treat it as we have said about tension, and care for it until it is healed.
de erratique	erratic
Erratique si est quant li nature de la femme n’est mie percie, ou li pertus est petis;	Erratic is it when the nature of a woman's body is not understood, or the opening is small;
et est naturez par naissance, ou accidens par maladie que venue i est;	and it is natural from birth, or accidental due to illness that has come;
ou c’est par char ajostee, ou dou syfac subtil ou espés, et est fais em parfont en la marris, ou en costez, ou desoz, ou que soit;	or it is due to added flesh, or a thick or thin layer of fat, and it is formed properly in the belly, or on the sides, or inside, or wherever;
et deffent le concevoir, et l’enfantement, et par aventure les flors a avoir;	and it prevents conception and childbirth, and possibly the onset of menstruation;
et li connoissance de ceu si est par le regart de la baile.	and knowledge of these conditions is gained through examination of the body.
Se li estoupemens est prochiens apparans, si quier a tes dois ou au rait.	If constipation is close at hand, either use two fingers or the right [finger].
S’il est dou syfac subtil, et il est prochiens as II leivres, si te haste, et la ront ensi:	If it is due to thin fat, and it is close to the second books, hurry, and treat thus:
met tes II dois indices ensamble, et li femme soit sus son dos, espandues ses jambes;	Place your two thumbs together, and have the woman lie on her back with her legs spread.
puis estent les II leivres forment, tant que li subtilz syfac soit rons, et soit overs li estoupemens;	then press the two thighs firmly together until the fine substance [of semen] is gone, and it should be above the obstruction;
puis pren laine, et la moille en oile, et la met sus le leu, et gise li femme a home chescun jor, si qu’il ne puist souder.	then take wool, and mix it with oil, and place it on the area, and have the woman lie face down each day so that she cannot sit.
Et se li syfac est dur et espés, si covient que tu lou copes au spatumile semblant a foille de mirte.	And if the wound is hard and thick, then you should cut it with a scalpel resembling a myrtle leaf.
Se li estoupemens est de char nee, si la sospent a l’oncine et la cope;	If the obstruction is of flesh, then suspend it to the thumb and cut it off;
et aies les medicines estainchans sanc, si com acaice, sanc de dragon, encens, ensamble abun d’uef;	and have the blood-stanching medicines ready, such as vinegar, dragon's blood, incense, mixed with plenty of egg;
puis amenistre une caine de plonc large, si que li plaie ne puisse souder;	Then apply a bandage of cloth wide enough so that the wound cannot close.
et ensi soit longement, et li amenistre une tente de lin sec;	and keep it on for an extended period, and apply a dry linen bandage.
puis soit curez d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	then continue treating with other treatments until he is healed.
Et quant en la marris vient char nee, si la covient coper selonc ceste maniere, se ce n’est apostemes enchancrez.	And when flesh becomes diseased in a wound, it should be cut according to this method, except for embedded abscesses.
Car a l’aposteme enchancreit qui est en la marris, ne doit on touchier de feir.	For in the embedded abscess that is in the wound, one should not cut it open.
des emorroides	of hemorrhoids
Emorroydes sont overtures de voines dont sans cort acostumeement, et quant les emorroydes sont vielles si devienent thelul;	Hemorrhoids are openings of veins that without proper treatment become hard and painful.
et nos avons jai dit en la division les semblances d’aus, et les signes, et je dirai ci celles qui resoivent curation.	and I have already mentioned in the section the similarities of these conditions, and the signs, and here I will say those that respond to treatment.
Je di que les emorroides et li thelul, quant il sont em parfont en la marris, et il n’aperent au sentir, si n’est mie li cure par fer.	I say that when hemorrhoids and hard lumps are firmly fixed in the wound and do not yield to touch, they cannot be cured by cautery.
Cil qui sont a la bouche de la marris, c’on puet sentir, sont cil c’on puet curer.	Those who have the mouth of the ulcer, which can be felt, are those who can be treated by curettage.
Il covient donques que tu mettes la femme en une maison froide, puis estent l’altelul as tenailles, et le cope en ses racines, puis poudre sus medicines restraignans sanc, si com acaice et sanc de dragon et encens, et semblans choses;	Then you must place the woman in a cold room, then extract the tumor with pliers, and cut it at its roots, then apply powder made from medications that constrict blood, such as oak bark and dragon's blood and incense, and similar things;
puis boute ses piez a la paroit une houre, puis la met en aigue froide;	Then place his feet against the wall for an hour, then put them in cold water;
et se decorremens de sanc i vient, si la fai seoir en une decoction de sumac et d’escorce de pomes grenates et de gales et de semblans choses, et puis pren farine d’orge, et la confis avec miel et aisil, et en fai I emplaustre sus son dos.	and if bleeding occurs, have him sit in a decoction of sumac and pomegranate rind and gall and similar things, and then take oatmeal, mix it with honey and oil, and make a poultice for his back.
Et se il estainche, c’est boin.	And if the bleeding stops, that is good.
Se ceu non, se li fai aerdre ventouses au dos et as mameles sens ferir;	If not, apply cupping to the back and breasts without injuring them;
puis pren lainne, et la moille en jus de plantain ou en jus d’aglentier avec vin viel, et fai aerdre au leu.	Then take wool, moisten it with plantain juice or sorrel juice mixed with old wine, and apply it to the area.
Et quant li aposteme repose, si cure lou leu d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez;	And when the abscess has subsided, treat the area with ointment until it is healed;
et celle qui est apelee «albathir» est rouge, et est semblans a I chief aspre, si le covient coper si com j’ai dit le thelul;	And that which is called "albathir" is red, and it resembles a rough head, so it must be cut as I have said about the thul.
et puis lou cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	And then treat it until it is healed.
des apostemes de la marris	for abscesses of the flesh
Maintes manieres d’aposteme vienent en la marris, si com chancre et aposteme pierous et herpes et estiomenes et fistules et emorroides et aposteme chaut, et plusors autres maladies que j’ai dit en la division.	Many types of abscesses occur in the flesh, such as canker sores and stone abscesses and herpes and ulcerations and fistulas and hemorrhoids and hot abscesses, and many other diseases that I have mentioned in the division.
Il covient donques que je die en cest traitier l’aposteme chaut qui vient en la marris, qui n’est mie des apostemes que coillent bowe;	Therefore, I must speak in this treatise about the hot abscess that comes in the armpit, which is not one of those that occur in the bowel.
et se tu vues savoir l’ovraige de fer, si regarde se li apostemes est agus en l’encomencement de sa venue, et plain de chalor et de fievre, et s’il devient rouge se tu le pues veoir.	And if you wish to know the work of iron, then observe whether the abscess is hard at the beginning of its appearance, and full of heat and fever, and turns red if you can see it.
Adonques ne te haster mie de percier, mais lou fais meurer tant que li dolor soit apaisie;	Then do not hurry to pierce it, but let it come to maturity until the pain subsides;
et puis fai seoir lou malaide sus I siege, et ait II petis sieges ou il se cline, et apoie sus son dos et assemble ses piez as parties defuer la jambe;	And then have the patient sit on one chair, and let him lean against two small chairs where he can rest his back, and support his feet at the parts below the knee;
et soient ses cuixes espandues, et mette ses braz desoz ses genous, et les lie bien d’un boin liien;	And let his thighs be spread out, and have him place his arms under his knees, and bind them securely with a good cloth;
puis succe li baille devers lou destre costeit, et i amenistre l’estrument dont on oevre la bouche de la marris, de coi ci aprés vient li forme;	Then succeed in bringing the instrument to his right side for working on the mouth of the dislocation, as will be described further;
et covient que quant tu i vues amenistrer cest estrument, que tu fiches le rait premier ens por savoir la parfondeté de la marris, si que ceu qui entre ens de l’estrument n’i viegne plus em parfont qu’il ne doit, et qu’il ne blece la malaide;	And it is necessary that when you bring this instrument, you first insert a probe to determine the depth of the dislocation so that what enters into the instrument does not go too deep and does not harm the patient;
et se li estrumens est plus grans, si covient covrir la parfondesce de la marris de drapelz, si que li estrumens ne li grieve;	and if the instrument is larger, it is necessary to cover the depths of the wound with cloths so that the instrument does not irritate it;
et covient qu’il mette le cornet de l’estrument au desus, et qu’il teigne l’estrument.	and he should place the tip of the instrument above, and hold it in position.
Et quant li apostemes apert, et on lou fent a la main mol, si le covient coper au chief, au spatumile leit;	And when the abscess is ready to be opened, and it is gently incised by hand, then it should be cut at the top, near the suture line;
et quant li bowe est vuidie, si covient que tu mettes en la plaie tentes moillies en oile roset, ou en oile vert sec;	and when the cavity is emptied, it is necessary to place moistened cloths in rose oil, or in dry green oil;
et met la tente fuer de la plaie au parfont de la marris, et met par defuer sus la marris et sus le poignil lainne nette moillie en aigue ou malves soient cuites;	and place the cloth directly over the wound at its deepest part, and put clean, moistened wool on top of the wound and around the finger in water or decoction of mallows;
puis le cure aprés II jors d’oignement avenant a ceu, tant qu’il soit sanez;	Then treat after two days of ointment application as needed, until it is healed.
et aucune fois leve on la marris et la plaie par clistere d’aigue et de miel, et puis d’aigue ou racines de lis et aristologe longe soient cuites;	and sometimes one lifts the swelling and cleans the wound with a mixture of water and honey, and then with water or boiled roots of lilies and artemisia.
puis reveigne a l’oignement.	Then return to applying ointment.
Et se li plaie est reponue en la marris, si covient que tu te gardes de cuire de fer, mais cure la si com nos avons dit en la division.	And if the wound is laid on the poultice, then you must avoid heating with iron, but treat it as we have said in the section.
de l’enfantement	of childbirth
Mestier est premier a la baile qu’elle conoisse la figure de l’enfantement natureil, et li signes si est quant tu vois la femme apresser aval, et desire odorer l’ar:	It is necessary first for the midwife to know the signs of natural childbirth, and these signs are present when you see the woman pressing downward and desiring to smell the air:
adonques se haste li enfes de fuer issir;	then the fetus hastens to come out;
adonc saiches que cil enfantemens est selonc la figure natureil, et est li issue soz son chief, et li secondine avec lui;	then you know that this birth is according to the natural pattern, and the passage is under its head, and the afterbirth with it;
et quant tu vois ces signes, si covient presser legierement son ventre, si que li enfes isse tost;	And when you see these signs, it is necessary to gently press his abdomen so that the child comes out quickly;
car quant il dessent sus son chief, si ist li secondine avec lui, et est mondee li marris de ses superfluitez par bone mundification;	for when it descends over its head, the afterbirth comes out with it, and the mother is cleansed of her excesses through proper postpartum care;
et cist qui vient autrement ne vient mie naturelment.	and those who come in another manner do not come naturally.
Car il vient aucune fois sus ses piez, et vient fuer li cors ou li chiés, et les mains, ou il vient sus son ventre, ou sovin, et est convertis par aventure sor son col, et par autres figures malvaises;	For sometimes it comes out feet first, and can exit from the thighs or hands, or emerge above its belly, or even twist around its neck, and in other deformed ways;
si est mestier a la baile qu’elle soit saige et subtilz en ces choses, et se warse d’error et de decevement, et je vos mostrerai toutes les figures coment on li doit aidier.	it is necessary for the midwife to be wise and skilled in these matters, to avoid error and deception, and I will show you all the forms in which one should assist them.
Se li enfes vient sus son chief par issue natureil, et li femme enfante griement, et li vertus de li est foible, si la fai seoir sus une selle, ou les femmes la tienent;	If the child comes out naturally on its head, and the woman gives birth painfully, and her strength is weak, then make her sit on a stool, or have women hold her;
et arose sa nature d’oile ou fenugreic soit cuit, et puis boute li baile entre ses dois le petit spatumile dont ci est li forme:	and prepare her nature with oil or fenugreek boiled, and then pour the mixture between her two small stibium containers whose form is described here:
et fende la secondine, et cope a son ungle tant que li moistors qui est ens corre fuers;	and split the second fingernail, and cut it at its base so that the moisture inside can come out;
et preint lou ventre de la femme tant que li enfes dessende, et s’il ne dessent, si covient clisterizer la femme de muscillaige de fenugrec avec oile de sisament;	and press the woman's abdomen until the child descends, and if it does not descend, then she must be given an enema of fenugreek mucilage with sesame oil;
puis la fai preindre et esternuer de condisi, et tien sa bouche et son neis une houre:	then make her drink and sneeze from conditi, and hold her mouth and nose for an hour:
si istra maintenant l’enfes.	Now remove the hair.
Et se les II mains issent fuer, si covient que tu les ramoinne legierement poc et poc;	And if both hands come out of joint, you must reset them gently bit by bit;
et s’elles n’i puent entrer, si met la femme sus I siege, et li lieve les piés en haut;	and if they cannot be reset, place the patient on a chair and raise their feet up;
puis deboute le siege sus terre, et teigne on la femme, qu’elle ne chiece au deboutement;	then lift the chair off the ground, and support the patient so she does not fall when standing;
et se li mains n’i puet entrer, et li enfes muert, si li cope les mains au couteil qui est ci devant mis, et estrai l’enfant, et ramoine igalment.	and if the hand cannot be reset and the child dies, cut the hands with a knife that is placed here beforehand, and extract the child, and reset gently.
de l’issue de l’enfant sus ses piés	of the issue of the child upon its feet
Quant li enfes vient sus ses piez, si lou covient bouter en haut;	When the child comes to its feet, it is necessary to lift it up;
et puis le torne poc et poc, tant qu’il soit igalz;	and then turn it little by little, until it is even;
puis preigne I des piez et l’estende poc et poc.	then take one of the feet and extend it little by little.
Cant il saut jusc’as cuixes, si la comande a preindre, et la fai esternuer de condisi;	When it jumps up to the thighs, then instruct them to grasp it, and make it sneeze from this position.
si saut fuer, se Deus vuet.	and may it jump out, if God wills.
Et s’il n’ist fuer si com nos avons dit, si le torne poc et poc, tant qu’il soit selonc la figure natureil.	And if it does not go further as we have said, turn it little by little until it is according to its natural form.
Car adonques ist il legierement.	For then it will move easily.
Et s’il ne vient fuer si com nos avons, dit si pren muscillaige de altee, et oile de sisament, et gomme fondue, et broie tout en I mortier;	And if it does not come out as we wish, take mastic of the terebinth tree, and sesame oil, and boiled gum, and grind all in a mortar;
et met sus la nature de la femme dedens et defuer cest oignement, puis la fai seoir en aigue tede jusque desoz les costelz;	and place the mixture according to the woman's condition and apply this ointment, then have her sit in warm water up to below her ribs;
et quant elle est moillifie desoz, se li fai I coliere de mirre, et li met desoz, et li laisse une houre;	and when it is softened, apply the collar of myrrh to it and place it underneath, and leave it for an hour;
puis la fai seoir sus I siege, puis la fai esternuer et estraint sa bouche et son neis, et li preint le ventre legierement, car li enfes saut maintenant.	then have her sit on the chair, then make her sneeze and hold her mouth and nose, and gently press her stomach, for the baby jumps now.
de l’issue de l’enfant sus ses genous	of the delivery of the child onto her knees
Quant li enfes vient en ceste forme, si i mette li baile ses mains poc et poc;	When the child comes in this condition, place the mother's hands on it little by little;
puis soit sovinee sus son col, et li pendent li piez aval, et soit gisans sor I lit;	then let her be seated on her neck, and hang her feet down, and lie her on the bed;
et plie ses mains poc et poc, et puis li preint les mains sus lou ventre, et li oste les cussins desoz, tant qu’elle soit appareillie aval;	and fold her hands little by little, and then press her hands on the stomach, and remove the cushions underneath until she is prepared to go down;
et se li enfes ne saut, si pren ses piez et li muef forment, puis li muef lou ventre amont, puis i boute tes mains;	and if the child does not jump, then take his feet and move them apart, then pull up his belly with your hands;
et ewe l’enfant poc et poc;	and lift the child little by little;
et comande a la femme qu’elle se preigne tant que li enfes isse.	and instruct the woman to hold on as tightly as she can when the child exits.
de l’issue de l’enfant qui vient dou large une main pendant	of the birth of the child who comes with one hand hanging down
I covient engignier a ramener la main:	It is necessary for the surgeon to return the hand:
s’on ne la puet ramener, si fai lever la femme, et aler;	if it cannot be returned, then help the woman stand and walk;
s’elle ne puet aler, si la fai gesir sus I lit, et li deboute les jambes forment;	if she cannot walk, then have her lie on the bed and spread her legs apart;
puis amenistre lou muscillaige que j’ai conteit;	then apply the ointment that I have described;
et s’elle n’enfante, si la fai seoir sus I siege, puis estudie au rameneir la main;	And if she does not give birth, seat her on a chair, then proceed to reset the hand.
et ewe l’enfant selonc la figure natureil, et la fai esternuer, et li comande qu’elle se preigne tant que li enfes isse fuer.	And place the child according to its natural position, and make her sneeze, and instruct her to hold on until the infant comes out.
de l’issue de l’enfant sus son col, et ait espandues ses mains, et sa faice tornee devers lou dos sa mere	of the birth of the child upon his neck, and with his hands spread out, and his face turned towards his mother's back
I covient que li baile teigne sa main, puis le torne poc et poc, et l’ewe legierement;	It is necessary for the patient to hold their hand, then turn it little by little, and move it gently;
et quant il est igalz, si met sus la nature muscillaige de altee et oile, si com nos avons dit, puis li comande qu’elle se mueve poc et poc;	And when it is even, place the natural medicinal herbs and oil, as we have said, then instruct her to move little by little;
et quant tu avras ce fait, si la fai seoir sus I siege, et li comande k’elle se preigne;	And when you have done this, seat her on the chair, and instruct her to hold on;
et la fai esternuer.	And cause it to sneeze.
de ceste meisme maniere a tout la secondine	In the same manner for the entire second part
Quant il vient fuer en ceste maniere a tout la secondine, si cope la secondine a ton ungle, tant que li moistors soit vuidie;	When the swelling comes to this state in the second area, cut into it with your nail until the moisture is emptied;
et se li enfes pent sus sa faice et sus son col, si la cope des la boude, qu’elle ne soit retenue, et muere li enfes;	and if the swelling rises on its face and neck, cut it from the base so that it is not restrained, and move the swelling;
puis boute l’enfant dedens, tant que tu l’aies mis si com il covient, et comande a la femme qu’elle se preigne aucune fois:	then insert the child as needed until it is in the proper position, and instruct the woman to hold onto something for support;
adonques si istra legierement.	then extract gently.
de l’issue des gemelz	Of the issue of the thighs
Saiches que gemeil naissent maintes fois, et aucune fois en naissent III ou IIII;	Know that gout comes many times, and sometimes three or four come at once;
et ceu n’est mie estrainge chose, et poc avient.	and this is not a strange thing, and it often happens.
Dui sont estrainge chose, et ne vivent mie, se poc nom;	These are strange things, and they do not live, though sometimes they occur;
je sai ceu, qu’il soient multipliiet, et sont desevrez par lou syfac qui les devise, qui est liiez a la boude;	I know that they are multiplied and are separated by the surface that divides them, which is attached to the root;
et aucune fois issent ausi naturelment com uns tous sous, si com nos avons dit.	and sometimes they emerge as naturally as any others, as we have said.
Et s’il issent griement, si la cure si com nos avons dit, et soit li baile subtilz, et faice tost et legierement ceu qu’elle fait;	And if they emerge severely, treat them as we have said, and let the hand be skillful, and do quickly and gently what it does;
et faice ensi com il vaut mues a salut.	and do so as it is worth for healing.
de plusors enfans	of many children
Aucune fois sont formez en la marris I ou II ou III ou IIII ou V ou VI ou VII, ou plusors jusc’a XV, et sont tout formeit en forme d’enfant par le mesurement dou saige glorious, et couvient que li baile saiche tout ceu, car par aventure semblans chose li avient;	Sometimes they are formed in the marrow I or II or III or IV or V or VI or VII, or even up to XV, and are completely shaped like a child according to the measurement of the wise physician, and it is necessary that he carefully examines all this, for perhaps something similar may happen to them;
si faice selonc ceu qu’il covient.	do as is appropriate according to these instructions.
de l’enfant mort	of the dead child
Quant tu cures la femme de l’enfant mort ou ventre, si com j’ai dit en la division, et il ne vient fuers, et tu es constrains d’ovraige de mains;	When you treat a woman of a dead child in her womb, as I said in the division, and it does not come out, and you are constrained to work with your hands;
si covient que tu saiches se li femme est de saine vertut, et n’ait accident ou elle ait paor de mort;	you must determine if the woman is in good health and has no condition that causes fear of death;
si covient que li femme soit sovinee sus son dos, et soit ses chiés enclins aval, et les jambes levees;	The woman should be laid on her back, and her shoulders inclined downwards, and her legs raised;
et li ministre la teigne de II pars, ou elle soit liie au lit si qu’elle ne soit traite au dessendement de l’enfant;	and the attendant should hold her from two sides, so that she is supported on the bed in such a way that she does not slide down with the descent of the child;
puis frotez la bouche de la marris d’oiles moistes avec muscillaige de altee et de fenugrec et semence de lin, puis oigne li baile ses mains de ces oiles et de ces muscillaiges;	then rub the mouth with warm oil mixed with a paste of hellebore and fenugreek seeds, and smear her hands with these oils and pastes;
puis les boute en la marris legierement, puis quiere I leu ou elle boute les oncines que soient covenaubles a ceu, et pren warde se li enfes est apparilliez qu’il dessende sus son chief;	then gently press them into the warm oil, then place your hands in positions suitable for this, and watch to see if the child is ready to descend head first;
si fiche les oncines en ses eulz ou en son col ou en sa bouche ou en som palais ou desoz la barbe ou en la forcele ou pres des costez, et se li dessendemens est sus piez, se li fiche ou poignil et as costes moienes;	Place the cautery on his eyes or neck or in his mouth or palate or behind the beard or in the armpit or near the ribs, and if the descent is at the feet, place it on the toes and middle sides.
et covient qu’il teigne l’oncine a sa main destre, et mette la corbeure entre ses dois de la senestre main, et li boute a tout sa main legierement, et fiche l’oncine en aucun de ces leus que nos avons dit, tant qu’il viegne a la chose vuide;	He should hold the cautery in his right hand, place it between his two fingers of the left hand, and press lightly with his whole hand, placing the cautery in any of the places we have mentioned until it reaches an empty spot.
et c’est li forme de l’oncine:	And this is the form of the cautery:
puis fiche encontre I autre oncine, ou le tier se tu en as mestier, si que li estractions soit igalz;	Then place the other cautery opposite it, or the third one if needed, so that the extractions are equal.
et puis l’estent igalment en movant d’une part et d’autre, por mues issir, et soit li oncines dentez por mues tenir, si com ci est li forme:	and then stretch it evenly by moving from side to side, so that the bones can exit, and let the muscles be in such a way as to hold the bones, as shown here is the form:
Et s’il en demoure une partie, si oigne li baile aucuns de ses dois d’oile, et les boute en celle partie, et traie l’autre partie;	And if one part remains stuck, anoint the joint with some of his oil and push it into that part, and pull on the other part;
et s’il en i demoure point, si met cest oncine ou plus haut leu, et fai ceu tant qu’il s’en isse tout fuers.	and if any part remains stuck, place this muscle higher up and do so until it all comes out.
Et se l’une mains vient devant l’autre, et il ne puet ramener por l’estreignement, si covient que tu envoloupes sus I drapeil, tant qu’il isse tote;	And if one hand comes in front of the other and he cannot bring it back for grasping, you must wrap around with a cloth until it fully emerges;
puis la cope en la jointure de la plante ou au coute, et ensi covient que tu faices en l’autre main, et as II piés.	Then place it at the joint of the sole or at the heel, and thus you must do with the other hand, and for both feet.
Et se li chiés de l’enfant est gros et il est estrois en l’issue, ou il ait ou chief aigue assemblee, si covient que tu boute le spatumile espinous entre tes dois, et fent le chief et estrai l’aigue;	And if the head of the infant is large and it is tight in the birth canal, or there is an acute assembly on the head, then you must insert a sharp spatula between your two fingers, cut the scalp and extract the fluid;
ou tu la ront a l’estrument qui est apelez «almidach», de coi li forme vient avec les estrumens ou chapistre qui est aprés cestui;	where you round it with the instrument called "almidach," from which the shape comes with the instruments in the chapter that follows this one;
et ensi meisme faice se li enfes a grant chief naturelment;	and do the same if the infant has a large head naturally;
et puis traie fuer les osses as tenailles, et se li chiés saut fuer et il estraint a la forcele, si soit fendus, tant que li moistors qui est ou pis issue fuer;	and then pull the bones with pliers, and if the head jumps out and it is stuck at the forceps, cut them until the moisture that is in the foot exit is reached;
et s’elle ne puet issir, si le cope par pieces au mues que tu pues;	and if it cannot come out, cut it piece by piece until you can.
et s’il est enflez au ventre ou desoz les costez, si covient que tu lou perces tant que li moistors corre.	and if it is swollen in the belly or under the ribs, you must pierce it until the moisture runs out.
Et se li enfes est sus ses piez, si est li attraction legiere, et li adrecemens a la bouche de la marris est legier.	And if the child is on its feet, then the traction is light, and the adjustment to the mouth of the socket is light.
Et s’il est estrois au ventre ou au pis, si couvient que tu l’estraies a I drapeil envoloupeit sus la main;	And if it is tight in the belly or chest, you must stretch it with an instrument wrapped around your hand;
et fent le ventre ou le pis, tant que li moistors qui i est corre;	and cut into the belly or chest until the moisture that is inside runs out;
et se li autre membre sont osteit, et li chiez demoure, si boute li baile sa main em parfont de la marris, et le traie jusc’a la bouche de la marris;	and if the other limb is removed and the head remains, push your hand in firmly through the wound, and pull it out to the mouth of the wound;
puis i boute I oncine ou II, et le trai fuer;	Then insert either one or two, and pull them out forcefully;
et se li bouche de la marris est retrecie por aposteme chaut qui i est venus, si n’i covient mie travillier, ains covient amenistrer choses moistes et grasses;	and if the mouth of the sore is narrowed due to a hot abscess that has come there, one should not work on it, but instead administer moist and greasy things;
et li amenistre emplaustres, et siece en aigue mollifians et amoistans.	and the physician applies plasters, and uses aqueous solutions that soften and moisten.
Et se li enfes est sus son costeit, et tu le pues mettre igal, si amenistre ceu que nos avons dit en l’enfant vif;	And if the child is on its side, and you can make it lie flat, then treat it as we have said for a living child;
et s’on nen ait pooir, si lou trai fuer par pieces, et n’i laissier rien de la secondine.	and if one has no power to do so, then pull it out forcefully in pieces, and leave nothing of the placenta behind.
Et quant tu avras ce fait, se li amenistre ceu que nos avons dit ens apostemes chaus que vienent en la marris;	And when you have done this, apply the remedies we mentioned for large abscesses that come in the marsh;
et se decorremens de sanc vient, si soit mise en aigue restraignant, et li amenistre autres cures.	and if bleeding occurs, apply cold compresses, and use other remedies as needed.
Et je vis une femme en cui ventre uns enfes avoit esteit mors, puis consut I autre sus celui, et refut mors li autres.	And I saw a woman in whom the fetus in her womb had died, then another was conceived upon it, and that one also died.
Aprés lonc tens li vint uns apostemes en la boude, et enfla tant qu’il ovrit, et comensa a grant porreture.	After a long time, she developed an abscess in her throat, and it swelled so much that it burst, and began to severely decay.
je fui apelez a la cure, et i pensai lonc tens, et ne pot soder li plaie.	I was called to treat it, and I pondered for a long time, and could not heal the wound.
Je mis sus emplaustre de fort attraction, et en issit uns os, et aprés aucuns jors uns autres.	I applied a plaster with strong adhesive properties, and out of it came a bone, and after several days another one.
Je me mervillai mout, por ceu c’ou ventre n’a point d’os.	I marveled greatly, for there are no bones in the abdomen.
Si pensai que c’estoit des os d’un enfant mort.	I thought that they were the bones of a deceased child.
Je quis la plaie, et en traï mains os, tant que li femme fut em millor point;	I treated the wound, and laid bare the bones, until the woman was in a better state;
et vesquit li femme lonc tens ensi, et issoit adés un poc de bowe dou leu;	and treated the woman for a long time in this manner, and she would occasionally discharge some pus from the area;
et je n’ai recordeit cest chapistre fuer que por ceu que, quant li maistres trueve une estrainge chose, qu’il i saiche mettre aide.	and I have recorded this chapter for the reason that when masters encounter something unusual, they should know how to offer assistance.
dou ramener la marris a son leu	to return the joint to its place
Ci aprés vient li forme dou pressor, a coi on ewe les livres;	Here follows the form of the pressure treatment, which can be found in books;
et a II tornans as II chiés des II liiens.	and to two turns at the two shoulders of the two limbs.
Toutevoie, li cornes soit plus subtilz dou restrictoire, et soit fais de ebene ou de bux;	Nevertheless, let the horns be finer than the rest of the instrument, and made of ebony or boxwood;
et soit li bouche dou fust I doi de large, et li marge des arbres I doit, et de lonc une palme et demi;	and let the mouth of the shaft be two fingers wide, and the margin of the wood one finger, and in length half a palm;
et enmi les II liemens soient dui ajostemens de cest meisme fust, qui soient fermeit en l’un et en l’autre, de demi palme de lonc ou un poc plus;	and between the two limbs there should be two adjustments of the same shaft, which are fixed in one and the other, half a palm long or a bit more;
et cist dui ajostement sont bouteit en la bouche de la marris por ovrir quant on torne les II cornes.	and these two adjustments are positioned at the mouth of the instrument to open when turning the two horns.
Une autre forme, a sa semblance plus subtilz et plus legiere, soit faite de fust de ebene ou de bux, selonc la semblance des tenailles;	Another form, more subtle and lighter, should be made of ebony wood or boxwood, according to the appearance of the tongs;
et ait as II chiés II ajostemens, si com tu vois, d’une palme de lonc, et II dois de large;	and have two heads with two joints, as you see, one palm in length, and two fingers wide;
et quant tu vues ovrir la marris a tout l’estrument, si fai seoir la femme sor I lit, les piez pendant et les jambes overtes, puis boute les II ajostemens ajostez ensamble en la marris, et tien le chief de l’estrument desoz entre ses cuixes;	and when you wish to open the vagina with the instrument, have the woman sit on a bed, her feet hanging down and her legs spread, then insert the two joints of the instrument together into the vagina, and hold the head of the instrument under between her thighs;
puis oevre ta main a tout l’estrument, si com tu as fait as tenailles igalment, selonc la quantiteit que tu vues ovrir la bouche de la marris, tant que li baile faice ceu qu’elle vuet.	then work your hand on the entire instrument, as you did with the tongs equally, according to the amount you wish to open the entrance of the vagina, until it is as wide as she desires.
Cist estrument sont tuit sormontez, et sont multiplies lor semblances;	These instruments are all elevated, and their kinds are multiplied;
et quant li mires les ait apareilliez, tant est plus hastans li oevre, et plus haute as homes por lor quantiteit.	and when the doctor has them prepared, the work is done more quickly, and they are more effective for people in terms of their quantity.
Si ne despire mie l’estrument que tu ne l’aies apparelliet, car lor necessitez n’est mie escusauble.	Do not despise the instrument because you have not prepared it, for their needs are not excusable.
Quant li secondine est retenue a l’enfantement, si covient que tu comandes a la malaide qu’ele reteigne son alaine, et puis la fai esternuer de condisi, et li estraint tes mains a la bouche et au neis;	When the afterbirth is retained during childbirth, you must instruct the patient to hold her breath, and then make her sneeze with something appropriate, and press your hands over her mouth and nose;
et s’elle saut per ceu, bien est.	and if she expels it because of this, so much the better.
Se ceu non, si prent I pot, et fai I pertus ou cuvercle, et i met herbes que puissent ovrir la bouche de la marris, si com calament, rue, anis, camomille, cassialigne et centoire;	If not, take a poultice and make a hole in the cover, and place herbs that can open the mouth of the womb, such as calamint, rue, anise, chamomile, cascara, and centaury;
toutes ces herbes, ou aucunes d’eles, soient cuites ou pot en aigue sus le feu;	all these herbs, or some of them, are to be boiled in water over the fire;
puis met une caine ou pertus dou pot, et l’autre chief en la bouche de la marris, et la teigne tant que li vapors viegne dedens la marris;	then place one end of a tube in the opening of the pot, and the other end in the mouth of the jar, and let it draw until the vapor comes inside the jar;
puis la fai esternuer, si com nos avons dit.	then make her sneeze, as we have said.
Si saut li secondine hastanment.	The second joint moves quickly.
Et s’elle remaint aprés ceste cure, et n’ist mie fuer, si comande a la baile qu’ele moille sa main senestre en oile de sesement ou en muscillaige de altee, et puis la boute en la nature, et quiere la secondine;	And if she remains after this treatment and does not improve, instruct the patient to moisten her left hand in sesame oil or in hellebore juice, and then apply it to the affected area, and seek a second opinion;
et quant elle l’avra trovee, si la preigne et l’estende poc et poc droitement, si que li marris ne chiece a l’estraction;	and when she has found it, take it and stretch it little by little straightly, so that the pus does not drip during extraction;
mais la covient movoir legierement a destre et a senestre, et puis traie;	but you must move it gently to the right and to the left, and then straighten;
si venra et se desaerdra.	it will come and disengage.
Et se li bouche de la marris est jai estrecie, nos avons dit la cure d’esternuer, et de fumigation des herbes;	And if the mouth of the nostril is narrow, we have described the treatment of sneezing and fumigation with herbs;
et s’elle n’ist de tout ceu que nos avons dit, si garde que tu ne foloies au traire;	and if it does not respond to everything we have said, be careful not to force it;
mais il couvient que ceu qui est a la bouche de la marris, que tu le lies a la cuixe de la femme, puis la clisterize d’oignement tetrafarmaçon;	but it is necessary that the part of the nostril be tied to the woman's thigh, then administer an enema of four-part ointment;
si la porrira et remettra, et venra fuer;	it will come out and return, and it will succeed;
mais toutevoie, quant elle porrist si en vient male odor au stomac et au chief, et blece la malaide.	however, when it comes to this, if a bad smell reaches the stomach and head, and it distresses the patient.
Si covient donques fumigations covenaubles a ceu:	Therefore, appropriate fumigations should be used for them:
aucun des anciens ont esproveit fumigation de cresson et de figues seches.	some of the ancients have tried fumigation with cabbage and dried figs.
Li forme de l’estrument a coi on fumige la femme a la retenue des flors et de la secondine si est ceste:	The form of the instrument with which one fumigates the woman to retain her flowers and menstrual cycle is as follows:
Et est de voirre semblant a une caine, et met on le chief subtil en la nature, et les chiés larges sus le feu;	And it appears similar to a cane, and one places the head subtly in the nature, and the joints wide over the fire;
et soit li fumigations sus les charbons, et la teigne tant qu’elle soit gastee, et rencomence une autre.	and let the fumigation be above the charcoal, and continue it until it is spent, and then start another one.
de percier lou fondement	to pierce the fundament
Maint enfant naissent qui n’ont mie le fondement perciet, ains l’ait estoupeit uns subtilz syfac:	Many children are born who do not have a discernible anus, instead it is closed by subtle membranes:
si covient donques a la baile qu’ele perce celui syfac a son doit, et ne lou perce mie de spatumile agut, et garse le lacement qu’elle ne le touche;	Then it is necessary for the surgeon to incise that abscess at its proper place, and not do so with a sharp spatula, and be careful that it does not touch;
puis met sus lainne moillie en vin et en oile, puis la cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez.	then apply wet linen soaked in wine and oil, then treat with an ointment until he is healed.
Et se tu doutes qu’il ne restoupe, si met ou pertus une caine de plonc, et li laisse mains jors, et soit ostee quant li enfes vuet aler en chambres.	And if you doubt that it will stay in place, insert a lead tube into the hole, and leave it there for several days, and remove it when the patient wishes to go to bed.
Et aucune fois vient cist estoupemens de soudement de plaie ou d’aposteme;	And sometimes this obstruction comes from the sudden closure of a wound or abscess;
si covient coper celui soudement:	then it is necessary to cut that closure:
si soit curez, si com nos avons dit de la caine de plonc.	and treat it as we have said about the tendon of the finger.
de la fistule dou fondement	of the fistula of the anus
Fistules qui vienent desoz le fondement sont nodation, et groissor que vienent delez lou fondement defuer, ou en l’espaice des II parties, si a une fistule ou plusors;	Fistulas that come from under the anus are nodular, and those that come near the anus to protrude, or in the space between the two parts, may be one fistula or several;
et quant celle nodation est anciene, si aoeuvre, et encort moistor awouse blainche ou subtilz bowe, et aucune fois sont ces fistule persans;	And when that knotting is old, it works, and still moisture keeps white or subtle bowel, and sometimes these fistulas are perforating;
et sont conues par ceu qu’il en ist ou egestion ou ventositeit quant li malaide fait egestion, et par aventure en saut uns vers.	And they are known by what comes out in vomiting or flatulence when the patient vomits, and sometimes a worm is expelled.
Et si a fistules que percent jusc’a la vessie, et jusc’a la moitiet de la verge;	And there are fistulas that penetrate to the bladder, and up to half of the penis;
et parvienent jusc’a la jointure de la cuixe, et jusc’a nout de la kowe.	and reach to the joint of the thigh, and to the root of the knee.
Et ensi conoist on la fistule persant au fondement, et ne mie persant:	And thus one knows the perforating fistula at the fundament, and not perforating:
et est que tu boutes ton doi indice ou fondement, et boute une aguille subtil d’arain ou de fer en la fistule quant il n’i a tortuositeit.	And place your index finger at the base, and insert a fine needle of steel or iron into the fistula when there is no tortuosity.
Et s’il ait tortuositeit, si i boute une tente de plonc subtil, ou I poil de cheval, tant que tu sentes la tente ou le poil a ton doit;	And if there is tortuosity, insert a fine tent of linen or horsehair until you feel the tent or hair with your finger;
et se tu ne le sens, et il ne vient dou pertus egestion ne ventositeit ne ver, si com nos avons dit:	and if you do not feel it, and there is no passage of pus or air or blood, as we have said:
saiches qu’elle ne perce mie;	you know that it does not perforate;
si te haste dou curer.	then hurry to treat it.
Et quant li fistule est persans jusc’a la vessie ou jusc’a conduit de l’urine, si en saut li urine, et ne puet soudeir par medicines.	And when the fistula reaches to the bladder or to the passage of urine, then he urinates through it, and cannot be treated with medicines.
S’elle est percie jusc’a la jointure de la cuixe, si est li tente venans jusc’au leu;	If it perforates up to the knee joint, then the tent reaches that place;
s’il n’i a tortuositeit et li invention de la dolor entor, si est qu’il en ist adés bowe, et n’i vaut medicine ne soudement par oignement;	if there is no twisting or the pain around it does not indicate injury, then it will quickly become a cramp, and neither medicine nor immediate treatment by poultice is effective;
et en ces fistules persans n’a point de cure fuer que labor, et vaniteit des folz mires qui s’en entremettent.	and in these persistent fistulas there is no cure other than diligent work, and the vanity of foolish physicians who intervene;
En celle qui n’est mie persans et n’est mie anciene, a esperance de saniteit par fer, si com j’ai esproveit, et est que li malaides gise entre tes mains sus son dos;	In the case that is not persistent and is not old, there is hope for healing by iron, as I have experienced, and it is when the patient lies on their back with their spine between your hands;
et li lieve les jambes jusque sus ses cuixes, et ait ses cuixes enclinees a son ventre;	and the patient lifts their legs up to their thighs, and keeps their thighs inclined towards their abdomen;
puis boute une tente d’arain, ou de plonc s’il i a tortuositeit, tant que tu saiches ou li tente vient.	then insert a tent of linen, or of flax if there is twisting, until you know where the tent reaches;
Se li malaides la sent entor le fondement, si covient que tu i boutes ton doi indice, se sens adonques que li tente l’ait perciet;	If the patient feels it around the fundament, then you must insert your finger there; if you then feel that the tent has been pierced,
et soit descoverte ou tu sens entre ton doit le syfac ou la char, adonques saiches qu’elle est persans;	and if you feel the space between your finger and the skin is exposed, then you know it is perforated;
si n’i travillier mie c’on ne la puet saner.	do not proceed as it cannot be healed.
On dist toutevoie c’on em puet bien saner aucuns, mais ce avient poc;	It is said that some can be healed well, but this happens rarely;
et li aide c’on i fait, si est c’on eschaufe le cautere subtil selonc la largesce de la fistule, si com il est devant dit;	and the treatment involves heating the cautery gently according to the width of the fistula, as was mentioned before;
et le boute tout chaut en la fistule, tant qu’il viegne delez le fondement;	and inserting it fully heated into the fistula until it reaches near the fundament;
et faice ceu II fois ou III, tant que tu saiches que ces chars fautrees soient arses, qui sont semblant a une penne d’oiseil;	and do this two or three times until you know that the burnt flesh is charred, which resembles a feather of a bird;
et puis le cure de tentes moillies em burre, tant que celle chars isse fuer, puis le cure d’oignement enjanrant char et soudant.	and then treat it with moist cloths dipped in butter until the flesh grows back, then treat it with an ointment that promotes healing and binds.
S’il est ensi sanez, c’est bien.	If he is thus well, it is good.
Se ceu, nom autrement ne puet estre sanez;	If this cannot be done otherwise, it cannot be healed;
et se li tente entre, et ne perce jusc’au doit qui est ou fondement, et a entre ton doi et la tente une coverture espesse de char ou de syfac, et tu vois la fistule a ceu qui enseut la coverture dou keur;	and if the tent (probe) enters but does not reach the deepest part that is at the foundation, and there is a thick layer of flesh or fat between your probe and the abscess, and you see the fistula under this covering of the heart;
si le cope des l’encomencement de la fistule, et boute adés avant la tente, et pues le cautere aprés, tant qu’il viegne au chief de la tente;	cut it from the beginning of the fistula and then insert the probe again, and apply the cautery afterward until you reach the end of the probe;
et sera delivré li tente, et cherra;	and the bladder will be relieved, and it will fall;
puis mondefie celles chars fautrees que semblent une penne d’oisel, et n’en remaigne niant.	then cleanse those damaged tissues that appear like a bird's feather, and leave nothing behind.
Et si li sans te vaint, et cort entre toi et l’uevre, si le cauterize de feu ou de medicine ague.	And if the blood fails you, and it cuts between you and the work, then cauterize with fire or with astringent medication.
Car li cauteres de feu assemble II bones choses:	For the fire cauterization brings together two good things:
c’est a savoir, l’arsure de ces chars ajostees, et l’esteinchement de sanc et la sechor de la moistor;	that is to say, the removal of excessive tissue, and stopping the blood and drying the moisture;
puis le cure de tentes moillies em burre ou en choz broiez, tant que li leus giete bowe, et isse fuer li chars arse en la bowe;	then treat moist bladders with butter or ground substances until the area sweats, and remove the burned tissue from the wound.
puis cure la plaie des oignemens soudans enjanrans dure char, et sont les medicines seches.	then treat the wound with hot applications and hardening dressings, and the medications should be dry.
Car quant il est restoree, si est sanee et ne revient mie.	For when it is restored, it is healed and does not return.
Et se fistule vient jusc’a parfont dou fondement, et est esloigniez dou cors, se li boute ton doi ou fondement, et enquier ceu.	And if a fistula comes up to the base of the tailbone and is distant from the body, place your finger inside it and examine it.
Se tu sens la tente, et entre II est li toile ou li syfac ou chars, ou il est pres a percier, si n’i ait fuers que voie de fiance et d’esperance, par l’aministrement de l’une des III manieres:	If you feel the tent, and it is between II tissues or flesh where it is close to piercing, there should be no hesitation but proceed with faith and hope, by means of one of the III methods:
ou tu le cauterizes si com nos avons dit, ou tu le cope jusc’a fons, ou se tu pues si i met tentes et cure si com premier;	where you cauterize it as we have said, or cut it down to the base, or if you can place tents and treat it as described first;
et n’aler mie trop em parfont, que tu ne coper le tenement qui tient le fondement, et viegne li egestions par lai sens volenteit;	and do not proceed too deeply, so as not to cut the tissue that holds the base, and ensure that evacuation occurs willingly;
puis le cure, si com nos avons dit;	then treat it as we have said;
par aventure si sera sanez, ou tu esloigne celle coverture et la munde puis qu’elle est copee delez lou fondement, ou par tente ou par autre estrument apointé;	perhaps it will heal, or you remove that covering and clean it after cutting near the base, whether by tent or other appropriate instrument;
puis mondefie cele char fautree qui est en la plaie, tant com tu pues;	Then cleanse the damaged flesh that is in the wound as much as you can.
puis estudie a restorer la plaie, et a demorer la fistule en la partie defuers le fondement:	Then proceed to restore the wound and to prevent a fistula from forming outside the rectum:
si iert plus legiere chose au malaide.	it will be easier for the patient.
Et aucune fois sont fistules selonc ceste maniere:	And sometimes fistulas occur in this manner:
et est quant tu boutes la tente en la fistule, et elle est ou costeit dou fondement delez lou cuir desus, si pren une tente percie au chief selonc ceste forme:	and it is when you insert the probe into the fistula, and it is on the side near the rectum under the skin, then take a probe with a point shaped like this:
Et i boute I fil tort en II, et boute la tente a tout le fil en la fistule tant qu’il soit au chief.	And insert the thread in a curve from I to II, and insert the probe along the entire length of the thread into the fistula until it reaches the end.
S’elle est persans en la marge dou fondement dedens, adonc estrai lou fil de celui pertus, ensi que tu boutes ton doi ou fondement;	If it is perforated on the margin of the rectum inside, then extract the thread from that passage, so you insert your finger into the rectum;
et trai le chief dou fil, et assemble les II chiés ensamble, et estraint l’un a l’autre, et le laisse I jor ou II;	and pull the head of the thread, and bring the two shoulders together, and hold them to each other, and leave it for one day or two;
et le restraint aucune fois, tant que li filz cope ces chars que sont entre dous, et chiecent;	and restrain it several times until the thread cuts through the tissues between them, and they fall;
puis cure la plaie tant qu’elle soit soudee et sanee.	then treat the wound until it is sealed and healed.
Se li fistule ne perce, si la fai percier en toutes les manieres que tu pues, s’ele n’est trop em parfont.	If the fistula does not open, pierce it in all ways that you can, if it is not too deep.
Car il ne covient mie faire por le lacement coper si em parfont, et puis le cure, si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez.	For it is not appropriate to make an incision too deep for the displacement, and then treat it as we have said, until it is healed.
Li forme dou spatumile espinous dont on fent la fistule si est mout agus d’une, part et trenchans;	The form of the spinous process where one makes the fistula is very sharp on one side and cutting;
et d’autre part non, por ceu c’on ne cope mie ceu c’on ne doit mie copeir, si com tu vois ci:	and on the other side not so, for that one does not cut what should not be cut, as you see here:
des emorroydes	for hemorrhoids
Emorrydes sont selonc II manieres:	Emorrhoids occur in two manners:
ou elles sont dedens le fondement, ausi com grain de resin, et s’en i a petites et grans, et en cort adés sanc, et s’en i a une ou plusors, et sont defuer le fondement et au chief dou fondement;	where they are within the fundament, like grains of sand, and there are small and large ones, and in the skin there is blood, and there may be one or more, and they are near the fundament and at the head of the fundament;
mais celles qui sont defuer si ont poc de moistor, et encort adés ou un poc d’aigue citrine ou un poc de sanc, et ont la color dou cors;	but those that are near have little moisture, and often there is a bit of clear water or a bit of blood, and they have the color of the flesh;
et li cure de ces qui les ont dedens le fondement, si est que tu comandes au malaide qu’il s’espreigne por aleir en chambres, tant que li fondemens li isse fuer, et c’aperent li filz;	and the treatment for those who have them within the fundament is that you instruct the patient to abstain from going out of doors until the fundament feels better and the children are aware;
si te haste, et le pent as tenailles, ou tu le tien a ton ungle, puis le cope en ses racines;	hurry and grasp it with tweezers, where you hold it with your nail, then cut it at its root;
et se li uncine ne les pueent tenir por ses moistors, si les prent a I drapeil, ou a couton, ou d’une piece de chamelot;	and if the hooks cannot hold them due to moisture, they take them with a sponge, or cotton, or a piece of cloth;
et les estrai a tes dois, puis les cope, et poudre desus aucunes chaudes poudres que soient en leu de cautere;	and extract them with your hands, then cut them, and apply some hot powder used for cauterization on top;
ou tu les cauterize si com il est dit ou chapistre de cautere, pues les cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez;	and you cauterize them as is said in the chapter on cauterization, then treat them with other methods until they are healed;
et se li fondemens ne puet issir, si clisterize le malaide de clistere mordant et aspre por laver ceu qui est ou fondement, si qu’il puist issir apertement;	and if the stool cannot be expelled, give the patient a harsh and abrasive enema to cleanse what is in the rectum so that it can pass freely;
cant li malaides se preint, et se li fil sont fuer dou fondement, si est li cure legiere;	when the patient is constipated, and if the stool is hard in the rectum, then the treatment is light;
et est que tu les preignes a ton ungle ou as tenailles, et les cope, puis les cure si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez, et qu’il redoute l’incision par fer.	And it is that you grasp them with your nail or with pincers, and cut them, then treat them as we have said, until they are healed, and that he fears the incision by iron.
Si covient que tu amenistre la costure selonc ceste maniere:	It is necessary that you manage the suturing according to this manner:
pren I fil tort, et le boute en une aguille, et puis trai le fil au desus et fai percier l’aguille d’autre part, et torne les II chiez dou fil desoz l’aguille, et si soit dou large;	take the thread and tie it to a needle, then pull the thread from above and make the needle pierce from the other side, and twist the two ends of the thread under the needle, and let it be loose;
et estraint le fil forment, puis noe le fil, et estrai l’aguille, et fai ensi de toz les autres, et en laisse I por corre la superfluiteit dou sanc;	and tightly pull the thread, then tie the thread, and remove the needle, and do this for all of them, and leave one to allow the excess blood to flow out;
puis met sus le fondement I drapeil moilliet en oile roset ou en cerote, et met sus le fondement, et comande au malaide k’il repose;	Then place a moist cloth soaked in rose oil or wax over the foundation, and instruct the patient to rest;
et puis le laisse tant qu’il chiecent, et quant il seront cheut, si les cure d’oignement et d’autre cure, tant qu’il soit sanez.	and then leave them until they dry, and when they are dry, treat them with ointment and other treatments until they are healed.
dou sechement dou fiens ou fondement	from the dryness of the feces or foundation
Maintes fois avient sechement de fiens en l’intestine, et par constrignement de nature, et quant li maladie est vielle et medicine n’i vaut.	Often there is dryness of feces in the intestine, and by constraint of nature, and when the illness is old and medicine is of no use.
Si covient que tu reses a la point d’un spatumile ou a ton ungle l’escorce desus, qui ne le laisse a moistir;	It is necessary that you cut with the tip of a scalpel or your nail through the skin above it, without allowing it to become moist.
puis le cure tant qu’il soit sodez si com il covient;	then treat it until it is healed as necessary;
et s’il ne puet soder, si rencomence la rasure plus fort que devant, tant qu’il saine mout, et soit escorchiez;	and if it does not heal, then restart the shaving more vigorously than before until it heals greatly, and even if it becomes irritated;
puis le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	then treat him until he is well.
dou fremit	with trembling
Formice est une petite apparance fautree antor le cors, et va mout em parfont;	The formice is a small striped appearance on the body, and it moves very quickly;
et aucune fois la trueve li frois, et le sent on ausi comme mort de fremit, et vient en tout le cors, et plus as mains que autre part.	and sometimes it is found in the cold, and one feels it like being chilled to death, and it spreads throughout the body, and more so in the hands than anywhere else.
Et li cure si est que tu pren une cainne d’une penne d’oie, ou une penne de vultul fort, et met celle caine sus le fremit, tant que li cercles porpreigne le fremit tot entor;	And the treatment is that you take a quill from a goose feather or a strong eagle feather, and place the quill on the chill, until the red circle surrounds the chill all around;
puis torne ta main a tout la cainne tant que tu copes tout entor le fremit, et le met em parfont, et esraiche le fremit de ses racines.	then move your hand around the quill until you cover all around the chill, and place it quickly, and uproot the chill from its roots.
Et se tu vues, si fai ceu d’une caine d’arain ou de fer selonc ceste forme, et soit subtilz desoz et traians desus:	And if you wish, do this with a thread of linen or iron according to this form, and let it be fine underneath and drawn over:
ne mie perciet, por mues tenir au doi, et mues presser.	do not pierce, to keep the hair, and press the hairs.
Et se tu vues, si cauterize lou fremit, si com il est devant ou chapistre de cautere.	And if you wish, cauterize the tremor as it is described before in the chapter on cauterization.
de la forme dou clistere	of the form of the enema
Aucune fois fait on clistere d’argent ou d’archaut, ou d’arain fondut ou mailliet;	Sometimes a cleansing enema is made of silver or sorrel, or molten silk or barley;
et aucune fois fait on de ces estrumens petis et grans, selonc ces a cui il sont amenistrez.	and sometimes these instruments are made small and large, according to the needs of those to whom they are administered.
Cil donques c’on amenistre en la cure des enfans et qui sont foible et dolorous, sont petis.	Those who treat children and those who are weak and in pain use small instruments.
Li forme dou clistere petit et grant si est desus large, ou li ventres est liiez selonc ceste maniere:	The form of the small and large purge is as follows, and the belly is bound in this manner:
et i ait une desevrance ou li ventres soit liiez, si com tu vois, et li chiez soit dedens perciez;	and there should be a space where the abdomen is bound as you see, and the intestines inside are pierced;
et ait a l’un des costez II pertus, et en l’autre I;	and there should be two holes on one side and one on the other;
et soit li ventres ou om met les medicines d’une vessie de beste ou de parchemin, et soit perciez tout entor de menus pertus, et ait entre chescun pertus I doit d’espaice, puis boute en ces pertus I fil fort de fil crut tort en X ou enqui entor, et assemble le ventre si com est une chievre;	And let the container in which medicines are placed be made from a beast’s bladder or parchment, and let it be pierced all around with small holes, and have one digit of space between each hole, then insert into these holes strong rawhide threads twisted ten times around, and assemble the container as if it were a drum.
et quant li medicine est dedens, si la lie a l’estrument devant d’un fil fort, puis clisterize;	And when the medicine is inside, tie it to the instrument with a strong thread, then administer it as an enema;
et c’est li forme dou cercle:	and this is the form of the circle:
Et soit li medicine ne trop chaude ne trop froide, et oint le chief dou clistere d’oile ou d’aubun d’uef, ou de semblant chose, puis le boute ens legierement;	And let the medicine not be too hot nor too cold, and anoint the tip of the enema with oil or beaten egg white, or something similar, then insert it gently;
puis l’espreigne li ministres a ses II mains ensamble, tant qu’il soit toz vuis, puis estrai lou clistere, et lieve li malaides ses jambes a la paroit, et se li medicine vuet issir, si la teigne tant com il puet;	Then the minister presses the patient with both hands together until it is fully inserted, then removes the enema, and lifts the patient's legs to the wall, and if the medicine wishes to come out, let it stay as long as possible;
et s’il dort une nuit atot, si est plus grans aide.	and if he sleeps one full night, then the help is greater.
Et se tu le clisterizes em maladie de decorrement de ventre, et li medicine se haste d’issir, si le rencomence tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if you administer an enema for a disease of intestinal discharge, and the medicine quickly exits, then repeat it until he is well.
Et se li emorroide sont ou fondement, ou aposteme, si soit li clistere ausi subtilz com por I enfant;	And if the hemorrhoids are at the fundament or abscessed, then the enema should be as fine as for a child;
et c’est li forme dou clistere subtil sus coi li cuir soit estraint:	and this is the form of the fine enema in which the leather is tied:
des plaies	of wounds
Nos avons jai dit en la division la cure des plaies;	We have already said in the section about the treatment of wounds;
or vos dirons les cures de mains et de medicine, selonc l’acomplissement.	We will tell you about the remedies of hands and medicine, according to the fulfillment.
Je dis que les plaies sont diverses selonc ceu qu’elles sont faites, et selonc les leus ou les plaies sont faites, et de coi elles sont faites.	I say that wounds vary according to how they are made, and according to the places where the wounds are made, and from what they are made.
Les choses par coi plaies sont faites sont par gitement de piere, et taille d’espee et de couteil, ou de lance ou de fust ou de siette, ou de semblans choses;	The things by which wounds are made are from falling stones, and the cutting of swords and knives, or spears or staffs or arrows, or similar things;
ou que sont faites selonc les leus dou cors, si com plaie que chiet sus le col, ou sus le chief, ou le peis, ou le ventre, ou le foie, et semblans membres;	or they are made according to the places on the body, such as a wound that falls on the neck, or on the head, or on the feet, or on the belly, or on the liver, and similar members;
et je vos dirai la cure de chescune plaie, et encomencerai as plaies dou chief simples, car li remenbrance venra en son chapistre.	and I will tell you the remedy for each wound, and I will begin with simple head wounds, because the memory will come in its chapter.
